paribhāṣāvṛtteḥ 
prathamādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ 
śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ 
sphuradabhinavarāgā bhāskarābhā pragalbhā prasabhaśamitadoṣā sphītasallokacakrā 
vihitahitavicārā jāḍyajātopaśāntyai prabhavatu paribhāṣāvṛttirāsevitaiṣā   
vyākhyānato viśeṣapratipattirna hi sandehādalakṣaṇam   
vyākhyānādācāryapāramparyopadeśātsandehe'pi viśeṣāvagamo bhavati na tu lakṣaṇābhāva iti 
tena ṣaṣṭho sthāneyogenetyasya pratyākhyāne ṣaṣṭhonirdeśeṣvanekasabandhasabhave'pi sthāneyogaiva bhavati 
tadukta vyākhyānato viśeṣapratipattirna hi sandehādalakṣaṇamiti sthāneyogeti vyākhyāsyāmaiti 
tathā catvāryaṇagrahaṇāni pūrveṇa ṇakāreṇa 
aṇaditsarvarṇasya cāpratyaya ityeka pareṇa 
iṇgrahaṇāni tu pareṇaiveti 
atra yuktayo'pi yathāsabhavamabhidhīyante 
tatra ke'ṇaḥ dralope pūrvasya dīrgho'ṇa ityatrāṇagrahaṇasāmarthādavasīyate pūveṇeti 
yadi pareṇa syāt 
acāmeva hrasvadīrghābhyā bhāvyam 
etaccācaśca iti paribhāṣayaiva siddha tatkimaṇagrahaṇeneti 
saiṣā yuktiḥ śakyate vyabhicārayitum 
 acaścetyeva siddhayo hrasvadīrghayoryadaṇgrahaṇa karoti tasyaitatprayojanamanaco'pyaṇo dīrghahrasvau yathā syātām agīṣkaḥ adhūṣkaḥ śvaliṅkaḥ  
madhuliṅkaḥ vaḍhā varḍhumiti  
eva ca laṇityatra yannyāsakṛtokta ke pare halāmaṇāmasabhavādityādi
tathā dīrghaśrutyā'caśceti sanidhāpite'ca eva dīrghatvena bhavitavyamityādi taccintyam 
atra ke ciccintayanti 
agīṣka ityādau visarjanīyādiṣu kṛteṣu hakāro'ṇ rephaśca nāsti 
na cāstyasiddhatvam 
na mune iti yogavibhāgena niṣiddhatvāt 
anabhidhāna tu na vaktavyam 
roḥ supi ityatrāgīṣkādīnā nyāse vyākhyātatvāt 
dīrghavidhau ca varḍhā varḍhumityādau pareṇa ṇakāreṇa pratyāhāragrahaṇādanaco'pi rephasya yaddīrghatvamuktam 
tanna 
yadyetatprayojana syāt tadā hayavarataṣṭakāreṇa pratyāhāra kuryāt 
dralope pūrvasya dīrgho'ṭa iti 
 atha vā'stu varḍhā varḍhumityādau dīrgha eva ṝkāraḥ tathāpi kṛte tasminnādguṇa ityakāraṛkārayorguṇenākāre raparatve ca kṛte tadeva rūpa varḍhā  
varḍhumiti  
ato'caśca iti siddhi yadaṇgrahaṇa tatpūrveṇa ṇakāreṇa pratyāhārārtham 
na ca pareṇa ṇakāreṇa pratyāhāragrahaṇe rephasya dīrghavaiyarthyātpunarādguṇabādhaḥ kalpanīyaḥ 
eva hi sāmarthyadvaya syāt 
savarṇavidhau pareṇa ṇakāreṇa pratyāhāragrahaṇe urṛt iti taparakaraṇa jñāpakam 
 yadi tatrāpi pūrveṇa syāt eva ca sūtropāttasya mātrikasya sthāne sūtropātte ṛkāre vidhīyamāne sāvarṇyābhāvād dvimātrikasya prāptireva nāstīti  
taparakaraṇamanarthaka syāt  
 yacca laṇityatra nyāsakṛtokta dīrghasyāpi sthānino yathāśrutena hrasvenaiva bhavitavyamiti taparakaraṇamanarthaka syād vyāvarttyābhāvāditi 
tatra dvimātrikasya sthānitva yaduktam 
tadasaṅgatam 
ādeśavatsthānino'pi dvimātrasyābhāvāt 
atha jātau dvimātrasya sthānitvamiti cenna 
evamādeśe'pi dvimātratvaprasaṅgaḥ 
atha sthānina prati jātirādeśa prati vyaktiretacca na hṛdayagrāhi 
eva tarhi ṛkāraṝkārayoḥ samāhāradvandvaikatvena napusakahrasvatvena ca urṛditi nirddeśe dīrghasyāpi sthānitvam 
numabhāvastvāgamaśāsanasyānityatvāt 
idamatha yuktam 
vyaktireke'ṇapratyāhāre ṝkārasyānantarbhāvāt sāvarṇyen ṛkāreṇa ṝkārasyāgrahaṇāddṛkārasyāctva nāsti 
ato'co hrasvatva vidhīyamānamṝkārasya katha syāt 
ucyate 
hrasvo napusake prātipadikasya ityanenāco hrasvatva vidhīyate 
 acpratyāhāre ca ṛkāro'sti tatra ṛkāreṇa ṛtvajāterāśrayaṇād dvimātrikasyāpi ṝkārasya hrasvatvena bhāvyameveti yukta dīrghasyāpi sthānina ityādi 
iya ca paribhāṣā laṇityatra bhāṣyakāreṇa jñāpitā 
taduktam 
 ki punaraya varṇotsattāvibra ṇakārassandehaheturanubaddho'pi punaranubadhyate yasmādanenāṇgrahaṇeyviṇgrahaṇeṣu ca sadehaḥ ki pūrveṇa pareṇa  
veti eva tarhi jñāpayatyācāryo bhavatyeṣā paribhāṣā vyākhyānata ityādi  
 atha katha viśeṣapratipattirityatra ṣaṣṭhīsamāsaḥ 
yāvatā karmaṇi ca ityanena pratiṣedhena bhāvyam 
na ca kṛdyogalakṣaṇā ṣaṣṭhī samasyata ityanena samāsaḥ śakyate karttum 
tadviṣaye eva karmaṇi cetyasyārambhāt 
ucyate 
karmaṇi cetyanenobhayaprāptau karmaṇi ityanena niyamena yā ṣaṣṭhī tasyā eva samāsapratiṣedho vijñāyate 
atra cārthe karttari ca iti sūtra pramāṇam 
anyathā apā sraṣṭā odanasya bhojaka ityādau karmaṇi cetyanenaiva pratiṣedhasya siddhatvāt karttari cetyanarthaka syāt 
na ca praiṣyasya hārayitā praiṣyasya kārayitā ityatra hṛkroranyatarasyām iti karttari ṣaṣṭhīsamāsapratiṣedhārthamidamiti 
tṛjakābhyā karttari ityanenaiva tatsiddhiḥ 
yattu tṛjakābhyā karttarītyatra vṛttāvukta tṛjgrahaṇamuttarārthamiti tatkarttari ceti sūtre sthite iti 
aṇyantāpekṣayoktamuttarārthamityeke 
 ubhayaprāptāviti niyamena ca ṣaṣṭhī ṣaṣṭhī hetuprayoge ityataḥ prayogagrahaṇānuvṛtteryatra sāmarthyaprāpta kartṛkarmaṇorubhayorupādāna tatraiva  
yathā syāt  
yathā āścaryo gavā doho'gopālakeneti 
 tathā hyatrāścarya pratipādya tacca durdohānā gavā karmaṇāmasuśikṣitasyāgopālakasya ca karttuḥ sāmarthyaprāpte upādāne ṣaṣṭhī bhavati nānyathā 
viśeṣapratipattirityatra tu śiṣyādeḥ karturakicitkaratvānna sāmarthyaprāpta kartturupādānam 
eva ca sati antarddhau yenādarśanamicchati ityatra yeneti tṛtīyā na yuktā kartṛkarmaṇoḥ kṛti iti karttari ṣaṣṭhīvidhānāt 
ucyate 
nirddeśādeva tṛtīyetyadoṣaḥ 
anyastvācaṣṭe 
gamyamāne'pi karmaṇi ubhayaprāptāviti niyamo bhavatyeva 
 tathā cāntarddhau yenādarśanamicchatītyatra nyāsakṛtā ubhayaprāptau karmaṇi ityatra rakṣitena ca gamyamāne'pi karmaṇi niyamātṣaṣṭhyabhāvena  
antarddhau yeneti nirddeśasiddhiruktā  
ki tvevamaiuṇityatra tasya grahaṇa bhavatyekeneti tatra tasyeti karttari ṣaṣṭhīti nyāse yadukta tanna śobhanam 
tathā hyatrāpi gamyamāne grāhye karmaṇi ubhayaprāptāviti niyamātṣaṣṭyā na bhavitavyam 
etacca śabdānuśāsane nyāsakṛtā vyākhyātam 
yattu tatra svamatimahimaprāgalbhyādanunyāsakāro vyājahāra 
yatra sāmarthyaprāptamubhayorupādāna sa ubhayaprāptau karmaṇītyasya viṣayaḥ 
anyathā kartṛkarmaṇoḥ kṛtītyasya vidherubhayaprāptāvityādeśca viṣayavibhāgo na syāt 
na cākartṛka karmāstīti nyāyāditi 
tadayuktam 
purā bhettā devadatta ityādau abhihite kartari niyamāprasaṅgāt 
atrocyate 
 ṣaṣthī hetuprayoge ityato'nuvarttamānamapi prayogagrahaṇamanaṅgīkṛtya yathā yuṣmābhirgamyamāne karmaṇi ubhayaprāptāviti niyama ucyate tathā'smābhirapyanabhihitādhikāramanaṅgīkṛtya  
vibhāgābhāva uktaḥ  
etaccāyuktam 
akākārayīḥ pratiṣedhoḥ vaktavya ityanyena yatra niyamo bādhyate tatra vidheḥ kṛtārthatvāt 
cikīrṣāraverālokānāmiti 
tathā kāryaḥ kaṭo devadattasyetyatrābhihite karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhīprasaṅgācca 
ucyate 
kartṛkarmaṇoḥ kṛtītyasya vidherubhayaprāptāvityādeśca vidheriti naite samānādhikaraṇe ṣaṣṭyau ki tarhi vaiyadhikaraṇye 
tadayamarthaḥ kartṛkaraṇoḥ kṛtītyasya sabandhī yo vidhiḥ karttari ca iti
tathobhayaprāptau karmaṇītyasya yo vidhiḥ karmaṇi ca iti etayorviṣayavibhāgo na syādityayamabhiprāyaḥ 
 yadi gamyamāne'pi karttari ubhayaprāptāviti karmaṇi niyamaḥ syāt tadā idhmavraścana ityādāvapi karaṇe lyuṭi karmaṇi ceti niṣedhaḥ syāt kartṛlyuṭyapi  
idhmapravraścano devadatta ityatrāpi ātmanā devadattenetyasya karturgamyamānatvādubhayaprāptiravyāhataiva  
eva ca karmaṇi yā kā citṣaṣṭhī tasyā eva sarvasyāḥ karmaṇi cetyanena samāsapratiṣedhe siddhe kartari cetyanārambhaṇīya syāt 
ārabdha cāto yuktamukta viṣayavibhāgo na syāditi 
etacca na 
ātmanetyasya kartturgasyamānatve pramāṇābhāvāt 
eva tarhi purāmbhettā devadatta ityādau yathā kartturabhihitatvānniyamo na bhavati tathā śabdānuśāsanamityatrāpi karturaprayogāt 
tatra yathā karttṛṣaṣṭhīprāptyā vināpi gamyamāne karttari niyama ucyate tathābihite'pi karttari niyamamuttkā niyamamuktā
viṣayavibhāga uktaḥ 
eva ca vidhiniyamavākyayoreva viṣayavibhāgābhāvaḥ 
etaccākākārayoḥ prayoge vidheḥ kṛtārthatvānāśrayaṇenocyate   
na hi kāryī nimittatvenāśīyate   
yatkāryabhāk tatkarya prati nimitta na bhavatītyarthaḥ 
tenādhyetā adhyāpakaḥ śayitā śāyaka ityatra iṅśīṅorṅitvāt kṅiti ca iti guṇavṛddhipratiṣedho na bhavati 
tathā'ririṣatītyatra dvirvacane'ci iti sthānivadbhāvo na bhavati 
yadi syāt iso dvirvacane kṛte'rīṣatīti syāt 
jñāpaka cātra dīdhīvevīṭām ityatra ṅitorapi dīdhīṅvevīṅorguṇavṛddhipratiṣedhārthamupādānam 
na ca kṅiti cetyanena iglakṣaṇāyā eva vṛddheḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate
ato'jlakṣaṇāyā api vṛddheḥ pratiṣedhārtha dīdhīvevyorubhayorupādāna syāditi vācyam 
indhibhavatibhyā ca ityatra bhavatigrahaṇenājlakṣaṇāyā api vṛddheḥ pratiṣedho bhavatītyasyārthasya jñāpitatvāt 
nanu ca bhāṣye vuko nityatvādindheścchāndasatvādindhibhavativyā ceti sūtra pratyākhyāta tathā dīdhīvevīṭāmityapi 
yadāha dīdhīvevyorgrahaṇamanarthaka anayośchāndasatvāt 
ādīdhet ādīdhayurityatra guṇadarśanācca 
iṭaścāpi grahaṇamanarthaka neḍvaśi kṛti ityata iḍgrahaṇānuvṛttau ārddhadhātukasyeḍvalādeḥ ityatra yadiḍgahaṇa tadiṭo vikārābhāvārtham 
tato laghūpadhaguṇābhāvāt siddha kaṇitā śvo raṇitā śva iti 
na caiva pipaṭhīrapāṭhīdityādāvapi dīrghatva na syāditi vaktavyam 
yataḥ samānajātīyatayāṅgakāryameva vyāvarttyate 
grahītetyatra tu graho'liṭi ityādisūtrārambhād dīrghatvam 
tarhi pipaṭhīṣi brāhmaṇakulānītyatra sāntamahataḥ sayogasya iti dīrghatva na syāditi cenna 
numevātra nāsti numi karttavye'llopasya sthānivattvenājhalantatvāt 
na ca kvau lupte na sthānivadityasti 
kvau vidha prati na sthānivaditīda vārttikamiti kaiyaṭena vyākhyātam 
eva ca kvau nātra num api tu sarvanāmasthāne 
vāmanastu kvau lupta ityeva manyate 
tathā ca maparyantasya ityatra tena parigrahaṇa varjanīyārthamityuktam 
tena yatraiva varjanīyamasti tatraivādeśa iti 
tena yuṣmadasmadorṇici ṭilopaḥ 
yuṣmayateḥ kvip tataḥ svādayaḥ atra varjanīyābhāvādādeśā na bhavanti 
na cāsti ṇilopasya sthānivattvam 
kvau lupte na sthānivaditi vacanāt 
tadeva sthitametat 
bhāṣyamate na hi kāryītyasyā liṅga nāsti 
sthaṇḍilācchayitari ityatra śayitarīti nirddeśo'syā liṅga kuṭādiṣu kuṅ śabde ityasya pāṭho vā 
anye tu vyācakṣate 
iglakṣaṇavṛddhipratiṣedhastāvat kṅitpratyayanimittaka eva sabhavati na tu kṅiddhātunimittakaḥ 
 ato mṛṣṭaḥ mṛṣṭavān nyanuvīt nyaghuvīt ityādau kṅinnimittakaḥ pratyaya eva parato vṛddhipratiṣedhastatsāhacaryād guṇapratiṣedho'pi bhūyate  
bobhūyate ityādau kaṅinnimittakaḥ pratyaya eva kartavyaḥ  
ata evādhyetā śayitetyatra kṅiddhātunimittakena pratiṣedhena na bhavitavyam 
 aririṣātītyatrāpi dvirvacaneci ityajādeśa prati nimittabhāvo'kāryitvenaiva niyataḥ tadevamajādeśasabandhe'cītyasyākāryitva tatsāhacaryād  
dvirvacanavidhāne'pi yadyakāryitvamevācītyasya tadā sthānivattva yathā cakruturiti  
aririṣatītyatra tu dvitīyasyakāco dvirvacanādikārasya dvirvacanabhāktamiti dvirvacanavidhāne'cītyasya kāryitva na punarakāryitvamiti 
tasmātparibhāṣā prayojanābhāvānna svīkarttavyā 
yukta caitat 
anyathā asyā satyā prorṇunaviṣatītyatra guṇāvādeśayoḥ kṛtayordvicane'cīti sthānivattva na syāt 
sannantasya kāryitvāt 
 tathā dvirvacane'cītyatrācīti kimityuktā heghrīyate dedhmīyate iti yatpratyudāhṛta tannopapadyate dvyaṅgavaikalyāt yathaiva yaṅ ajādirna bhavati  
tathā dvirvacananimittamapīti  
tatra tahīrda vaktavyam 
kāryamanubhavanneva kāryo nimittatvena nāśīyate
jeghrīyata ityatra kāryamananubhavan nimittatvenāśrīyate 
anyanstu nāśrita eva 
tathā hi 
aririṣatītyatra sthānivattvena iso dvirvacanaprasaṅgādajādereva sanaḥ kāryitva nimittatva ca 
prorṇunaviṣatītyatra tu ajādeḥ sano nimittatva kāryitva ca dhātornuśabdasyaiva tasyaiva dvirvacanavidhānāt 
ato'tra sanaḥ sākṣāt kāryitva nāstīti yuktameva nimittatvenāśrayaṇamiti 
evamapi śādhītyatra śāhau ityasya śādeśasya dhibhāva prati samānāśraye hāvasiddhatvanna syāditi 
dhibhāvasya sthānino hiśabdasyānimittatvena samānanimittatvābhāvāt 
tatra vaktavya prāyikametat 
lakṣyavaśāt kva cidāśrīyate   
itaretarāśrayāṇyapi kāryāṇi śāstre prakalpante   
itaretarāśrayāṇi kāryāṇi viroddhānna pravarttanta iti nyāyaḥ yaduktamitaretarāśrayatvādaprasiddhiriti 
tadapavādo'yamārabhyate 
apiśabdaḥ kva cidarthe 
tadayamarthaḥ 
kva ciditaretarāśrayāṇi pravarttanta iti 
yathā vanasihayoḥ parasparāśrayāpi rakṣā pravarttate 
tathā śāstre gārgīya ityādau vṛddhisajñayā bhāvitasyāpi vṛddhisajñā prakliptiḥ 
anyathā śālārairauprabhṛtiṣu sāvakāśā vṛddhisajñā itaretarāśrayatvānna syāt 
jñāpaka cātra igyaṇaḥ saprasāraṇam ityatra saprasāraṇena yaṇaḥ sthāne iko bhāvyante 
yaṇsthānikānā cekā saprasāraṇasajñeti itaretarāśrayatvam 
kathametadanyathā prakalpate 
yadītaretarāśrayatva kva cinna syāditi 
bhāgavṛttikārastvāha 
nityaśabdānāmanvākhyānamātramidamiti tato netaretarāśrayadoṣaḥ 
yadukta sarvāṇītaretarāśrayāṇi bhāṣye parihṛtāni siddha tu nityaśabdatvāditīti 
athaitatsyāt yaṇaḥ sthāne igvidhīyate sthānyādeśabhāvaśca pauruṣeyaḥ tatkṛto nityatvamiti 
naiṣa doṣāḥ 
 loke hi iṣṭa yaṣṭetyādayo nityāḥ tatra yajerarthe ijirviśiṣṭaviṣaye sādhurityetāvati puruṣāśrayatva svabhāvata eva yajeḥ sthāne ijisiddhiḥ 
āgamāstaṅguṇībhūtāstadgrahaṇena gṛhyante   
 ādyantau ṭākitau ityatrādyantaśabdayoravayavavacanatvāt ṭitkitorāgamayorādyantāvayavatvamatidiṣṭa midaco'ntyātpara ityatrāpi antagrahaṇanuvṛttyā  
mito'pyantāvayavatvam  
avayavāścāvayavigrahaṇena gṛhyante ityuktamataḥ siddheya paribhāṣā āgamāstadguṇībhūtā iti 
sukhapratipattyartha ca jñāpakamapi kecidāhaḥ 
ṇeraniṭi ityatrāniṭīti pratiṣedhaḥ 
yadyāgamigrahaṇenāgamo na gṛhyeta tadā kārayitavyamityādau itā vyavahitatvādeva ṇilopo na prāpnotīti kimaniṭītyaneneti jñāpakam 
tena sarveṣāmityatra suṭaḥ subgrahaṇena grahaṇājjhalādau supi etva siddhyati 
nanu asyā satyā cicchidatuḥ cicchiduḥ ityādau halādiḥ śeṣeṇa tuko nivṛttiḥ prāpnoti 
ucyate 
halādiḥ śeṣa ityatrāṭaturāṭurittyādisiddhyartha jātipakṣa āśritaḥ 
tatracaikameveda lakṣaṇa sakṛdeva papāṭhetyādau anāderhalo nivṛtti karoti 
tadeva cicchidaturityādau halādiḥ śeṣānantara yastuk tasya nivṛttirna prāpnoti 
lakṣaṇābhāvāt 
avaśya caitat 
anyathā'jāderdvitīyasyetyatra bhāṣyakāreṇa ca maitreyeṇa ca yadudāhṛtam 
oṇeruvoṇiṣatīti syāditi sāvakāśameva dvitīyadvirvacanamiti 
tadasaṅgata syāt 
halādiḥ śeṣeṇa vakāralopaprasaṅgāt 
yadyeva vavṛte ityādau urattve raparatve ca kṛte rephasya lopo na syāt 
ucyate 
halādiḥ śeṣa ityatra urat ityanuvarttiṣyate tena uraditi kṛte rephasya nivṛttirbhaviṣyati 
eva tarhi uñcheraiñcicchadityatra tuki kṛte halādiḥ śeṣeṇa tasya nivṛttiḥ syādeva 
ucyate 
checa ityatra hrasvagrahaṇe'nuvarttamāne punaryaccakāreṇa tasyānuvarttana tatsāmarthyāt hrasva āgamī svīkriyate na tu hrasvāntaḥ samudāyaḥ
eva cābhyāsāvayavasyaiva bhaktastuk kriyate tatsāmarthyādihāvayavāvayavo'pi avayavigrahaṇena na gṛhyate anyatra tu gṛhyata eva 
ataeva śerata ityatrāvayavāvayavaḥ samudāyāvayavo bhavatītyuktā śīṅo ruṭ ityatra śīṅaḥ sārvadhātuke guṇa uktaḥ 
eva tu śobhanacchāya ityatra tukā uttarapadasya vyavadhānātpuvadbhāvo na syāditi dūṣaṇam 
ucyate 
hrasva pratīda jñāpaka padāntādvā ityatra tu nāsti 
dadhi chādayatītyatra svaravidhau vyañjanamavidyamānavaditi tiṅñatiṅa iti nighātaḥ śakyate karttum 
asyā satyā prātipadikāntanum vibhaktiṣu ca ityatra numgrahaṇasya prayojana na dṛśyate 
bhartṛhariṇā tūktam yaḥ prātipadikānto nakāro na bhavati tadartha numgrahaṇa prāhiṇvaditi atra hi hiverlaṅi numo ṇatvamiti 
tatra ca pūvapadādhikāraḥ samāse ca pūvottarapadavyavahāraḥ tatkathamiha ṇatvamiti na vyaktīkṛtamiti bhāgavṛttikṛtoktam 
yadyeva prahiṇvannityetadartha tarhi numgrahaṇa syāt 
ucyate 
 alpāctaramityanena prātipadikānta ityādau numaḥ pūrvanipāte karttavye yatprātipadikavibhaktimadhyastha numgrahaṇa karoti tadeva bodhayati  
yo'nayoreva madhyastho numnakārastasya ṇatva bhavatīti  
 aṭkughāṅnumvyavāsepi ityatra bhāgavṛttikṛtā pratipādita numaḥ pūvanipātalakṣaṇavyabhicāracihnāt prenvamityatra ṇatvābhāvaḥ kṣubhnādityādvā  
tena saha samānam  
nanu mitvānnumaḥ pūrvāntatve niṣkauśāmvinī kule ityatra paratvānnumi kṛte napusakahrasvatva na prāpnoti ajantatvābhāvāt 
yathā suvāk brāhmaṇakulamiti 
naiṣa doṣaḥ vibhaktyāśrayaṇād bahiraṅgo num hrasvatamantaraṅga vibhaktyanāśrayatvāt tatprathama bhaviṣyati 
taduktam 
na vā bahiraṅgalaṇatvāditi   
nirddiśyamānasyādeśa bhavanti   
ṣaṣṭhyā nirddiṣṭasya samudāyasya tadekadeśasya vā''deśā bhavanti 
tadyathā 
pādaḥ pat iti ṣaṣṭhyā nirddhiṣṭasyaiva pādaḥ sthāne padbhavati dvipadaḥ paśyeti nāṅgādhikāraparibhāṣayā tadantasya 
tathā bhavetāmityatra tasaḥ sthāne tāmādeśo bhavati na sayāsuṭaḥ 
tadekadeśasya yathā 
udaḥ sthāstambhoḥ pūrvasya iti tiṣṭhaterādideśasya pūrvasavarṇo vidhīyamāna udasthādityatrāṭo na bhavati 
tathā ṣyaṅaḥ samprasāraṇam iti ṣyaṅekadeśasya samprasāraṇe vārāhīputra ityatrānayā rephavakārayoḥ samprasāraṇābhāvo vyākhyātaḥ 
iya paribhāṣā ṣaṣṭhī sthāne yogā ityasyārthe paṭhyate 
tathā hi tatra bhāṣyam 
yadyapyekaśata ṣaṣdyarthāḥ yāvantaste tāvantaḥ ṣaṣṭhyāmuccāritāyā sarve prāpnuvanti arthā ye punaḥ samīpāntaravikārādyāḥ
śabdasya tu ko'nyo bhavitumarhati anyadataḥ sthānāt 
nanu śabdasyāpyanantarādayaḥ sambandhāḥ sambhavanti 
astebhūrbhavatīti sandehaḥ ki sthāne samīpe vā tatra samīpe na bhaviṣyati dvayorekārthayorekatra prayogānupapatteḥ 
ki ca sandehamātramatat 
sarvasandeṣvidamupatiṣṭhate bhavati hi vyākhyānato viśeṣapratipattirna hi sandehādalakṣaṇamiti sthāne iti vyākhyāsyāmaḥ 
na tarhīdānīmaya yogo vaktavyaḥ 
vaktavyaḥ 
ki prayojana ṣaṣṭhyanta sthāne yathā prasajyeta 
yataḥ ṣaṣṭhī uccāritā tadeva kāryopayogi yathā syāt 
tadetenaitatpratipādita nirddiśyamānasyādeśā bhavantīti 
 asyā satyā śīṅo ruṭ ityatra yannyāsakṛtokta yadi ruḍāgamo jhakārasyaiva syāt tadā'dādeśo jhakārasya na syāt tasyaiva ruṭaḥ syāt ādeḥ parasyeti  
vacanāt  
tathā maparyantasya ityatra yadudāhṛta yuvakāmiti sākackasya syāditi 
etadanapekṣya tatsamādheyam   
nānubandhakṛtamanekāltvam   
anubandhakṛtamanekāltva nāśrīyate 
tenārvaṇastrasāvanaña iti arvantau arvanta ityatra trādeśo'ntyasyaiva bhavati na sarvasya 
ke cittu dyubhyā dyubhirityudāharanti 
tanna śobhanam 
diva ut ityanena ukārasyaiva vidhānāt 
tathā hi taparastatkālasya iti udityeṣā sajñā ukāramātrasyaiva vidhīyate 
eva ca diva udityanena ukāra eva kevalo vidhīyate na tūcchabdaḥ 
avaśya caitat 
anyathā'tobhisa aisa ityatra kā gatiḥ syāt 
na hyatrāta ādeśo vidhīyate ki tarhi atsajñayā akāraḥ sajñī nirddiśyate 
yattu sthāghvoricca ityatrokta icca kasya takārettvamiti tatpratipādakaikadeśānā pratipādyaikadeśatvamabhyupagamya 
tatmatenaiva titsvaritam ityatra tiditi pratyayagrahaṇamiti bhāṣye uktam 
taparastatkālasya ityatra tu varṇa eva sajñītyukta na punastaparaḥ samudāyaḥ 
yukta caitat 
anyathā taparastatkālasyetyatra svagrahaṇānuvṛttyā bhavadbhirityatrāpyais syāt 
iya ca paribhāṣā anubandhā avayavā ityatra pakṣe 
jñāpaka cātrānekālśitsarvasya ityatra śidgrahaṇam 
yadyanubandhenāpyanekāltva syāt tadā sarve ityādau śībhāvasyānekāltvādeva sarvādeśe jasaḥ siddhe śidgrahaṇamanarthaka syāt 
 nanu dhvasoreddhāvabhyāsalopaśca iti lopaḥ śidvaktavya iti yaḥ śidabhyupagamyate tatra sarvādeśārtha śidgrahaṇa syāt dehi dhehīti sarvasyaiva  
lopo bhavati  
ucyate 
yadetallopasya śittvamāśrita tatsāmarthyādeva sarvādeśo bhaviṣyati 
atha vā lopaḥ śidvaktavya iti nāśrayaṇīyam 
nānarthake'lontyavidhiriti survasyaiva lopo bhaviṣyati 
yattūcyate tatrānabhyāsavikāreṣviti tallakṣyasthityā na sarvatreti 
nanu yadi iya paribhāṣā'sti ṇal tarhi sarvādeśo na prāpnoti 
ucyate 
ānupūrvyāt siddhamidam 
tathā hi 
sarvādeśe sati ṇalo ṇakārasyopadeśe pratyayāditvamiti tataścuṭū itītsajñā tatastasyānubandhatvam 
tadeva sarvādeśapūrvakamanubandhatva sarvādeśatā vihantu na kṣamate sarvādeśatāyāḥ pūrvameva niṣpannatvāt   
varṇāśraye vidhau pratyayalakṣaṇa na bhavati 
tena gave hita gohita rāyaḥ kula raikulamityatra pratyayalakṣaṇenācīti avāyādeśau na bhavataḥ 
lavaṇā yavāgūrityatra lavaṇāllugiti ṭhako lukikṛte pratyayalakṣaṇena ṭhagantāṭṭiḍḍhāṇañ iti ṅībna bhavati 
ṅīpo varṇamātrāśrayatva yathā syādityevamarthamakārastatrānuvṛttaṣṭidādibhirviśeṣyate na tvakāreṇa ṭidādayaḥ 
ata eva kvarapkhyunāmiti ṣaṣṭhyā nirddeśaḥ kṛtaḥ 
aya cārthaḥ pratyayalope pratyayalakṣaṇam ityatra dvitīyena pratyayagrahaṇena sādhitaḥ 
tathāhi tatroktam 
 tallakṣaṇamiti vaktavye pratyayalakṣaṇamityatra yatpunaḥ pratyayagrahaṇa pratyayāśritameva kārya pratyayalakṣaṇena yathā syāt yathā suptiṅanga  
padam iti 
acītyetadvarṇamātrāśrita mābhūditi 
jñāpaka cātra śravaṇākārttikīcaitrībhya iti śravaṇeti ṭabanto nirddeśaḥ 
nanu yadi varṇāśraye pratyayalakṣaṇa nāsti tarhi atṛṇeḍityatra tṛṇahaim iti im na prāpnoti imāgamasya halvarṇāśrayatvāt 
ucyate 
nāya varṇāśrayo'pi tvaṅgādhikāreṇa pratyayākṣepāddhalādipratyayāśrayaḥ 
 etadukta bhavati pratyaye dvividha kārya pratyayanimittamapratyayanimitta ca tatra pratyayanimitta yattadeva pratyayalopalakṣaṇena yathā  
syāditaranmābhūdityevamartha pratyayalope pratyayalakṣaṇamityatra dvitīya pratyayagrahaṇam  
 tenaico'yavāyāva ityavādirvaṇāśrayatvātparibhāṣayā khaṇḍyate imāgamastu pratyayanimitta eva aṅgādhikāreṇa pratyayākṣepāttadbhavane ko virodhaḥ 
na caiva śriyai ida śryarthamityatrājādipratyaye iyaṅṅāśaṅkanīyaḥ 
na lumatāṅgasya iti pratiṣedhāt 
yattu śāsa idaṅhaloḥ ityatrāsyāḥ prāyikatvamuktā nyāsakāreṇātṛṇeḍityatra varṇāśraye'pīmāgamo bhavatītyuktam 
tadupāyāntaram 
nanu gohitamityādau luko vidhāna na tu lopasya tadeva pratyayalakṣaṇasya prasaṅga eva nāsti tatki paribhāsāśrayaṇena 
ucyate 
lukyapi pratyayalakṣaṇa bhavati lopasyādarśanārthatvāt 
pramāṇa cātra na lumatāṅga'syeti pratiṣedhaḥ   
kva cidekadeśo'pyanuvarttate 
svaritatvabalena kva citsūtraikadeśaḥ padaikadeśo'pyanuvarttate 
tena dāmahāyanāntācca ityatra saṅkhyāvyayāderityataḥ saṅkhyādigrahaṇamātramanuvarttate 
tathā jhonta ityatrāyannādisūtrādādigrahaṇanivṛttāvapi pratyayagrahaṇamanuvarttate 
jñāpaka cātra tasminniti nirddiṣṭe pūvasya ityata iti śabde prakṛte tasmādityuttarasya iti punaritiśabdaḥ 
yadi hi sahaiva padānāmanuvṛttiḥ syāt tadā nirddiṣṭagrahaṇavaditiśabdo'pyanuvarttiṣyate pūvasūtrāt 
tatkiminikaraṇena 
tatkurvannācāryo jñāpayati kva cidekadeśo'pyanuvarttata iti 
eva hi sati nirddiṣṭagrahaṇameva kevalamanuvarttate netikaraṇamiti 
arthadgrahaṇe nānarthakasya   
arthavadanarthakavicāre arthavata eva śabdasya grahaṇa nānarthakasya 
tena vanora ca ityanena kvanivvanipoḥ karṭṭṛrūpeṇārthena sārthakayoreva vano rephādeśo bhavati 
dhīvarī pīvarīti 
na nirarthakasya 
atiśunī atiyūnīti 
tathā inhanpūṣāryamṇām ityādau kvibantasyaivārthavato hantergrahaṇam 
tena plīhānau plīhāna ityatrāpi niyamena dīrghavyāvṛttirna bhavati 
nanu kathamatiśunītyādau vanśabdasyānarthakatvamukta yāvatā svarūpeṇārthenārthavattā'styeva 
yathā vṛddhirādaic ityatroktam 
sajñāsajñisambandhātprāgvṛddhiśabdasya svarūpeṇārthenārthavattvāt prātipadikatvam 
tathā cāhṛḥ 
yasminnuccarite śabde yadā yo'rthaḥ pratīyate 
tamāhṛrartha śabdasya nānyadarthasya lakṣaṇamiti 
yo hi svarūpaparaḥ prayujyate tasya svarūpamevārthaḥ tatparatvāttasya 
na cātiśunītyādau vanādayo varṇasamudāyāḥ svarūpaparāḥ 
atiśunyādisamudāyasapādanāya teṣāmuccāraṇāt 
ata evārthavat sūtre vana dhanamityatra nāntasyāvadheranarthakatvamuktam 
yadā tvatiśunyādau vanādayo varṇasamudāyāḥ svarūpaparā bhavanti tadā teṣā bhavatyevārthavattvamiti 
āto lopa iṭi ca ityatra tu dvayorapi nirarthakasyāgamasya sārthakasya ca pratyayasyeṭo grahaṇam 
 iṭo't ityatra viśeṣaṇārthe ṭhakārādau karttavye yadiṭaṣṭakāraḥ kṛtastasyaitatprayojanamāto lopa iṭi cetyatra sāmānyagrahaṇa yathā syāditi 
etaccāto lopa iṭi cetyatra ṭita ātmanepadānā ṭere ityatra ca bhāṣyakhyākhyāna rakṣitenoktam 
ki tvevamiṭo'dityatrāpi dvayorāgamapratyayayorgrahaṇa prāpnoti 
tatheḍvahimahiṅityatra pratyāhārtha varṇāntare karttavye ṅakārakaraṇa ṅitkāryārthamapi syāt
eva ca sasrasimaha ityatrāniditā hala ityanunāsikalopaḥ prasajyeta 
tadetatsamādheyam 
puruṣottamadevena tu dādhāghvadāp ityatra dāśṭadhāvudhātvekadeśayordādhāśabdayoranarthakayoragrahaṇamuktam 
tathā śe ityatra sūtre kāśe kuśe iti padaikadeśasyānarthakasya 
etadanyena kṣamante 
tathā hi pranidāśati pranidhāvatītyatra satyāmapi ghusajñāyā nergadādi sūtreṇa ṇatva nāsti dādhāśabdau prati nerūpasargasajñāyā abhāvāt
tathā ca bhāṣyam 
na cetau dādhau prati kriyāyoga iti 
sani mīmāghu ityādau cāṅgasya ghorgrahaṇādasakārāditvācca didāśiṣatītyādau na doṣaḥ 
kāśe kuśe śeśabdasya lākṣaṇikatvāt pragṛhyasajñāyā abhāvo nyāsakṛtaiva śe ityatra vyākhyātaḥ 
svarūpavidhiviṣayā ceya paribhāṣā 
arthavadadhātuḥ ityatrārthavadgrahaṇāt 
tena pralambata ityatrānarthakādapi praśabdādavyayādāpsupa iti subluk siddho bhavati 
anarthakasyāvyayatvamupasargatva prātipadikatva ca nipātānāmanarthakānāmarthavatkṛtāni kāryāṇi bhavantīti vacanāt 
jñāpaka cātrādhiparī anarthakau ityadhiparyoranarthakayorupasargasajñānivṛttyartha nipātasajñādhikāre karmarpravacanīyasajñāvidhānam 
ata eva nipātasya cānarthakasya prātipadikasajñā vaktavyeti bhāṣye pratyākhyātam 
yadyeva nipātatvād yadavyayatva tatsāmarthyādeva subluk siddhaḥ 
naitat 
nipātatvasya svarārthatvamātreṇopapannatvāt 
anarthakatva tu praśabdasya prakarṣārthasya prakarṇādināvagatatvāt 
 ihānarthakatvādvibhaktyabhāvo na pūrvapakṣyate prātipadikārthetyatra prātipadikagrahaṇāt tasya hyetatprayojanamanarthakādapi prātipadikamātrātprathamā  
yathā syāditi  
iya ca paribhāṣā sva rūpam ityatra bhāṣye jñāpitā 
tatra hyukta rūpagrahaṇa na karttavyam 
sva śabdasyetyucyamāne yadyapi śabdasya rūpamarthaśca sva bhavati 
tathāpi rūpameva grāhya nārthaḥ 
yataḥ śabdoccāraṇe rūpapratipattirādau tato'rthapratipattiḥ 
tathā śabdo'nukaraṇakāle'rtha jahāti na rūpam 
tadevampratyāsannabuddhitvādaheyatvena nityasambandhitvācca śabdasya rūpameva grāhya nārtho viparyayāt 
ataḥ svagrahaṇādeva rūpagrahaṇe siddhe vyākaraṇaśāstre rūpavadarthopyaṅgīkriyata iti labhyate 
atha vā vraścādi sūtre bhrājagrahaṇamasyāstitve jñāpakam 
yadi hyanarthakasyāpi grahaṇa syāttadā rājagrahaṇenaiva bhrājaikadeśasyāpi grahaṇe siddhe rājabhrājeti bhrājagrahaṇa na kuryāt 
kṛta cāto jñāpakamarthavata eva grahaṇa nānarthakasyeti   
na varṇagrahaṇeṣu   
pūrvāpavādoyam 
varṇā akārādayaḥ 
tadgrahaṇe'rthavarparibhāṣā nāsti 
yatheko yaṇaci iti nirarthakasyāpīko nirarthake'pi yaṇ bhavati bhavatyatra bhavatviti 
anyathā ṅībādisabandhina eva sārthakasyekaḥ sārthake evāci yaṇ syāt kumāryauśvaśvāviti 
tathā'sya ghvau iti nirarthakasyāpi bhavati 
śklīkarotīti anyathā'rthavata eva viṣṇuvācakākārasya syāt 
 iko jhal ityatregiti yoya varṇasamudāyaḥ sa ki sārthakaḥ pratyāhāro gṛhyatā nirarthako vā dhāturiti vicāre yuktameva rakṣitenārthavatparibhāṣayā  
pratyāhāragrahaṇamuktam  
yataḥ pratyāhāre vyavasthite uttarakāla varṇagrahaṇa na tu prathamata eva 
nanu yadi varṇagrahaṇe'rthavatparibhāṣā nāsti katha tarhi vija iṭ ityatrārthavata iṭo grahaṇa nyāsakṛtā śaṅkyate 
tathā iṭot ityatra sārthakasyeṭo grahaṇamabhidhīyate 
katha vā sīyuḍāgame kṛte kevalasyeṭaḥ sārthakatvam sasīyuṭkasyaivārthavattvāt
yathā bhindyurityatrosa ānarthakyamuktam 
 kathamiḍgrahaṇe'rthavatparibhāṣābhidhīyate yāvatā āto lopa iṭi ca ityatroktamiḍvahimahiṅityatra ṭhe karttavye ṭitkaraṇamāgamapratyayayorubhayorapi  
grahaṇārthamiti  
tadeva sāmānyagrahaṇenaiva bhavitavyam 
ucyate 
yattāvadukta varṇagrahaṇamidam 
tanna 
yato yatrānubandhamuccārya kārya vidhīyate tatra varṇāśritaḥ pratiṣedho na bhavati 
 atra ca graho'liṭi dīrgha ityatreḍapavāde īṭi karttavye'grahīdityatra sthānivadbhāvena iṭa īṭi iti sico lopārtha yadetatkṛta dīrghagrahaṇa  
tadetatsāmānyajñāpakam  
tena yatrānubandhopādāna tatra na varṇagrahaṇeṣviti na pravarttate 
yadyevamiko yaṇaci ityatrāpyanubandhopādānādanayā nopasthātavyam 
naitadasti 
kakārādīnā samudāyānubandhatvādigiti nekārādīnā sānubandhānāmupādānam 
samudāyānubandhānāmavayavānubandhatā na svīkriyate 
karmeṇiṅ iti ṅakāreṇa saṅiti pratyāhāra kṛtvā saṅantā dhātava iti karttavye sanādyantā dhātava iti jñāpakāt 
tato na sasrasimaha ityatrānunāsikalopo bhavati 
 kuruta ityatra tu ñittvādātmanepada gandhanādisūtrādanantara nānuparābhyāmiti karttavye'nuparābhyā kṛña iti yatkṛta tatsvaritañita ityasyāpi  
pratiṣedho bhavatīti jñāpanārtham  
tadeva kṛño ñakārasya samudāyānubandhatve'pyavayavānubandhatvamiti 
yastu svādi sūtre auḍasiti kṛte ḍitvāṭṭilopo doṣa uktaḥ 
so'nuparābhyā kṛña ityasya sāmānyajñāpakatvamabhyupagamya boddhavyaḥ 
yadapyukta sāgamakasyaivārthavattvamiṇmātra tvanarthakamiti 
tadapi na 
prakriyākrameṇāgamāstadguṇībhūtāstadgrahaṇena gṛhyante ityāśrayaṇāt 
bhindyuḥprastāve tvanāgamakānā sāgamakā ādeśā bhavantītyāśritam 
yaccāpyukta ṭhe karttavye ṭittvātsāmānyagrahaṇamityādi 
tadapi na 
sati prayojane jñāpakāt pratyayāgamayorgrahaṇamucyate 
vija iṭ ityitra na ki cidāgamasya ṅittve prayojanam 
atannimittatvād guṇasya 
iṭot ityatra ca prākaraṇikasyeṭo'dādeśavidhānātkuta āgamaprasaṅgāśaṅketi 
jñāpaka cātroña iti sūtram 
 yadyarthavatparibhāṣā varṇagrahaṇepi syāttadā u itītyatretiśabdekāre'narthake'rthavatparibhāṣayaiva yaṇādeśāprasaṅgaḥ siddha ityuña iti pragṛhyasajñā  
na kṛtā syāt  
kṛtā cāto jñāpakam 
atha vā bhakṣyeṇa miśrīkaraṇam iti nirddeśe jñāpakaḥ   
bhāvyamāno'ṇ savarṇānna gṛhṇāti   
vidhīyamāno'ṇ savarṇānā grāhako na bhavati 
tenehetidama iś iti trimātrasya sthānina āntaratamyāt trimātra ādeśo na bhavati 
tathā he anaḍvan ityatrāmsabuddhau iti dīrgho na bhavati 
lavitā lavitumityatra vṝto vā itīṭo vikalpena dīrghavidhānādiṭo na sarvarṇagrahaṇamityāhaḥ 
iya ca paribhāṣā aṇuditsarvaṇasya cāpratyaya ityatrāpratyaya ityasyaivārthaḥ paṭhyate 
tathā hi 
pratyāyyate vidhīyate bhāvyate iti pratyayaḥ na pratyayo'pratyayaḥ
abhāvyamāna ityarthaḥ apratyayo'ṇ sarvarṇān gṛhṇātītyasminnarthe bhāvyamānoṇ savarṇānna gṛhṇātīti vyaktamavatiṣṭhate 
sukhapratipattyartha jñāpakamapi ke cidāhaḥ 
īhalyaghoḥ iti dīrghekāravidhānam 
anyathā dīrghasya sthāne sāvarṇyārddirgha eva syāt 
anityā ceya paribhāṣā 
tenāmū ityatra dvimātrasyaukārasya dvimātra evokāro bhavati 
atra cārthe diva ut iti taparakaraṇa jñāpakam 
 yadi bhāvyamāno'ṇ sarvathaiva savarṇānna hṛhṇāti tadā dyubhyāmityatra cchroḥ śūḍanunāsike ca ityūdyapi kṛte dīrghasya sthāne hrasvaḥ siddhaḥ  
syāt ki tapakaraṇena  
tatkṛta jñāpayati kva cidbhāvyamāno'ṇ sarkṇan gṛhṇātīti 
śāsa idaṅ haloḥ iti taparakaraṇa vā jñāpakamiti   
yasminvidhistadādāvalgrahaṇe   
yasminniti saptamnirdiṣṭe algrahaṇe varṇagrahaṇe yo vidhiḥ sa tadādau samudāye bhavati na tadante 
tena pivatereśi pape ityatra pāghrādi sūtreṇa pivādeśo na bhavati 
tathā'cīti iyaṅṅuvaṅāvajādau bhavataḥ
śriyo luluvartululuvuriti 
śriyau luluva ityatrāpi vyapadeśavadbhāvāt 
yadi hyatra tadantavidhiḥ syāt śriyo luluvaturityatra na syāt halantatvāt 
aya cārtho yena vidhi sūtre tadantavidyapavādastadādividhirupasakhyātaḥ paribhāṣārūpeṇa padyata iti 
vāmanena tu guṇo'pṛkta ityatrāpṛktagrahaṇādiya varṇitā 
taduktam 
 uto vṛddhirluki halītyanuvarttamāne halādau guṇe prāpte'pṛktagrahaṇa halmātra eva yathā syāddhalādau mābhūdityevamartha kriyamāṇa jñāpayatyastīya  
paribhāṣā yasminvidhirityādi  
tena halītyanuvṛttau halādau syāt 
apṛktagrahaṇe tu varṇamātra eva bhavati praurṇoditi 
yadyeva kṅiti saprasāraṇa kṅādāveva syād gṛhīto gṛhītiriti 
yagādau na syād gṛhyata iti 
ucyate 
kṅitīti neda varṇagrahaṇamiti kṅāvitau yasyeti bahubrīhiṇā varṇasamudāyasya parigrahāt   
vidhividhānavidhibhājā trayāṇā sanidhāne tadantavidhirbhavati   
tena erac itīvarṇāntādattpratyayo bhavati 
iya paribhāṣā yena vidhi sūtrasyaiva sāmarthyāllabdho'rthaḥ padyate 
tathāhi 
yeneti karaṇe tṛtīyā na cākartṛka karaṇamastīti karttāpyāśritaḥ 
sa punariha sabandhiśabdatvādantaśabdenāvayavavācinā sannidhāpitaḥ samudāyo vijñāyate 
sa ca karttā tribhiḥ prakāraiḥ sannihito bhavati 
kva cinnirddeśāt 
yathā īdūdeddvivacanam iti dvivacana karttṛbhūta nirdiṣṭa yattadīdādibhiḥ karaṇaiḥ pragṛhyasajñā vidadhāti 
kva citprakaraṇāt 
yathā erac ityatra dhātorityadhikārāt prakaraṇāddhātuḥ karttā sanidhāpitaḥ sa ikāreṇa karaṇenāca vidadhāti 
kva citsāmarthyāt 
yathā iko jhal ityatra dhātoreva ca san vidhīyate iti sāmarthyāddhātuḥ karttā sanidhāpita ikā karaṇena sanaḥ kittva vidadhāti 
 tadevamīdūdeddvivacanamityādau pragṛhyasajñāyā vidhīyamānasya karmaṇo vidherīdūdetaḥ karaṇasya vidhānasya dvivacanasya ca kartturvidhibhājaḥ  
sabhavādyena vidhistadantasyeti tadantavidhirvidhīyate  
tadeva yena vidhiḥ ityasya sūtrasyārtha evāyamevavidho vidhividhānavidhibhājā trayāṇā sannidhāne tadantavidhirbhavati 
eco'yavāyāva ityādau vidhibhājo'sabhavānna pravarttate 
nanu śabdānuśāsanaprastāvācchabdarūpa karttṛ vidhibhāk syāt tatkatha kartturabhāvo'bhidhīyate 
ucyate 
śabdarūpa kartṛtvena nāśrīyate atiprasaṅgāditi suptiṅanta padam ityatra rakṣitena vyākhyātam 
tenaico'yavāyāva ityādau śabdarūpasyāsvīkāradejmātrasyaiva sthānitvamajmātrasya paratva naijantasyājādāviti 
tasya sthānitve vṛkṣāvatretyādāvāvādayo'nekālatvātsarvādeśāḥ syuḥ 
nanu nirddiśyamānasyādeśā bhavantītyeca eva sthāne ādeśena bhavitavya naijantasya 
satyametadvyaktau jātau tu doṣaḥ 
anyastvāha 
varnavidhitvamalvidhīnā na syāt 
tathā na yena vidhi sūtre bhāgavṛttikṛtoktam 
 iko yaṇaci itīkā acāvayavenāvayavinaḥ samudāyasya sanidhāpitatvādigantasyājādau yaṇādeśa iti varṇavidhireva na syāt tiṣṭhatu dadhyaśāna tva  
śākeneti  
 ki tu satyapogantasyājādau yaṇādeśe padavidhitva na bhavatyeva padasya padāt supsupetyādyanuccāraṇena ṣaṇādeśādikāryāṇā vidhānāditi   
iti mahāmahopādhyāyaśrīsīradevakṛtāyā paribhāṣāvṛttau prathamaḥ pādaḥ   
ekayoganirddiṣṭānā saha vā pravṛttiḥ saha vā nivṛttiḥ   
ekayoganirddiṣṭānā padānā pravṛttirvā nivṛttirvā sahaiva syāt 
na tvekasya pravṛttiraparasya nivṛttiḥ 
tena uśca ityatra liṅsicāvātmanepadeṣvityetatsarvamanuvarttate 
tadayamarthaḥ 
ṛvarṇāntāddhātoḥ parau liṅsicāvātmanepadeṣu kitau bhavata iti 
tatra hi ṛ iti ṛvarṇānto dhāturgṛhyate na ṛ gatāviti 
atra nyāsakāraḥ kāraṇamāha 
śailīyamācāryasya yatrāsya dhātorgrahaṇamicchati tatrāvaśya śtipā nirddeśa karoti 
yathā'rttipiparttyīśca sarttiśāstyarttibhyaśca iti 
atra ca nyāse sandehavicchedāyetyadhyāhāryam 
tenāyamarthaḥ 
yatrāsya dhātorgrahaṇamicchati tatra sandehavicchedāyāvaśya śtipā nirdeśa karoti 
yatra na sandehastatra karoti na karoti ca 
eva ca smipūṅrañjvaśā sani ityatra ṛgatāvityasya grahaṇe'pi na śtipā nirddeśaḥ 
tatra hi kiraśca pañcabhya ityatra dṛṅdhṛṅorgrahaṇānna sandehaḥ 
anyathā didiriṣate didhariṣate ityatra smipūṅrañjvaśā sani ityeveṭaḥ siddhatvāṭḍhṛṅdhṛṅorgrahaṇamanarthaka syāt 
yattu tatra rakṣitenoktam 
sadehavicchedāyetyatrādhyāhāryam 
tataśca śmipūṅrañjvaśā sani ityatrāvirodhaḥ 
kiraśca pañcabhya ityatra kṛgṛsvīkāra eva viccheda heturiti 
tadayuktam 
yato vṝto vā ityanuvṛtto iṭ sani vā iti vikalpeneṭi prāpte nityamiṭo vidhānārtha kṛgṝgrahaṇa syāt 
ucyate 
yadi nityamiṭo vidhānārtha kṝgṝgrahaṇa syāt tadā kiraśca pañcabhya iti sūtramakṛtvā smipūṅrañjvaśkṛgṛpracchā sanītyeva kuryāt 
na cottaratra rudādibhyaḥ sārvadhātuke ityatra pañcabhya ityasya prayojanamastīti vācyam 
rudādipañcadhātuparigrahārtha tatra vṛtkaraṇa karttavya tata eva vyavasthā bhaviṣyati 
 atha vā kṛgṛsvīkāra iti bahubrīhiraya kṛgroḥ svīkāro yasminniti kṛgṛsvīkāraḥ kiraśca pañcabhya iti yogastasminkṛgṛsvīkāre kiraśca pañcabhya  
iti sūtra evāntarbhūtayorddaṅdhṛñorgrahaṇa vicchedaheturityarthaḥ  
atha vā smipūṅrañjvaśā sani ityatra ṛgrahaṇa hrasvāntārtha tāvanna bhavati dṛṅdhṛṅgrahaṇāt 
dīrghantādapi yadi iṭ sani vā iti vikalpaḥ syād dīrghārthamapi na syānnityavikalpayorvirodhāt 
 eva ca ṛgrahaṇamanarthaka tasmādiṭ sani vā ityatra ṛgrahaṇa nānuvarttate vṛṅvṛñāvevānuvarttate vṛṅvṛñoreveḍvikalpaḥ ṛtā tu smipūṅrañjvaśā  
sani ityanenaiva nityamiṭ siddha iti kṛgṛgrahaṇameva vicchedaheturiti  
jñāpaka cātra hanaḥ sic iti sijgrahaṇam 
 yadyekasūtranirddiṣṭayorapi padayorekamanuvarttate nāparamiti tadā liṅsicāvātmanepadeṣu ityato liṅgrahaṇa nānuvarttiṣyate sijgrahaṇamevānuvarttiṣyata  
iti sijgrahaṇamanarthaka syāt  
aya ca svaritatvalabdho'rthaḥ paribhāṣārūpeṇa paṭhyate 
ata evopadeśe'janunāsika it ityato laśakvataddhita ityatra idgrahaṇānuvṛttāvapi anunāsikagrahaṇa nānuvarttate 
upadeśagrahaṇānuvarttana prati rakṣitānunyāsayorvivāda eva 
tathāhi 
gāṅkuṭādi sūtre'nunyāsakāreṇoktamādeśapakṣe idgrahaṇamanarthakamāderhi bhavato laśakvataddhita ityanenaivetsajñāyāḥ siddhatvādityādi 
 rakṣitena tūktamādibhūto ṅakāro laśakvataddhita ityatropadeśagrahaṇānuvṛtterasatīdityetasminnetsajñaka iti na jñāpakamidityetadādeśābhāvasyeti 
tatrāya rakṣitābhiprāyaḥ 
laśakvataddhita ityatrāsatyupadeśādhikāre niśśabdātsaptamībahuvacane nicśvityatra śakārasyetsajñ syāt 
na cetsajñāyā karttavyāyāmasiddhatvamasti 
sasajuṣoruḥ ityatra rorukārasyānunāsikyapratijñānasamarthyāt
riṅśayagliṅkṣu iti nirddeśācca sāmānyenetsañjñāyā karttavyāyāmasiddhatvāpravarttanasya jñāpitatvāt 
tathā bhiyaḥ kruklukanau iti bholuka ityatra klukanaḥ kakāre lupte lakārasyetsañjñā syāt 
naitadasti 
prayojanābhāvādevetsañjñāyā apravṛttiḥ 
svarastu na prayojana nittvādeva tasya siddhatvāt 
eva tarhi yaṅluki bebhīluka ityatra svaraḥ prayojanam 
tathāhi 
nittvādekāra udātto bhavati littvādīkāraḥ syāditi 
anunyāsakārasyāyamabhiprāyaḥ 
nicśvityatretsañjñā na bhavivyatyasiddhatvāt 
yattūkta rorukārasyānunāsikyapratijñānasāmarthyālliṅkṣviti nirddeśāccāsiddhatva na bhavatīti 
tadupadeśe'janunāsika it
halantyam ityetsūtradvayakarttavyatāyāmevāsiddhatva na bhavati tatraiva pramāṇasambhavāt 
anyatra tvasiddhatvameva 
bebhīluka ityatra yaṅlukaśchāndasatvāditsañjñā na bhaviṣyatīti 
yadi vā lakārasyetsañjñāyā yaṇādeśe kṛte bebhyuka ityeka evājiti kva litsvaraḥ syāt 
nicśviti jastvena śakārasya jakāraḥ ścutvena sakārasya śakāraḥ svari ca iti cartva jakārasya cakāraḥ 
nanu stoścunā ścuḥ ityatra rakṣitenokta jhalā jaś jhaśi iti nirddeśāt śakārasya jaśtva nāsti 
 ata eva masjinaśorjhali ityatra majjatisiddhaye jaśtvena sakārasya dakārastasya bhṛjjati iti nirdeśādasiddhatvābhāvāt ścutvena jakāro nyāse  
uktaḥ  
anyathā ścutvena sakārasya śakāre kṛte jastvena jakāre siddhe bhṛjjati iti nirddeśādasiddhatvābhāvapravarttanamayuktam 
eva ca kathamatra jaśtvena śakārasya jakāraḥ 
ucyate 
 jhalā jaś jhaśi ityatra cavargaparasya śakārasya jaśtvābhāvādanyatrāpi cavargaparasyaiva jaśtvābhāvastulyajātīyatvāditi yathā katha cit jñāpakasiddha  
na sarvatreti vā    
uṇādayo'vyutpannāni prātipadikāni   
aya cārtho'rthavat sūtrapraṇayanādastītyāhuḥ 
anyathā sarveṣāmuṇādīnā dhātujatvena kṛdantatvāt prātipadikasajñāsiddhau tanna kuryāt 
anye tvataḥ kṛkami ityatra kamigrahaṇa kṛttvā kasagrahaṇādetāmāhuḥ 
 tena kṛgṛkuṭividibhidibhyaśca iḥ kiditīkārapratyayāntayoḥ kirigiriśabdayorosi yaṇādeśe kṛte dhātutvābhāvāddhali ca iti dīrghatvanna bhavati  
kiryoḥ giryoriti  
etacca na samyak 
acaḥ parasmin iti sthānivatvāddīrghatvāprasaṅgāt 
na cāsti dīrghavidhi prati na sthānivaditi 
svaradīrghayalopeṣu lopājādeśo na sthāvaditi vacanāt 
yathā pratidīvneti 
 eva tarhi jīryaterdhātorjīyateḥ krin raśca va iti krin pratyaye ittve raparatve ca rephasya vakāre kṛte jivririti dhātutvābhāvāddīrgho na 
sarvo dvandvo vibhāṣayaikavadbhavati   
tena bābhravāśca śālaṅkāyanāśca bābhravaśālaṅkāyana bābhravaśālaṅkāyanā ityekavacana bahuvacana copapanna bhavati 
yadyeva samāhāhāradvandve'pi vāktvaca śrīsrajam ityatrāpi dvivacana prāpnoti paśce tathetaretarayogadvandve'pi pakṣe ekavacana syāt 
ucyate 
sarvo dvandva ityanena samāhāradvandvastathetaretarayogadvandvaśca nāpūrvatayā vibhāṣaikavat kriyate ki tarhi nyāyasiddho'nūdyate 
tathāhi 
 cārthe dvandva ityanena cārthe dvandvaḥ kriyate cārthaścetaretarayogaḥ sa eva yadodriktāvayavabhedo bhavati tadāvayavabhedānugamād dvivacanabahuvacane  
siddhe eva yadā tu tirohitāvayavavivakṣā sahatiḥ pradhānamiti yāvat tadā samāhāra iti tatra sahatipradhānatvādekavacanamiti  
tadeva cārthe eva sarvo dvandvo vibhāṣayaikavadbhavatīti paribhāṣārūpeṇa paṭhyate 
nanu cārthaḥ samuccayo netaretarayogaḥ 
caśabdaprayoge samuccayasyaiva pratīteḥ 
satyametat 
ki tu tatprabheda evetaretarayogo na tu samuccayādayaḥ 
tathāhi 
samuccaya eva yadā yugapadarthābhidhāyinā parasparāpekṣāṇā padānā bhavati tadā dvandvaḥ kriyate 
etāvataivetaretarayogaścārtha evetyucyate 
 nanu yadi cārtha evāya sarvo dvandva ityādi kimartha tarhi tiṣyapunarvasvoḥ ityatrā'sya bahuvacanagrahaṇa jñāpanārtha nyāsakṛtābhidhīyate 
tiṣya ekaḥ punarvasū ca dvau iti bahutvādbahuvacana siddhameva ekavacanasya prasaṅga eva nāsti 
bahuvacanaprsaṅge eva dvivacana bhaviṣyati ki bahuvacanasyetyanena 
tatkṛta jñāpayati 
astīya paribhāṣā sarvo dvandva ityādi 
ucyate 
jñāpayati bodhayati jñāpaka bodhakam 
kasya bodhakam 
abhimatasya niyamasyeti 
kvābhimataniyamaḥ 
dvandvaśca prāṇitūryasenāṅgānām ityatra samāhāre eva prāṇyaṅgādīnāmiti 
prāṇyaṅgādīnāmeva samāhāre nānyeṣāmiti viparītaniyame hi tiṣyapunarvasūnā sarvadā itaretarayoga eva dvandvaḥ syānnasamāhāre 
eva ca bahuvacanaprasaṅga eva dvivacanamiti gahuvacanagrahaṇamanarthaka syāt 
 etacca dvandvaśca prāṇitūrya ityatra prāṇyaṅgādīnāmeva samāhāra ityeva viparītaniyamo nāśrīyate tiṣyapunarvasvornakṣatradvandve bahuvacanasya  
iti bahuvacanagrahaṇādityādina granthena rakṣitena vyākhyātam  
nanveva dvandvaśca prāṇitūrya iti sūtramanarthaka syāditi 
tena hi samāhāre evaikavadbhāvo vidhīyate 
tatra samāhāradvandvaikatvādekatvādekavacana siddhameva 
ucyate 
prāṇyaṅgādīnā samāhāra eva dvandvo yathā syāditaretarayogo mābhūditi sūtraprayojanam 
nanu kimartha samāhāra ekavattva kriyate netaretarayoga evaikavadbhāvaḥ kriyatām 
eva ca samāhāradvandvagrahaṇa prayatnapratipādya na bhavati karya ca vidhimukhenaiva pravarttate 
ucyate 
itaretarayoga evaikavadbhāve satyasthitvacamityatra samāhāralakṣaṇo dvandvāccudaṣahāntātsamāhāra iti ṭac syāt 
nanvevamapi pūrvoktaprakāreṇa samāhāra evaikavadvacana bhavati samāhāraścaika eva 
eva caikavaditi vatirnopapadyate na hyeka evaikavadbhabhavati 
ucyate 
buddhyānekatvamāropya vatirbhaviṣyati 
ukta ca 
buddhirhi bhagavatyabhede'pi bheda janayati 
yathā rāhoḥ śira iti 
atha vā nāya vatiḥ ki tarhi vadervijanto'yamekavaditi 
nanu ca tathāpyaśeṣadvandva ekatvāvidhānāt sarvaśabdārtho'ghaṭamānaḥ syāt 
ucyate 
sarvo dvandva iti korthaḥ 
itaretarayogasamāhārātmaka ityarthaḥ 
nanvevamapi vibhāṣā vṛkṣamṛgādi sūtramanarthakam 
anayaiva paribhāṣayā bābhravaśālaṅkāyana bābhravaśālaṅkāyanā itivat plakṣanyagrodha plakṣanyagrodhā ityevamādīnā siddhatvāt 
ucyate 
siddhe paribhāṣayaikatve vṛkṣādīnā sajātīyaireva dvandva ekavadyathā syāt
na vijātīyairiti vyatikaranirāsārtha vibhāṣayaikavadvidhānamiti 
tena paśvādīnā vijātīyairdvandva ekavanna bhavatītītaretarayogo'sau dvandvao bhavati 
tathā ca bhaṭṭiḥ 
naravānararakṣāsāmiti   
iti mahāmahopādhyāyasīradevakṛtāyā paribhāṣāvṛttau gāṅkuṭādipādaḥ   
ūditsavarṇa gṛhṇāti na savarṇamātram   
udidvarṇo'ṇuditsavarṇasya iti sthānaprayatnābhyā viśiṣṭameva savarṇa gṛhṇāti na savarṇamātram 
tena coḥ kuḥ iti kugrahaṇe hakārasya grahaṇa na bhavati 
jñāpaka cātra na vibhaktau tusmā ityatra tugrahaṇa kṛtvā sakāragrahaṇamiti 
aya ca nyāyasiddha evārthaḥ sukhapratipattyartha jñāpakenokaḥ 
tathāhi 
sthānaprayatnābhyā sadṛśasya savarṇasajñā vidhīyamānā takārasakārayoḥ sparśovāṇoḥ prayatnabhedādeva sāvarṇya nāstīti tat kuto jñāpakam 
yata eva sthānaprayatnābhyā sādṛśyāt sāvarṇyamata evāi uṇiti sūtre vṛttikṛtoktam 
hrasvamavarṇa prayoge savṛtam 
dīrghaplutayostu vivṛtatvam 
teṣā sāvarṇyaprasiddyarthamakāra iha śāstre vivṛtaḥ pratijñāyata iti 
tatraika nyāsakāreṇoktam 
vivṛtataraḥ pratijñāyata iti draṣṭavyam 
anunyāsakāreṇa tu vivṛtatamaḥ pratijñāyata iti draṣṭavyamityuktam 
anyathā ākārasya vivṛtatamatvādakārasya vivṛtataratvapratijñāne satyapi sāvarṇya na syāt 
nyūnādhikaprayatnatvāt 
nyūnādhikaprayatnānā ca sāvarṇya nāstyeva 
tathā ca jājjhalau iti sūtre śakārasya sāvarṇyenāctvābhāvārtha bhāṣyakāreṇoktam 
spṛṣṭa karaṇa sparśānām
īṣatspṛṣṭamantasthānām
vivṛta karaṇamuṣmaṇām
īṣadityanuvartate
svarāṇā ca
vivṛtamityanuvarttate īṣaditi nivṛttamiti 
etenekāraśakārayorvivṛteṣadvivṛtayoḥ sāvarṇyābhāva ukto bhavati 
eva ca nā'jhalau ityasyāpi prayojana na dṛśyate 
dadhi śītamityādau nyūnādhikaguṇatvādeva sāvarṇyābhāvāt 
nyūnādhikaguṇānā ca sāvarṇyābhāvo'vaśyamevāṅgīkarttavyaḥ 
anyathā eṅaḥ padāntādati ityādau ekāraukārābhyā sāvarṇyādaikāraukārayorapi grahaṇa syāt 
rakṣitena tu eṅa ityatra eoṅṅakāreṇa praṭyāhāragrahaṇasāmarthyāt sāvarṇyābhāva uktaḥ 
anyathā aikāraukārayorapi grahaṇe eca iti cakāreṇa pratyāhāragrahaṇa kuryāt 
ki tveva yatra svarūpeṇaikāra upādīyate tatra sāvarṇya syāt 
īdūdeddivacanam iti 
atra ekāreṇa aikārasya grahaṇe sāvarṇyabhāvātkaravāvahāyitītyatrāpi pragṛhyasajñā syāt 
na cātra taparakaraṇātsāvarṇyābhāvo vācyaḥ 
taparakaraṇasya prayojanāntarābhāvena vṛttinyāsayornirdeśārthatvena vyākhyātatvāt 
 yadyevamiṇkoḥ ityatra katha nyāsakāreṇa dāsyatītyatra ākārahakārayornyūnādhikaguṇayoḥ sāvarṇyāt ṣatvaprāptimuktā vayasyāsu iti nirddeśād vyavasthoktā 
tathāhi 
hakārasya vivṛtvam 
ākārasya vivṛtatamatvam 
yadāha śikṣākāraḥ 
vivṛta karaṇamūṣmaṇā svarāṇā ca
tebhya eṅau vivṛtatarau
tābhyāmapyeau
tābhyāmapyākāra iti 
atrāhuḥ 
 vivṛta karanamūṣmasvarāṇāmityekapade karttavye yadvivṛta karaṇamūṣmaṇā svarāṇā ceti pṛthak pada kṛta tataḥ svarāṇāmityasyaivottaratra  
sūtre sambandha iti  
 tena svarāpekṣamevākārasya vivṛtatamatva noṣmāpekṣamata ākārahakārayoṣtulyaprayatnatvād dāsyatītyatra nirddeśāt ṣatvābhāvo yukta evābhihitaḥ 
rakṣitena tu iṇkoḥ ityatra nyūnādhikaguṇasyāpi sāvarṇyamuktam 
nanu dāsyatītyādāvākārahakārayorajjhaltvānnājjhalau iti sāvarṇyapratiṣedhādeva mūrddhanyo nāsti tatkimiti nirddeśena vyavasthocyate 
ucyate 
nājjhalau ityagṛhītasavarṇānā pratiṣedho vaktavya iti vacanāt 
ākārastu gṛtasavarṇaḥ 
tatkato'tra pratiṣedhaḥ 
 nanu kimarthamagṛhītasavarṇanā pratiṣedha ucyate na sāmānyenaiva pratiṣedho'stu tena dāsyatītyādau sāvarṇyābhāvo nājjhalau iti niṣedhādeva  
sidhyati  
tathā khaṭvā hastaḥ kumārī śete ityādāvakaḥ savarṇe dīrghatvābhāvārthamacītyanuvarttanīya na bhavati 
ucyate 
yadi gṛhītasavarṇānāmapi nājjhalau iti pratiṣedhaḥ syāt tat nissa ityatra jharo jhari savarṇa iti pakṣe sakāralopo nasyāt 
nṛkāreṇācā savarṇasya sakārasya grahaṇāt tasyācthalyupadeśāddhaltvamajjhalornājjhalau iti pratiṣedhāt 
na ca lṛkārasakārayornājjhalau iti savarṇasajñāniṣedhaḥ śakyate karttum 
ātmani kriyāvirodhāt 
tathāhi 
lṛkārasakārayornājjhalau iti pratiṣedhena sakārasyāctvābhāvāt 
lṛkārasakārayornājjhalau iti niṣedhī nopapadyate 
eva cātmana eva ātmanā pratiṣedhaḥ kṛtaḥ syāditi 
 agṛhītasavarṇānā pratiṣedhaśca nājjhalau ityatra savarṇasajñāpratiṣedhavākye savarṇasajñāyā anabhinirvṛttatvena grahaṇakaśāstrasyānabhinirvṛttatvāt 
eva hyukta pūrva hyapavādāḥ pravarttante paścādutsargā iti   
prakṛtivadanukaraṇa bhavati   
tena kaścidāha dviḥ paṭatīti 
tamanyo'nukaroti dviḥ paṭatītyāheti 
tatra prakṛtivadbhāvātpadatve tiṅṅatiṅa iti nighātaḥ siddho bhavati 
padatvābhāve sa na syāt 
tathā vṛṣaṇvasvaśvayorityatra nalopābhāvaṇatve bhavataḥ 
 jñāpaka cātra parivyavebhyaḥ kriya ityādau nirddeśe kriāderanukaraṇaśabdasya vibhaktyutpattyartha prātipadikasajñābhyupagame'pi dhātutvāśrayasyeyaṅādeśasya  
karaṇam  
yadyeva katha viparābhya jeḥ ityādinirddeśaḥ 
na cātra vidyamāno'pīyaṅādeśaḥ paratvād gherṅiti iti guṇena bādhyate iti śakyate vaktum 
kṣiya iti nirddeśātparamapi guṇa bādhitvā iyaṅeva bhavati pūrvavipratiṣedheneti rakṣitena vyākhyātatvāt 
eva ca kṣiyo ḍhīrghāt ityatra dīghagrahaṇamupapadyate 
anyathā hi kṣiya itīyaṅā nirddeśādeva dīrghaparigrahe siddhe dīrghagrahaṇamanarthaka syāt 
ucyate 
dvividhamanukaranam 
sārthakasya nirarthakasya ca śabdamātrasya 
tadeva kriya ityādau sārthakasyaiva labdhadhātuvyapadeśasya krītyasyānukaraṇam 
tatra dhātukāryasyeyaṅo vidyamānatvādanukaraṇe'pi tadbhavati 
viparābhyā jeḥ ityādau nirarthakasya varṇasamudāyamātrasyānukaraṇa tatra ca kriyārūpasyārthasyābhāvāddhātusajñaiva nāsti 
eva cānukārye eva dhātusajñāyā abhāvādiyaṅādeśo nāsti tadanukaraṇe kā punaḥ kathā 
tadeva dvividhamanukaraṇamiyaṅaḥ karaṇākaraṇābhyāmavadhāryate 
ata eva paṭhanti 
sārthakānukaraṇe prakṛtivadanukaraṇa bhavatīti 
nanu yadi jeriti nirarthakasyānukaraṇa katha tarhi jayaterdhātorātmane pada bodhyate 
ucyate 
sāmānyasya viśeṣagrahitayā dhātorapi pratipādanāt 
nanu yadi prakṛtivadbhāvād dhātukāryamiyaṅ tadā'dhāturiti prātipadikasajñāpratiṣedhaḥ prāpnoti 
ucyate 
adhāturiti nāya prasajyapratiṣedho dhātorna bhavatīti ki tarhi paryudāsaḥ 
dhātoranyatra bhavatīti 
krīprabhṛtayaśca śabdā anukaraṇatvenādhātavaḥ prakṛtivattayā ca dhātava iti dhātvadhātutvāddhātoranya eva bhavanti 
tathā ca kṣiyo dīrghāt ityatra kṣiyaḥ svāśrayā prātipadikasajñā bhaviṣyatīti nyā vyākhyātam 
atha vā paryudāse'dhāturiti neda śāstrīya kāryam tastatkarttavyatāyā na prakṛtivadityatideśaḥ 
paryudāse nañityeta ccārthavadadhāturapratyayaḥ prātipadikam ityatra kṣiye dīrghāt ityatra ca rakṣitenoktam 
nanvevamapyanarthaka tvādanukaraṇaśabdasya prātipadikasajñā na prāpnoti 
na cānukā evārthaḥ 
bhedābhāvāt 
bhede hi sati vācyavācakasabandhaḥ 
cānukaraṇaśabdasyānukāryaśabdātkopi bhedo'vadhāryate 
tathāpi bauddho bhedaḥ syāt 
evamapi anukāryasya vācyasya śabdātmakatvādanukaraṇasya vācakasya na tadabhidheyatvamupapadyate 
na hi śabdasya śabdāntara vācya ki tarhyartha eva 
naidasti 
śabdo'pi śabdasya vācyo dṛśyo 
yathā bhūvādiśabdo dhātuśabdasyeti 
nanu yukta tat 
ācāryeṇa sajñāvidhānāt 
eva tarhi anukaraṇamapyanukāryasya vācaka yuktam 
ācāryasya tathā vyavahārāt 
vācyavācakabhāve vyavahāra eva hi nibandhanam 
nanvevamapi satyapyarthavattve'nukaraṇādvibhaktirna prāpnoti sakhyāyā sāvidhīyate 
na cānukāryeṣu śabdeṣu dravyasamavāyinī sakhyā sabhavati 
teṣā śabdātmakatvenāvaraguṇatve satyadravyatvāt 
sakhyāpi guṇa eveti na tatrāsāvasti 
nirguṇā guṇā iti vacanāt 
ucyate śabdasyeda taditi sarvanāmaparāmarśayogyatvād dravyatvamiṣyate 
tasmātsiddhānukaraṇaśabdādvibhaktiḥ   
vikaraṇebhyo niyamo balīyān   
śabādivikaraṇāt prāganudāttaṅita ātmane padam ityādīni niyamaśāstrāṇi tāvadbhavanti tato vikaraṇāḥ 
tena nerviśa ityādau vṛttau yaduktamaḍāgamastadbhaktastadgrahaṇena gṛhyata iti tadupapanna bhavati 
tathāhi 
vikaraṇānnityāt parasmādapi niyamaḥ karttavyaḥ 
niyamakāle ca tadaivāḍāgamaḥ prāpnoti nāsāvaḍāgamo niyamenāpasāryate vikaraṇādeva niyamasya balīyastvāt 
nāpi vikaraṇenāpasārayitu śakyate niyamapravṛttikāle tasyāvidyamānatvāt 
tadeva niyamāḍāgamayoryugapatprāptau paratvādaḍāgamastato yuktamuktamaḍāgamastadbhaktastadgrahaṇena gṛhyata iti 
nanu ca niyamena pravarttamānena vikaraṇo bādhyeta tadbādhakakāḍāgamapravṛttikāle vikaraṇo nityo'ḍāgamāt prāk kasmānna bhavati 
ucyate 
yadi vikaraṇī'ḍāgama bādheta tato niṣpratidvandvī kimiti niyamo vikaraṇa na bādheteti 
tathā edhiṣyate aidhiṣṭetyatrānudāttaṅita ātmanepadameva bhavati na parasmaipadamiti 
anyathā paratvānnityatvācca vikaraṇeṣu kṛteṣu syādiṣu tairvyavadhānādanudāttaṅidbhya evātmanepada śeṣādeva parasmaipadamiti niyamo na syāt
eva ca sāmānyena tibādayaḥ syuḥ 
niyamastvāste śete ityādiṣu kṛtārthaḥ 
yadyeva syādīnā lāvasthāyāmutpattirna prāpnoti 
lādeśe tu kṛte edhiṣyate ityatra dvaya prāpnoti yak pratyayaḥ syapratyayaśca tatra paratvādyakaiva bhāvyam 
ucyate 
kartṛvācini sārvadhātuke śapi prāpte bhāvakarmaṇostu yaki syādayo vidhīyamānāḥ sāmānyena sarveṣāmapavādatvādbādhakā bhavanti 
 aya cārtho vṛdbhyaḥ syasanoḥ ityatra parasmaipadabidhā nena jñāpitaḥ anyathā vṛtu varttana ityevamādīnā syena vyadhāna cādanudāttaṅita ātmanepadam  
iti niyamo nāstīti sāmānyavihiteṣu tibādiṣu siddhamubhaya vartsyati varttiṣyatai iti kimanena vidhānena  
tatkṛtamasyārthasya jñāpakam 
anye tvasmāj jñāpakāt kṛte'pi vikaraṇe niyamaḥ pravarttate iti paribhāṣāmāhuḥ 
asmin darśane edhiṣyata ityatra lāvasthāyāmevāntaraṅgatvātsyapratyayena bhavitavyam 
tathā'sminneva darśane aupyata auhyata ityatrājāditvādāḍajādīnām ityāḍ bhavati 
anyathā hi vikaraṇānniyamasya balīyastve niyamāḍāgamayoḥ sapradhāraṇāyā paratvādaḍāgamena bhavitavyam 
na cāḍāgamapravṛttikāle nityo vikaraṇaḥ śakyate pravarttayitum 
pūrvameva niyamenāpasāritatvāt 
āḍāgamastu niyamena nāpasāryat iti paratvādasau bādhakaḥ prāpnotyeva 
tadeva halāditvādaḍāgame kṛte āṭaśca iti vṛddyabhāvādauhyata ityavamādi na sidhyati 
tathā'sminneva darśane ṛccheranādeśasya grahaṇam 
atyārdeśasya carttītyeva siddheriti samo gamyādi sūtre vṛttgrantha upapadyate 
na hi vikaraṇānniyamabalīyastve śeti vikaraṇe vidhīyamāna ṛcchādeśa ātmanepadātprāgeva bhavate 
tathā'sminneva darśane nergadādi sūtre vikaraṇāttasyāḍāgama uktaḥ 
anyathā vikaraṇānniyamabalīyastve tatopi paratvādaḍāgame kṛte katha vikaraṇāntasyāḍāgama upapadyate 
 atha vikaraṇebhya ityatra nirddeśe bhyasaḥ sakārasya rutve kṛte rukārasyopadeśe'janunāsika it itītsajñā na prāpnoti pūrvatrāsiddham ityasiddhatvāt 
ucyate 
rorukārasyānunāsikapratijñānasāmarthyādasiddhatva na bhavati 
tathā copadeśe'janunāsika ityatra rakṣitaḥ 
itsajñāyāmasiddhatva nāsti sasajuṣo ruḥ ityatrokārasyetsajñārthamanunāsikatvapratijñānasāmarthyāditi 
atrocyate 
haśi ca ityatrānunāsikaviśiṣṭasya rorgrahaṇa yathā syādityevamartha rorukārasyānunāsikatvapratijñāna syāt 
tena taruvanamityatra haśi ca ityutva na bhavati 
tatkutastatsāmarthyāditsajñā'bhidhīyate 
na ca vācya kṛtrimākṛtrimanyāyena sasajuṣo ruḥ ityasyaivottvena bhavitavyam 
na taruvanādau 
kṛtrimākṛtamayorubhayorhi sabhave kṛtrimaparibhāṣāpravṛtteḥ 
tathāhi 
utvaśāstre sasajuṣo ruḥ ityasyāsiddhatvāttaruvanasyaiva sambhavo netarasya 
eva tarhi rephasyaivānunāsikatva pratijñāyatā svaritatvapratijñānavat 
tathā cottvavidhāvanunāsikaviśiṣṭasya rephasyottve vidhīyamāne punarbhavādau kathamuttvaprāptiḥ 
tadeva rephasyānunāsikatve pratijñātavye yadukārasya pratijñāna tatsāmarthyāditsajñā bhaviṣyati 
etadapi na 
eva sthita eva śāstre rorukāramakṛtvaiva punaranantaroktaprakāreṇeṣṭasiddherukāro'nubandho vyarthaḥ syāt 
eva tarhi vyaktipadārthāśrayaṇena sāmarthyam 
etacca sasajuṣo ruḥ ityatrokārasyetsajñārthamanunāsikatva pratijñātamiti vadatā maitreyeṇa pratipāditam 
anyaḥ punarāha 
anunāsikaviśiṣṭasya yadroruttva tadapyasiddhabādhanamantareṇa na sambhavati 
tathetsajñāpi 
tatra yathā'siddhatva bādhitvānunāsikapratijñānamuttva pravarttayati tathetsajñāmapi pravarttayati 
na cottvamāśrayātsiddhamiti vacanātpravarttate 
vipakṣe pramāṇābhāvāt   
iti paribhāṣāvṛttau bhūpādaḥ   
sakṛḍgatau vipratiṣedhe yadbādhita tadbādhitameva   
punaḥ prasaṅgavijñānātsiddham   
vacanadvayamida vipratiṣedha sūtre vyaktijātipakṣayo phalabhūta paribhāṣārūpeṇa paṭhyate 
tathāhi 
vyaktau padārthe pratilakṣya lakṣaṇasya vyāpārabhedātparyāyeṇa dvāvapi vidhī prāptau 
yathā devadattayajñadattābhyāmekatra bhājane krameṇa bhujyate 
tatra vipratiṣedhe param ityanena vipratiṣedhaviṣayo niyamyate 
vipratiṣedhe parameva na pūrvamiti 
na caitena pūrvavākyānarthakyam 
vipratiṣedhasūtreṇa tasyāsattvākhyāpanāt 
tadidamucyate 
sakṛdgatau vipratiṣedhe yadbādhita tadbādhitameveti 
tasyāyamarthaḥ 
sakṛdekavāra yadbādhita tadbādhitameveti 
gatau vipratiṣedhe 
tenājjaserasuk ityanena paratvādasuki kṛte punaḥ śībhāvo na bhavati 
ye pūrvāsa iti 
tathā stāt tvamityatra tātaṅaḥ sthānivattvāḍvibhāvo na bhavati 
ghvasoreddhāvabhyāsalopaśca iti sasyaittva ca 
etacca sthānivat sūtre bhāṣye vyākhyātam 
jātau tu padārthe sakṛdekavāra lakṣaṇa pravarttate 
viṣayāntare cobhaya caritārthamiti vipratiṣedhaviṣaye'pravṛtirevobhayoḥ prāpnoti 
yathobhayostulyabalayorekaḥ preṣyo virodhādekasyāpi kāryena pravarttate 
tatra vipratiṣedhe para kāryam ityasya paravidhau vyāpārātpūrvanivṛttāvavyāpāra iti 
nanu pūrvavākyasya prāgevoktā nivṛttistatkathamidānī tadvidhānam 
ucyate 
yugapadvirodhādapravṛttirityuktam 
paratvātparavidhau kṛte virodhābhāvādyukta eva pūrvidhiḥ 
tadidamucyate 
punaḥprasaṅgavijñānātsiddhamiti 
tena bhinddhakītyatra paratvāddhibhāve kṛte punarakac kriyate 
ījaturityatra paratvātsaprasāraṇe kṛte punardvirvacanam 
yatra pūrveṇa pravarttamānena parasya bādhā tatra sakṛdgatiparibhāṣā 
yatra tu pūrva pravarttamāna para na bādhate tatra punaḥ prasaṅgavijñānātsiddhamiti keṣā cinmatam 
tadayuktam 
eva hyakṣī ityatra paratvādī ca dvivacane itīkāre kṛte punarnum syādeva 
tasmāllakṣyasthityaiva hyetayorvyavastheti 
atha punaḥprasaṅgavijñānādityatra nirddeśe punaḥśabde padatvāśrayaḥ katha visarjanīyaḥ 
yāvataikavākyatāyā karmādīnāmekatvādau svādibhirbhavitavyam 
punaḥ śabdaścāvyayam 
avyayāni ca liṅgasakhyārahitāni 
ucyate 
pañcakapakṣe sāmānyena svādividhānam 
tato bahuṣu bahuvacanam ityanena bahuṣvartheṣu bahuvacanamevetyarthaniyamena pratyayasyāniyatatvādavyayebhyaḥ svādayo vidyanta eva 
athāpi bahuṣvartheṣveva bahuvacanamiti pratyayaniyamaḥ 
tathāpi tulyajātīyāpekṣayā niyamasya yatra sakhyāsti sakhyāntara ca vyāvarttya tatraiva niyamena bhavitavyam 
 eva ca sakhyāśabdebhyo devadattayajñadattaviti dvandvasamāsācca tathā vanasyāgre'grevaṇa prācīna grāmādāmrā ityatrānabhidhānāt sarvasubādyabhāvo  
vācyaḥ  
ata eva hi trikapakṣe'pyanekavākyatā svādi sūtre vakṣyati nyāsakāraḥ 
bahuṣu bahuvacanam ityanenānekavākyatāpīhākhyāyata iti 
atha yadā trika ekavākyatāpakṣastaḍhā katha svādayaḥ 
katha ca na syuḥ 
ekatvādyabhāvāt 
 yadyeva vṛkṣādibhyo'pi na prāpnuvanti tatra yathā vṛkṣādibhyo bahuṣu bahuvacanam ityādinā svādibhiravidyamānā eva sakhyādayo'bhidhīyante 
tathā'vyayebhyo'pyabhidhāsyante 
naitat 
pratyāsattyā prātipadikārtha eva yatra sakhyādayaḥ prātipadikenānuktāstatra svādibhiḥ sakhyādayo'bhidhīyante nānyatra 
yathā ajādyataṣṭāp iti striyāmabhidheyāyā vidhīyamānaṣṭāb vṛkṣādibhyo na bhavati 
eva tarhyavyayādāpsupaḥ iti jñāpakātsakhyākarmādirahitebhyo'vyayebhyo'pi svādayo bhavanti 
tathā ca bahuvacanamityatra nyāsakṛtoktam avyayādāpsupaḥ iti jñāpakādavyayebhyastu nitsakhyebhyaḥ sāmānyavihitāḥ svādayo vidyanta eveti 
tatra rakṣitenoktam 
avyayādāpsupaḥ iti jñāpaka vyaktau 
astyeva hi tasya viṣayaḥ pralambate svarityādiravakāśaḥ 
 pralambate svarityatra hi pralambanakriyāpekṣayā svaḥśabdādavaśyamevāpādāne pañcamyā bhavitavyamatastasyā lugartha saj jñāpaka katha syāt 
tarhi vyaktāvaliṅgasakhya yadavyaya nīcairityādi tadartha yatkṛta taj jñāpakam 
nanvatrāpi prātipadikārtha ityādinā 
prātipadikārthamātre vihitāyāḥ prathāmāyā lugartha syāt tatkatha jñāpakam 
ucyate 
dvitīyādyartha yat kṛta taj jñāpakam 
etaccāsamyak avyayād dvitīyādividhānasya na ki citprayojanam 
sapūrvāyāḥ prathamāyā vibhāṣā iti vikalpitatemayādividdyabhāvaḥ prayojanamiti cet  na 
prathamāvidhānapakṣe teṣāmavaśyabhāvāt 
eva tarhi dvitīyādyantānā dvitīyādisamāsaḥ prayojanamiti cet 
etadapi na 
yataḥ pratyāsattyā tatra śritādinimittā dvitīyā samasyate 
eva ṣaṣṭhītyādāvapi supsupetyadhikārāttannimittā vibhaktirgrahītavyā 
ucyate 
prātipadikārtha sūtre arthagrahaṇamanabhisadhāya jñāpakamidam 
tadabhisadhāne jñāpakasya prayojana nāsti 
arthagrahaṇādevāvyayebhyaḥ prathamāyāḥ siddhatvāt 
ata eva prātipadikārtha sūtre rakṣitaḥ 
arthagrahaṇamaliṅgārtham 
taccāvyayam 
ata eva sakhyārahitebhyopi prathamā siddhetyavyayādāpsupaḥ iti sūtra jñāpaka prapañcatayoktam   
antaraṅgabahiraṅgayorantaraṅga balavat   
iya paribhāṣā vipratiṣedha sūtre bhāṣye nyāse ca paṭhitā 
tena dyaukāmiḥ sautthitirityādau vibhajyānvākhyānapakṣe bahiraṅgāyā vṛddherdaurbalyādantaraṅgau yaṇekādeśau bhavataḥ 
tadetadudāharaṇa diṅmātram 
samarthānā prathamādvā ityatra samarthagrahaṇātsamarthitasarvakāryāttadvitena bhavitavyamityeva yaṇekādeśayoḥ siddhatvāt 
ida tūdāharaṇa vṛkṣāi ihetyādau bahiraṅgādakaḥ savarṇadīrghādantaraṅgo guṇaḥ 
na caitadasiddha bahiraṅgaḥ mantaraṅgaḥ ityanayā paribhāṣayā sidhyati 
acorānantarye nājānantarye bahiṣṭvapraklṛptiriti tasyāḥ pratiṣiddhatvāt 
nanveva kṛte'pyatra savarṇadīrghatve'caḥ parasminpūvavidhau iti sthānijadbhāvādāṅguṇena siddha vṛkṣa iheti 
naitadasti 
ekādeśasya pūrvagrahaṇena grahaṇāt padāntavidhitvena sthānivattvapratiṣedhāt 
parādigrahaṇa tu na vācyam 
parāditvena na padāntādi sūtrāvyāpārasyāyuktatvāt 
nanvantaraṅgaparibhāṣāpi na prāpnoti 
nājānantarye iti niṣedhādeva 
tathāhi yathā asiddhaparibhāṣayā ṣatvatukorasiddha ityasyānarthakatva tathāntaraṅgaparibhāṣayāpi 
ucyate 
naivāntaraṅgaparibhāṣayā ṣatvatukorasiddha ityasyānarthakyam 
yatastuko'ntaraṅgatvātprāptiḥ 
dīrghasya nityatvāt 
tatra paratvāddīrgha eva prāpnoti 
yattūcyate nityādapyantaraṅga balīya iti tatparatvaphala na tvapūrvamiti 
atha vā'stvantaraṅgatvāttuk 
dīrghatve kṛte nimittāpāyaparibhāṣayā tannivṛttiḥ syādeva 
tadeva bahiraṅgaparibhāṣayaivānarthakya ṣātvatukorasiddha ityasya 
atastasyā eva nājānantarya iti pratiṣedhaḥ 
ki ca yadyatrāntaraṅgaparibhāṣāyāḥ pratiṣedhaḥ syāttadāntaraṅgaparibhāṣā nirviṣayā syāt 
iya ca paribhāṣā bahiraṅgaparibhāṣayaiva sarvakāryasya siddhatvād bhāgavṛttikṛtā nābhyupagamyate 
tanmate vṛkṣa ihetyādāvacorānantarye yadyapi bahiraṅgaparibhāṣā nāsti 
tathāpi padasaskārapakṣe doṣapratikṣepo vyākhyeyaḥ 
yadāhuḥ 
suvicārya padasyārtha vākya gṛhṇanti sūraya iti 
yukta caitat 
anyathā vākyasaskāre vṛkṣai ihetyādau śabdaparavipratiṣedhenāntaraṅgamādguṇa bādhitvā sarvaṇadīrghatvameva syāt 
yathā diva ut ityatra divokamo devā ityatra ukārasya yṇādeśo rakṣitenotkaḥ 
na cāntaraṅgaparibhāṣāsāmarthyād vṛkṣai ihetyādāvābguṇenaiva bhavityam 
eva hi divokasa ityatrāpi ikārasya yaṇādeśaḥ syāt 
athāsyā udāharaṇāntara kaścāya 
ṛtviya iti 
atra ghas tasya iyādeśe kṛte siti ca iti padasajñāntaraṅgatvādajādau vidhīyamānā bahiraṅgā yaci bham iti bhasajñā bādhate 
samāveśastu nāsti 
ekasajñādhikārāt 
etaccāyuktam 
siti ca iti sūtrārambhādeva bhasajñābādhakatvasya siddhatvāt 
ata evaitadarthataikasajñādhikārasya na ghaṭate 
tathāhi 
 svādiṣviti padasajñayā yaci bham iti bhasajñāyāḥ samāveśe siddhe siti ca iti kṛta yadi punaḥ samāveśaḥ syāttadā siti ca ityanarthakameva  
syāt  
athaitatsyāt 
yaci bham ityatraikasajñādhikārābhyupagamād bhapadasajñayoḥ samāveśo nāsti 
eva ca siti ca ityatrāsatyekasajñādhikāre ṛtviya ityatra bhapadasajñayoḥ samāveśaḥ syādeva 
nanvemapi siti ca ityanarthakam
tasya hyetatprayojanam 
ṛtviya ityatra sittvātpadatvenaurguṇo mābhūditi 
bhasajñāsamāveśe tu syādevaurguṇaḥ iti 
eva cākaḍārāt ityatra yadetadanunyāsakāreṇoktam 
anavakāśāyāstvidamucyate 
aya te yonirṛtviya ityatra padasajñā bhasajñā bādhata iti 
tadayuktam 
nāyuktam 
padatvasyāvagrahārthatvāt   
ubhayanirddeśe pañcamīnirddeśo balīyān   
yatra pañcamīnirddeśo'sti saptamīnirddeśaścopātto'nuvṛtto vā tatra pañcamīnirddeśasya balīyastvāttasmādityuttarasya iti pravarttate 
 tenāmi sarvanāmnaḥ suṭ ityatrāt ityanuvṛttau avarṇāntātsarvanāmna ityanayā pañcamyā āmītyasyāḥ saptamyāḥ ṣaṣṭhyā parikalpitāmāma eva suḍāgamo  
bhavati  
aya ca vipratiṣedhe para kāryam ityasyārthaḥ paribhāṣārūpeṇa paṭhyate 
tathāhi 
tasminniti nirddiṣṭe pūrvasya iti saptamīnirddeśa iko yaṇaci iti dadhyatra madhvantretyatra sāvakāśaḥ 
tasmādityuttarasya iti pañcamīnirddeśo raṣābhyā no ṇa ityatra kṛtārthaḥ 
āstīrṇamiti 
yatra tu saptamīnirddeśaḥ pañcamīnirddeśaścobhaya kṛtārtha tatrobhayaprāptau paratvāttasmādityuttarasya iti pravarttate 
tathāhi 
āmi sarvanāmnaḥ suṭ ityatrāt iti pañcamī ājjaserasuk ityatrāsugvidhau kṛtārthā 
amīti saptamī trestraya ityatra kṛtārthā 
ubhayostulyabalayorvirodhe paratvātpañcamī saptamyāḥ ṣaṣṭhītva kalpayati 
yatra tvanavakāśā saptamī tatra saptamīnirddeśa eva pañcamyāḥ ṣaṣṭītva kalpayati 
yathā''ne muk ityatra''na iti saptamī niravakāśāto yeyaḥ ityatrāta iti kṛtārthāyāḥ pañcamyāḥ ṣaṣṭhītva kalpayati 
tataścāne parato'kārāntasyaivāṅgasya mug bhavati 
yadyeva ḍaḥ si ghūṭ ityatra kathamanayā sakārādeḥ parasya dhuḍāgamaḥ 
na hi sītyasyāḥ saptamyāḥ kvāpi kṛtārthatvam 
ucyate 
yathā sītyasyāḥ saptamyā anavakāśatva tathā ḍa ityasyā api pañcamyāḥ 
eva cobhayoranavakāśayoryuktameva paratvam 
na ca yugapadanyonyaṣaṣṭhīkalpanā śaṅkyā
nāpi krameṇa 
ekaḥ pūrvaparayoḥ ityatra pūrvaparagrahaṇāt 
taduktam 
na ca yugapadabhaye prakalpike pūrvaparagrahaṇāditi 
na caiva saptamīnirddeśasyānarthakyam 
lāghavārthatvāt 
sa iti nirddeśe gaurava syāditi 
etacca ḍaḥ si dhuṭ ityatra nyāse uktam 
iha tu dīrghātpadāntādvā ityatra yadyapi cha iti saptamī kṛtārthā
tathāpi tasyāḥ svaritāsaṅgādihānuvṛttāyā niravakāśatvāddīrghādityasyāḥ pañcamyāḥ ṣaṣṭhītva prakalpayati 
pañcamī tu paurvāparya prakalpya sāvakāśā nivarttate 
tenāyamartho bhavati 
dīrghāduttaro yaśchākārastasminparataḥ pūrvasyaiva dīrghasya tugbhavati tatrāsyā na vyāpāra iti tasmādityuttarasya ityatra nyāsaḥ 
dīrghāt ityatra tu nyāsakṛtā tasmādityuttarasyetyatra tasmāditi yogavibhāgaḥ karttavyaḥ 
pūvasūtrātpūrvasyetyanuvarttate 
tena dīghāt ityādau satyapi pañcamīnirddeśe pūrvasyaiva kārya bhavatītyuktam   
sarve vidhayaśchandasi vikalpyante   
tana dhuri dakṣiṇāyāmityatrārthe saptamyā vikalpitatvāccheṣe ṣāṣṭhīvidhānāddhuri dakṣiṇāyā iti sidhyati 
tathā ye yūpāya takṣatītyatra takṣatīti bahutve ekavacanam 
aya cārthaḥ ṣaṣṭhīyuktaśchandasi vā ityatra yogavibhāgena sādhitaḥ 
iya ca paribhāṣā vyatyayo bahulamityasyaiva prapañcaḥ   
pratyayagrahaṇe yasmātsa vihitastadādestadantasya grahaṇam   
pratyaye gṛhyemāṇe yasmādasau vihitastadādereva bhāgasya tatpratyayāntasya ca grahaṇa bhavati 
prayojana dhātupratyayaprātipadikataddhitāḍhyaḥ 
sanādyantā dhātavaḥ iti yasmātman vihitastadādestadantasyaiva dhātusajñā 
cikīrṣatīti 
na saghātasya 
prācikīrṣaditi 
kṛttaddhitasamāsāśca iti kṛttaddhitāntasya prātipadikasajñā tadādestadantasyaiva 
kārako gārgya iti 
na saghātasya 
vipraḥ kārako vipro gārgya iti 
supa ātmanaḥ kyac 
putramiccati putrīyati 
saghātānna bhavati 
mahāntamputramicchatīti 
taddhitavidhau yañiñośca iti pratyayayorgrahaṇa yatastau vihitau tadādereva phak pratyayo bhavati 
gārgyāyaṇa iti 
saghātānna bhavati 
vipro gārgyāyaṇa iti 
supsupā iti samāso na saghātasya 
ṛddhasya rājñaḥ puruṣa iti 
sa cāyamartho yasmātpratyayavidhi sūtre yogavibhāgena sādhitaḥ 
tathāhi 
yasmātpratyayavidhistadādi pratyaye iti vigṛhyate 
gṛhyamāṇe iti cādhyāharttavyam 
pratyaye gṛhyamāṇe yasmāt vihitastadādireva ghiyate na tu pratyayāntaḥ saghāta iti 
ata evāṅgapāde yasmādādi sūtra kṛtvā aṅgasya iti sūtra na khaṇḍyate 
nanu tatrāpi yogavibhāgena paribhāṣā sidhyati 
satya sidhyati 
ki tu na strīpratyaye cānuparjane iti dvitīyā na sidhyati 
tathāhi 
atra kṛte neyaṅuvaṅsthānāvastrī ityato'strīgrahaṇamanuvarttate 
tatrānuvṛttisāmarthyātstrīpratyayasya grahaṇam 
pradhāne ca kāryasapratyayānna strīpratyaye cānupasarjane iti labhyate 
tarhi prakaraṇamevedamaṅgapāde kriyatām 
nacaivamatatakṣadityatra laghusajñāgurusajñayoḥ samāveśaḥ syāditi vācyam 
laghusajñāpraṇayanavaiyarthyaprasaṅgāt 
anyathā laghupradeśe hrasvagrahaṇameva kuryāt 
ucyate 
yasmādādisūtrāttadādigrahaṇa suptiṅanta padam ityatrānuvarttate 
tadarthamiha prakaranam 
tena dviḥ prayogo dvirvacanamiti pakṣe tadādigrahaṇāt pacasipacasi iti samudāyasya suptiṅanta padam iti padasajñā sidhyati 
tathāhi 
 artharūpayoḥ sāmyāt sa eva pacśabdaḥ sa eva tiṅ yaḥ pūrvasmādvihitaḥ sa eva parasmādapi vihitaḥ yaḥ parasmādapavihitaḥ sa pūrvasmādapitī tadādigrahaṇāt  
samudāyasya padatvam  
tasya ca padatve āpacasipacasi devadattā ityatrāma ekāntaramāmantritamanantike ityekāntaratā siddhā bhavati 
etacca sarvasya dve ityatra bhāṣyavyākhyāna rakṣitenoktam 
atrocyate 
nanvekaikasmādapyatra tiṅ vihitastatoneka padam 
ucyate samudāyena vākyaparisamāptiriti samudāyasya padatvam 
yatha samudāyasyāvayavānā caikāctve samudāyasya dvirvacana bhavati nā vayavānā papāceti 
tathehāpi samudāyasya padatvam 
eva samudāyaśāstramanugṛhīta bhavati 
avayavayostu padasajñāyā samudāyasya tyāgāttadviṣaya śāstra hīna syāt 
tadādigrahaṇānuvṛttirapyapārthā syāt 
atra tu pakṣe andho'ndho duḥkhītyādau pratyeka padatvābhāve padakārya na syāt 
tadartha pratyeka vākyaparisamāptyā tatre padatve padakāryamanusandheyam 
anyastvāha gaurībhyāmityatra gurusajñāyā guroranuta iti plutaḥ syāt 
sthite tvekasajñādhikāre nadīsajñaivāpavādatvānna gurusajñeti 
nanu sthitepyekasajñādhikāre gurusajñānadīsajñayorbādhyabādhakabhāvo nāsti 
bhinnaviṣayatvāt 
tathāhi 
gurusajñā varṇamātrasya nadīsajñā tvīkārāntasya 
ucyate 
varṇamātrasyaiva keṣā cinmate nadīsajñā 
na cāsmin pakṣe lakṣmīprabhṛtiṣu strītvābhāvānnadīsajñā na prāpnotīti vācyam 
yatsamudāyagata strītvamavayave samāropya nadīsajñāvidhānāt 
jñāpaka cātra neyaṅavavaṅsthānāvastrī iti pratiṣedhaḥ 
tathā cācchīnadyornum ityatra śīnadyoḥ parata iti vṛttāvukta tadeva varṇapakṣe doṣaḥ 
tasmādyathānyāsamevāstu 
etattvanāgamam   
na strīpratyaye cānupasarjane   
yeya pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣā sā strīpratyaye'nupasarjane grāhikā na bhavati 
tena stryadhikārapratyayagrahaṇe saghāto'pi gṛhyate 
na tu yataḥ strīpratyayastadādireveti vākyārthaḥ 
tena strībhyo ḍhak iti yato'ṇ tadantātkāraśabdān ṅīp 
na tadādestadantādeva ḍhak pratyayaḥ 
api tu samudāyādeva kaumbhakāreya iti 
anyathā hi avayavasya vṛddhisvarau syātām 
nanvaṇantān ṅīb vidhīyamānaḥ kṛdgrahaṇaparibhāṣayā kumbhakāraśabdādeva bhaviṣyati 
ucyate 
ṭiḍḍhāṇañ ityatrāṇiti na kṛdgrahaṇam 
api tu kṛdakṛdgrahaṇam 
 nanu pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣāyā abhāvādyathā strīpratyayāntāḍ ḍhagvidhīyamānaḥ kumbhakārītyasmātsamudāyaśabdādbhavati tathā kāraśabdādapi kva  
citsyāt  
naitat 
prādhānyātsamudāyādeva pravṛtteḥ 
tathā ṣyaṅaḥ saprasāraṇam ityatra ṣyaṅaḥ stryadhikāre vidhānāt strītva
sthānivadbhāvena pratyayatvam 
atastadgrahaṇe pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣāyā niṣedhāt ṣyaṅmātrasya saprasārana paramakārīṣagandhīputra iti 
anupasarjana iti pratiṣedhādupasarjane strīpratyaye pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣā pravarttata eva 
tenātikārīṣagandhyaputro'tikārīṣagandhyapatirityatra saprasāraṇa na bhavati 
nanvevamapi pradhāne kāryasapratyayātpradhānapratyayagrahaṇa eva pratyayagrahanaparibhāṣayā bhavityam 
eva cātikārīṣagandhyaputra ityatra saprasārana syādeva ucyate 
yadyatra saprasāraṇa syāttadānupasarjana iti pratiṣedho'narthakaḥ syāt 
nanvevamapyardhapippalītyatrāpi pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣayā halṅyādinā sulopo na prāpnoti 
strīpratyayāntasyopasarjanatvāt 
ucyate 
ekavibhakti cāpūrvanipāta ityatrānuvṛttavibhāṣāgrahaṇasya vyavasthitavibhāṣāvijñānādupasarjanasajñāyā abhāvaḥ kṛtaḥ 
ato na strīpratyaya iti tadāditadantaniyamaniṣedho bhavatyeva 
nanu śāstrīyopasajarnasajñāmābhūt 
laukika yadupasarjana tasminsati na strīpratyaya iti pravarttitu notsahate 
anupasarjana iti pratiṣedhāt 
tataśca pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāsayā tadādiniyamena bhavitavyameva 
upasarjanagrahaṇena laukikamupasarjana gṛhyata eva 
tathāhi 
 pañcakhaṭvītyatra samudāyibhyo'nyaḥ samudāya ityetasmindarśane śāstrīyopasarjanasajñābhāve'pi laukikamupasarjanamāśritya gostriyorupasarjanasya  
iti hrasvamuktā dvigoḥ iti ṅībuktaḥ  
ucyate 
 ekavibhakti cāpūrvanipāte ityatrānuvṛttavibhāṣāgrahaṇasya vyavasthitavibhāṣāvijñād yathārdhapippalītyatra śāstrīyopasarjanābhāvena laukikopasarjanāśraya  
hrasvatva na bhavati  
tathānupasarjana iti pratiṣedho'pi na bhavati 
atha vā halaṅyādi sūtre dīrghagrahaṇāt kva cidupasarjanastrīpratyaye'pi na strīpratyaye ityevātra varttata ityāhuḥ 
tenārdhapipyalītyatra halṅyādi lopaḥ sidhyati 
nanu katha jñapakam 
yāvatā vipakṣe he amba he nadi ityatra sulopo mābhūdityevamartha dīrghagrahaṇa karttavyam 
nanvatra bhavitavyamevaiṅhrasvātsabuddheḥ iti sulopena 
na ca dīrghagrahaṇātte nāpi na bhavitavyamiti vācyam 
anyathā hi halṅyādi sūtre dīrghagrahaṇameṅhrasvāt iti sūtra cākṛtvā hrasvaiṅoraṅyāpaḥ sabuddheriti kuryāt 
ata eveha he amba he nadi ityādau sulopo na bhaviṣyatīti 
 nanvevamapi badaryāḥ phala vikāra iti tasya vikāra ityarthe'nudāttādeśca ityañaḥ phale luk iti luki luk taddhitaluki iti ṅīpo'pi luki kṛte'sati  
dīrghagrahaṇe pratyayagrahaṇena badaramityatra sulopaḥ syāt sa mābhūditi sārthaka dīrghagrahanam  
ucyate 
paratvādiha napusakādamā sulopo bādhanīyaḥ 
vyaktipadārthāśrayaṇāduktamiti vā   
sajñāvidhau pratyayagrahaṇe tadantavidhirnāsti   
tena taraptamapaughaḥ iti tarammātrasya ghasajñāyā gharūpakalpa iti ghe hrasva ucyamānastarapi bhavati 
na tu tarabante 
gaurī brāhmaṇitareti 
tathā ktaktavatū niṣṭhā iti ktaktavatvoreva niṣṭhāsajñā 
na tu tadantayoḥ 
tena dṛṣattīrṇetyatra dṛṣado dakārātparasya natvābhāvo dakārasya ca pūrvasyeti 
nanu sajñāvidhau pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣā mābhūt 
hrasvavidhau tu ghānte evottarapade hrasvatvena bhāvyam 
ucyate 
hṛdayasya hallekhayadaṇlāseṣu ityatrāṇgrahaṇa kṛtvā lekhagrahaṇāddhrasvavidhāvapi na tadantavidhiḥ 
radābhyām iti natva vidhāvapo sajñāvidhau tadantavidhipratiṣedhasāmarthyādeva na tadantavijñānam 
nanu hrasvavidhau tadantavidhiniṣedhasya kṛtārthatvāt sāmarthyamayuktam 
ucyate 
 yadi sajñāvidhau tadantavidhi pratiṣedhasya taraptabvidhāveva prayojana tadā suptiṅanta padam ityatrāntagrahaṇamakṛtvā sajñāvidhau pratyayagrahaṇe  
tadantavidhirnāstītyapyajñāpayitvā taraptamapau pitau gha iti kriyatām  
aya cārthaḥ pitau taraptamapau ghasajñau bhavata iti 
antagrahaṇāttu sajñāvidhāvityāderano'pi viṣaya iti 
atha vā natvavidhau pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣā nāsti niṣṭhāśabdasya takāraviśeṣaṇatvenopādānāt 
kṛttaddhitasamāsāśca ityatra kṛttaddhitagrahaṇena tadantasyaiva sajñā na tatrayamupatiṣṭhate 
yato'pratyaya iti pratiṣedhe prāpte kṛttaddhitayoḥ sajñā''rabhyate 
apratyaya iti ca pratyayāntasya pratiṣedha ityuktam 
tena tadantasya pratiṣedhe prāpte sajñā''rabhyamāṇā tadantasyaiva bhavati 
sātpadādyoḥ ityatra sādgrahaṇācca 
 yadi kevalasya taddhitasya sajñā syānna tadantasya tataḥ sāteḥ prātipadikatvāt tataḥ supi padāditvāt ṣatvapratiṣedhe siddhe sādgrahanamanarthaka  
syāt  
supi stha ityādau tu subgrahaṇe tadantasyopapadasajñārtho yatnaḥ karttavyaḥ 
jñāpaka tvasyāḥ suptiṅanta padamityatrāntagrahaṇam 
suptiṅoḥ pratyayatvāt pratyayagrahanaparibhāṣayaiva tadantatve sitdhe antagrahaṇamihānarthaka syāt   
iti paribhāṣāvṛttau kārakapādaḥ   
iti prathamo'dhyāyaḥ   
prātipadikagrahaṇe liṅgaviśiṣṭasyāpi grahaṇam   
yatra prātipadika gṛhyate tatra liṅgaviśiṣṭasya ṅyābantasyāpi grahaṇa bhavati 
liṅgagrahaṇenātra liṅgābhivyaktihetavaṣṭāvādayo gṛhyante 
abhidhāne abhidheyopacārāt 
tena yatheha bhavati lohitādiḍājbhyaḥ kyaṣ lohitāyate 
tathehāpi lohinīyate 
yathā sarvanāmnastṛtīyā ca iti yatheha bhavati bhavatā hetunā 
tathehāpi bhavatyā hetuneti 
ke cittvacittahastidheṣṭhak iti yathā hastinā samūho hāstikamiti bhavati 
tathā hastinīnā samūho hāstikamityāhuḥ 
taccāśobhanam 
ṭhagutpatteḥ prāgeva bhasyāḍhe taddhita iti puvadbhāvāt 
na ca jāteśca iti puvadbhāvapratiṣedho'sti yata aupasakhyānikasya tena pratiṣedho na kriyate 
 etacca pravāhaṇeyībhārya ityatra jāteśca iti puvadbhāvapratiṣedhe siddhe vṛddhinimittasyeti punaḥ puvadbhāvapratiṣedhārtha pravāhanasya  
ḍha iti yaduttarapadavriddhividhāna kṛtam  
tena jāteśca ityasyānityatva jñāpitam 
tena jāteśca ityaupasakhyānikasya pratiṣedho na bhavatīti tatra nyāse vyākhyātam 
avaśya caitat 
anyathā sthite'pi hāstikamityatra bhasyāḍha ityasya jāteśca iti pratiṣedhāt puvadbhāvo na syāt 
atha bhasyāḍha ityatra taddhita iti prasaptamī na viṣayasaptamīti cenna 
bhikṣādibhyo'ṇ ityatra viṣayasaptamyā vyākhyātatvāt 
tatra hyukta yuvatiśabdasya pāṭho bhyasyāḍhe taddhit iti puvadbhāvapratiṣedhārthaḥ yauvatamiti 
anyathā hi tipratyayāntasya yuvatiśabdasyānudāttāditvādanudāttāderañ ityañbādhanārthaḥ syāt 
tathā'ṇiñoranārṣayoḥ ityatra viṣayasaptamītvamasyā rakṣitenoktam 
ucyate 
ye parasaptamīmāśrityānudāttādeśca ityañbādhanārthameva bhikṣādibhyoṇ ityatra yuvatiśabdasya pāṭhamicchanti 
tanmatena draṣṭavyamidam 
ata eva bhāgavṛttikāro yuvatīnā samūho yauvanimityāha 
dṛśyate ca 
rūpalāvaṇyasapanna kalākuśalayauvanam 
yasya puṇyakṛtaḥ preṣya saphala tasya jīvita miti 
etasminneva darśane ṅyāp sūtre rakṣitenāsyāḥ paribhāṣāyā hastinīnā samūho hāstikamityudāharanamuktam 
jñāpaka cāsyā bhāṣyakāreṇa yuvā khalatipalitabalinajaratībhiḥ ityatra samānādhikaraṇādhikāre yuvajaratyoḥ samāsavidhānamuktam 
anyathā yadyeṣā na syāttadā'nayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyānupapatteḥ samāso'ghaṭamānaḥ syāt 
atrocyate 
nanu satyapi paribhāṣāyā astitve yuvatijaratyorbhinnārthatvādanupapanna eva samāsaḥ 
tathāhi 
yuvatirdvitīyavayāḥ 
jaratī tu vṛddhābhidhīyate 
ucyate 
yuvatirjaratīva cāñcalyavirahāt 
jaratī vā yuvatiriva cāñcalyāditi yuvatijaratyoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyamasti 
yadyeva yuvā jaratīva ucchūnastanatvāt 
śmaśruśūnyatvācceti 
tathā yuveva jaratī prāgalbhyāt 
tataścātrāpi sāmānādhikaraṇyamasti tatkatha paribhāṣā jñāpyate 
ucyate 
yuvajaratītyatra yūno jaratyā saha samāse kṛte tathopacarita sāmānādhikaraṇya na pratīyate svabhāvāt 
yathā pañcabhirbhuktamasyetyasyārthaḥ pañcabhuktaśabdena 
etacca bhāṣyakāradivarṇitaliṅgaviśiṣṭaparibhāṣāyā anyathānupapattyānumīyate 
nanu yadi sāmānādhikaraṇyānupapatteḥ paribhāṣājñāpanam 
tarhi viparītorthaḥ kimiti na jñapyate 
liṅgaviśiṣṭagrahaṇe prātipadikasyāpi grahaṇamiti 
prayojana cāpi revatījagatīhaviṣyābhyaḥ praśasye ityatra jagatīgrahaṇena jagato'pi grahaṇamiti 
tathaiva eṇyā ḍhañ ityatra ṇīgrahaṇena ṇasyāpi grahaṇamiti 
ucyate 
yadi viparīto'rtho jñapitaḥ syāttadā kumāraḥ śramaṇādibhiḥ ityatra śramaṇādīnā strīliñgānā nirddeśo'narthakaḥ syāt 
nanvevamapi jaratyā samāsa ucyamāno jaratā na prāpnoti yuvajaranniti 
naitadasti 
vṛttyantare jaradbhiriti paṭhyate 
ubhayathā hyācāryeṇa śiṣyāḥ pratipāditā ityubhaya sidhyatīti yuvakhalatītyatra nyāsaḥ 
svarūpavidhiviṣaye'svarūpavidhiviṣaye ca sāmānyena paribhāṣeyam 
jñāpakamapyāhuḥ 
roṇī iti 
kutsito'ha nirddeśaḥ prathamāntatvāt 
pratyayavidhau pañcamī nyāyyā 
tatra yathā prākaraṇikī pañcamyatikramyate 
tathā grahaṇavatā prātivadikena tadantavidhirnāstītyetadapi vacanam 
tena yathā rauṇa ityatrāṇ bhavati tathā''jakarauṇa ityatrāpi 
nanu grahaṇavatā prātipadekena tadantavidhirnāstīti tadantavidhirniṣidhyate 
naceda roṇīti prātipadika strīpratyayāntatvāt 
eva tarhi taj jñāpayatyasvarūpavidhiviṣaye paribhāsā pravarttata iti 
tena kumārīmācaṣṭe kumārayatītyasya siddhaye bahulavacana nātikliśyate 
anityā ceyam 
taccānityatva śaktilāṅgalāṅkuśayaṣṭitomaraghaṭaghaṭītyatra ghaṭīgrahaṇena jñāpitam 
tenānmahata ityādinā mahatīpriya ityatrāttva na bhavati 
dviṣatparayostāpeḥ ityatra tu dviṣatī tāpayatītyatra dvitakārakanirddeśāt khacpratyayābhāvo vṛttikṛtā vyākhyātaḥ 
rājāhaḥsakhibhyaṣṭac ityatrāpi rājaśabdasyāpi pūrvanipātakaraṇānmahārājñītyatra ṭacpratyayābhāvo vṛttāvuktaḥ 
prātipadikagrahaṇe ityatra ṣaṣṭhīsamāsaḥ sa ca samarthaḥ padavidhiḥ ityetatparibhāṣosthānād bhavati 
tasyāḥ paribhāṣāyā ayamarthaḥ 
padānā vidhiḥ samartho bhavatīti 
vidhiśabdaścāca karmasādhanaḥ 
vidhīyate iti vidhiḥ 
na bhāvasādhano vidhāna vidhiḥ 
nāpyadhikaraṇasādhanaḥ padāni vidhīyante'sminniti padavidhiḥ 
karmaṇyadhikaraṇe ca iti lyuḍpavādaḥ kipratyayaḥ 
tatra karmasādhanagrahaṇe tatropapada saptamīstham ityatropapadamiti mahatyāḥ sajñāyāḥ karaṇa jñāpakam 
 tathāhi anvarthasajñeya mahatī uapapadamiti tena samarthaparibhāṣopasthānāt mahānta kumbha karotītyatra sāpekṣatvenāsāmarthyātkarmaṇyaṇpratyayo  
na bhavati  
etacca prajonam evamupapacyate 
yadyatra karmasādhanasya vidhiśabdasya grahana nānyatheti 
yattu tatra maitreyeṇokta vidhīyate vidhiḥ 
etena karmaṇi kipratyayāntatāmācaṣṭe 
karaṇādhikaraṇayorhi lyuṭā kipratyayo bādhyate 
na ca tatra vāsarūpa vidhirasti 
ktalyuṭtumunkhalartheṣu vāsurūpavidhirnāstīti vacanāt 
sapradānāpādāne ca niravatārevipūrvasya dhāñaḥ karotyarthatvāt 
bhāvasādhanastu sabhavannapi nyāsakāreṇa nirasta iti 
tatrādhikaraṇe kipratyayo nāstīti yadukta tadayukta yasmāt padaśabde karmaṇyupapade karmaṇyadhikaraṇe ca iti lyuḍapavādaḥ kipratyo'styeva
ucyate 
yathā kevala vidhiśabdamupakramya nyāsakṛtokta maitreyeṇāpi tathā vidhānādadoṣaḥ 
tathāhi 
tatra karmopapadatvābhāvāt karmaṇyadhikaraṇe ca ityasya na prāptiḥ 
 nanu tathāpyuttarakāla padaśabdasya karmaṇo'bhisabandhāt kipratyayaviṣayo'yamiti parihṛtyāpavādaviṣayamutsargo'bhiniviśata iti lyuṭ pravarttinu  
notsahate  
ucyate 
paḍhasaskārapakṣe'ntaraṅgatvātpravartito lyuṭ kipratyayena bādhitu na śakyate śvaḥ kariṣyatītyatra yathā luṭā lṛṭ pratyayaḥ 
etaccāsamyak 
śvaḥ kariṣyatītyatra yuktā lṛṭā luṭo bādhā 
luṭpratyayasyopapadasabandhenāvidhānāt 
kipratyayasya tu karmopapadasabandhena vidhānāt sarvadā vākyasaskāra eva yukta ityāhuḥ   
vibhaktau liṅgaviśiṣṭagrahaṇam   
vibhaktyāśrayeṣu kāryeṣu liṅgaviśiṣṭaparibhāṣā na pravarttate 
tena gomatītyatrogidacām iti numna bhavati 
tathā supusītyatra puso'suṅ neti 
yuvatīḥ paśyetyatra śvayuvamaghonāmataddhhita iti saprasāraṇa na bhavati 
anye tvāhuḥ allopo'n ityatrān iti yogavibhāgādangrahaṇābhisabandhādannantānā śvayuvamaghonā saprasāraṇam 
yukta caitat 
anyathā yadyanayā paribhāṣayā saprasāraṇābhāvo vijñāyate tadā yuvatśabāt kṛdikārāditi ṅiṣi kṛte yuvatītyatra saprasāraṇa syādeva 
iya ca paribhāṣā yuvoranākau ityatra bhāṣye paṭhitā 
matuvasorityatra nyāsakāreṇa vyākhyātā 
etāvataiva pramāṇam   
iti sīradevakṛtāyā paribhāṣāvṛttau samarthapādaḥ   
sūtre liṅgavacanamatantram   
tena karmaṇā yamabhipraiti ityatra yamiti pulliṅgenaikavacanena ca nirddeśasyātantratvāt liṅgāntare vacanāntare ca sajñā bhavati 
brāhmaṇyai dadāti brāhmaṇebhyo dadāti 
nyāyasiddho'yamarthaḥ 
sūtre dhānyapalālanyāyena liṅgavacanayorūpādānāt 
jñāpaka cātrārtha ākaḍārādekā sajñā ityatraikāgrahaṇam 
ardha napusakam ityatra napusakagrahaṇa ca 
dyadbhyo luṅi ityatra tvekavacanena nirddeśe karttavye yadbahuvacana tatsāmarthyānneya pravarttate   
nañivayuktamanyatsadṛśādhikaraṇe tathāhyarthaḥ   
tenāñceśchandasyasarvanāmasthānam iti sarvanāmasyānasadṛśamasarvanāmasthāna vibhaktirgṛhyate 
asyā bhāṣye'rtho vyākhyātaḥ 
nañivayuktamanyasminsadṛśādhikaraṇe varttana iti 
eva cānyaditi prathamāntapratirūpako nipāto'nyasminnityarthe varttata iti vijñeyam 
anyaḥ punarāha 
nañivayukta śabdarūpa sadṛśādhikaraṇe varttate 
kutaḥ 
yasmādanyacchabdarūpa mukhyārthavāciśabdarūpādityarthaḥ 
tadeva nañivaśabābhyā mukhyādarthādvyavacchidya gauṇa 
rthe śabdo vyavasthāpyate 
tathahyartha iti 
tādṛśa evārthaḥ pratīyata ityarthaḥ 
etenāsyārthasya pratītisiddhatva darśayati 
sā caiṣā pratītirnañsamāsa kurvatā''cāryeṇa vyaktīkṛtā 
tathāhi 
kṣiatriyārthe upacarito yo brāhmaṇaśabdastena saha nañ samasyate na brāhmaṇo'brāhmaṇa iti 
ata eva tatra nañā mukhyādarthādvyavacchidya gauṇe'rthe vyavasthāpyate 
yathā nīla ca tadutpala ceti nīlotpalamiti nīlaguṇetaraguṇebhyo vyavacchidya nīlaguṇamutpala vyavasthāpyate 
iyāstu viśeṣaḥ 
kevalaḥ prayukto'ya brāhmaṇaśabdo mukhyamevārtha gamayati prasiddhivaśāt 
gauna tu nañsanikarṣāt 
tatropacaritasya kṣatriyārthasyābhidhānāt 
tadeva paryudāse nañ vyākhyāto bhavati 
eva cābrāhmaṇa ityasya tatpuruṣasyottarapadārthapradhānatopapadyate 
tasyā ca satyāmanekamityatraikavacanāntatā sidhyati 
tathāhi
