bhramavaśād dvitvādāvarthe loke ekārthasyopacaritasya nañsanidhau gamyamānatva dṛśyate 
tathā cāropitaikatvasyārthasyābhidhāna ekaśabda upāttaḥ svasakhya eva 
yathā sākāśya catvāri yojanānītyupacāre ekavacanamupapadyate 
yadā tu yatrādvitvādāvarthe dvitvamāropita tadbhedaścāśrīyate tadā tadvacanabhedaḥ 
yathā dyudbhyo luṅi vṛdbhyaḥ syasanoḥ iti 
eva ca kṛtvā anekeṣāmityādayaḥ prayogāḥ sidhyanti 
yo'yamatrottarapadārthaprādhānye nañuktastasya prāyikatvamāhuḥ 
akarttari ca kārake ityatra kārakagrahaṇāt 
nitye hyasminnañyuktakartṛsādṛśyādeva kārakapratītiḥ syāt 
tena prasajyapratiṣedhe'pi nañisaddho bhavati 
asūryapaśyā rājadārā iti 
tathā'bhidhānasāmarthyādadharmādayo nañsamāsā viruddhādāvarthe dṛśyante iti 
nanu nañsamāsavidhau ñakāro na karttavyo na hyanyo naśabdo'sti vyadvyavacchedāya ñakāropādānamiti 
atra pūrvapakṣe rakṣitena vyākhyātam 
atrāpīdamasti prayojana netyukte niṣedhasūtrametanmābhūditi 
naitat 
vidhivākyānarthakyaprasaṅgāt 
na ca vidhipratiṣedhayoḥ paryāyaḥ kalpanīyaḥ 
mahāvibhāṣayā vikalpasya siddhatvāt 
asati vā naño ñakāre svarūpanirddeśādanavyayatve vibhiktiśrutireva pratiṣedhavākyatā nirasyati 
na caivamasmadādeśasya ṣaṣṭhībahuvacanasya grahaṇaprasaṅgaḥ 
ṣaṣṭhyantasya ṣaṣṭhītyanenaiva samāsasya siddhatvāditi 
atrāhuḥ 
nanu katha ṣaṣṭhyantasya nañśabdasya ṣaṣṭhī ityanenaiva samāso'bhidhīyate 
 yāvatā grāmo naḥ svamityatrāntaraṅgānapi vidhīn bahiraṅgo lug bādhate iti vacanānnasādeśātprāk samāse vibhakterluki ca kṛte ṣaṣṭhyantatvābhāvānnasādeśo  
na prāpnoti  
na cāsti pratyayalakṣaṇena ṣaṣṭhyantakāryam 
sāmānyātideśe viśeṣānatideśa iti ṣaṣṭhyantaviśeṣakāryātideśābhāvāt 
athāpyanalvidhāvityatra vidhigrahaṇādviśeṣo'pyatidiśyata evamapi tatra śrūyamāṇavibhaktyarthāt sthagrahaṇādvibhaktyabhāve nasādeśo nāstyeva
na iti tu samāsārthe sūtre kṛte'ntaraṅgāniti paribhāṣā nāstīti 
nasādeśasya samāsaśāstranimittatvāt 
tasmāccintyo'ya rakṣitaḥ 
atra ke ciccintayanti 
yādṛśo'tra pūrvapakṣastādṛśa eva siddhāntaḥ 
yathā hi 
 antaraṅgānapīti vacanāt ṣaṣṭhībahuvacanasya nasśabdasya grahaṇa śaṅkita tvayā tathā mayā'pi ṣaṣṭhyantasya ṣaṣṭhī ityanenaiva samāsaḥ siddha  
ityuktam    
gatikārakepapadānā kṛdbhiḥ samāsavacana prāk subutpatteḥ   
 supsupā ityadhikāre'pi kugatiprādayaḥ kartṛkaraṇe kṛtā bahulam upapadamatiṅ iti ca gatīnā kārakāṇāmupapadānā ca yo'ya samāsaḥ sa subutpatte  
prāgeva veditavyaḥ  
tena praṣṭhītyatra praśabdasya gatisajñakasya sthaśabdenāsubantenaivātaścopasarga iti kapratyayāntena kugatiprādaya iti samāso bhavati 
yadi tu subantena samāsaḥ syāttadā supaḥ prāgantaraṅgatvāṭṭāpsyāt 
eva cādantatvābhāvātpuyogādākhyāyām iti ṅīṣ na syāt 
tathā'śvadhanaśabdayośca labdhakaraṇavyapadeśayoḥ kṛdantenaiva krītaśabdena kartṛkaraṇe kṛtā bahulam iti samāsaḥ 
tathā cāśvakrītadhanakrītaśabdayoradantatvāt krītātkaranapūrvāt iti ṅīṣ bhavati tathā 
kacchaśabdasya kapratyayāntena paśabdenopapadamatiṅ iti samāsaḥ 
tathā ca kacchapaśabdasyādantatvāt kacchapīti jāteḥ iti ṅīṣ bhavati 
anyānyapi bahūni prayojanāni bhāṣye pratipāditāni 
 nanu kṛdantaiḥ samāsa kṛtvā strīpratyayaḥ kimartha pratipādyate yāvatā kṛtpratyayotpattyanantarakāla eva samāsāttannimittabhūtācca supastato'pyantaraṅgatvāt  
strīpratyayācca prāgeva puyogādākhyāyām ityādyairvākyaiḥ strīpratyaye kriyamāṇe praṣṭhī aśvakrītītyādi siddhyati  
maivam 
eva hi praṣṭhādisamudāyasyākṛdantatvena prātipadikatvābhāvattatsamudāyāt strīpratyayo na śakyate kartum 
atrocyate 
 kṛttaddhitasamāsāśca ityatra kṛdgrahaṇena kṛdgrahaṇe gatikārakapūrvasyāpi grahaṇamiti kṛdgrahaṇaparibhāṣayā samudāyasya prātipadikatvamastyeva 
maivam 
arthavadadhāturapratyayaḥ prātipadikam ityatrāpratyaya iti pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣayā pratyāntasya prātipadikasajñā na prapnoti 
ata eva tadviṣaye kṛdgrahaṇena kṛdantasya sajñā na tu kṛdgrahaṇaparibhāṣayā gatikārakapūrvasyāpi 
yadi syāttadā mūlakenopadaśa bhuṅkte iti tṛtīyāprabhṛtīnyatarasyām iti samāsābhāvapakṣe'pi tṛtīyāyā luk syāt 
na ca vācyameva hi vikalpena samāsavacanamanarthaka syāt 
svarārthatvāt 
gatikārakopapadātkṛt 
ityeṣa tatpuruṣāśrayaḥ svaro mā bhūditi 
 ki ca yadi samāsātprāk strīpratyayaḥ syāt tadā prabhāvinī prabhaviṇītyatra ṅyantasyottarapadasyānto nakāro na bhavatīti prātipadikāntanumvibhaktiṣu  
ca iti pakṣe ṇatva na syāt  
iha yadyapi prāk subutpatteriti sāmānyenoktam 
tathāpi gatikārakopapapadānā subantānāmeva samāso bhavati 
tena carmakrīti carmakārītyatra subantatvātpadanibandhano nalopaḥ sidhyati 
vaiyākarana ityatra ca padatvādaijāgamaḥ 
pramāṇa cātra tatpuruṣe kṛti bahulam iti saptamyā alumvidhānam 
atra ca pakṣe'bhiprayaṇādeḥ śakandhvāditvātsamāsastena sādhutvam 
nanu yadyuttarapade vibhaktirna bhavati tarhi tasya padatva na syāt 
tataścottarapadavyapadeśābhavāduttarapade parato vidhīyamāno'luk sarasijamityatra na syāt 
ucyate 
samāsāvayavasya hi parasya bhāgasya rūḍhyottarapadavyapadeśaḥ svīkriyate 
etaccottarapadādhikārādavasīyate 
avaśya caitat 
anyathā satyapi subantānā samāsa uttarapadatve cāpadādividhāviti vacanāt kvāpyuttarapadatva na syāt 
jñāpitā ceya paribhāṣā bhāṣyakāreṇopapadamatiṅ ityatiṅgrahaṇena 
taduktam 
supsupā ityadhikārāttiṅantena samāsasabhava eva nāsti kimatiṅgrahaṇena 
kṛta ca taj jñāpayatyetayoryogayoḥ supsupā iti nābhisambadhyate 
tena gatikārakopapadanā kṛdbhiḥ samāsavacana prāk subutpatterityupapanna bhavati 
nanu yadi gatyādīnā supaḥ prāk subantena śabdāntareṇa samāsastadā dhātūpasargasamudāyasyāpi syāt 
eva ca dhātūpasargasamudāyādvibhaktiḥ syāt 
ucyate 
pūrva dhātuḥ śādhanena yujyata ityetasmindarśana ida samādheyam 
etasyāśca dvāvarthau 
gatikārakopapadātkṛt ityatra nyāsakṛtā vyākhyātau 
gatikārakopapadānā kṛdbhireva samāso bhavati sa ca prāk subutpatterityekorthaḥ 
gatikārakopapadānāmaviśeṣeṇa samāso bhavati kṛdbhistu prāk subutpatteriti dvitīyaḥ 
tatra dvitīye'rthe prapacatitarāmityatrāpi samāsaḥ 
ke cittu subantenaiva gatyādīnā kṛdbhiḥ kva citsamāsamāhuḥ 
tathā copapadamatiṅ ityatra rakṣitenoktam 
yathā dhanakrītetyatra subantena samāsastathoraḥkeṇetyatrāpi 
tena so'padādau iti satva na bhavati 
uraśśabdasya subantena kapratyayāntena samāse kṛte kakārasya padāditvāt so'padādau iti visarjanīyasya satva na bhavatīti 
tadetadayuktam 
tathāhi yadyapi subantena samāsastathāpi satvena bhavitavyam 
uttarapadatve cāpadādividhāviti pratyayalakṣaṇapratiṣedhāt 
kaśabdasyāmubantatvena padatvābhāvāt 
ucyate 
uttarapadatve cāpadādividhāviti yo'ya pratyayalakakṣaṇapratiṣedhaḥ sa so'padādā iti pratiṣedhe karttavye na pravarttate 
gatikārakopapadānāmityasya prāyikatva so'padādau ityatra pratyayalakṣaṇapratiṣedhāpravarttana ca bhāskārāntetyatra satvanipātanādavasitam
tathāhi 
gatikārakopapadānāmiti kṛtvā yadi supaḥ prāk samāsaḥ 
tadā bhāskara ityatra uttarapadatvābhāvādeva so'padādau iti satva siddham 
 athāsyāḥ paribhāṣayāḥ prāyikatvādbhāskara ityatra subantayoreva samāsastathāpyuttarapadatve cāpadādividhāviti pratyayalakṣaṇapratiṣedhena padatvābhāvātsopadādau  
iti satva siddha syāt  
tatkṛtamuktārthasya jñāpakamiti 
jñāpakasya prayojanam 
uraḥkeṇetyādau so'padādau iti satvābhāvaḥ 
nanveva yadā supaḥ prāk samāsastadā kakārasyāpadāditvādayaḥkrītītyatra so'padādau iti satva syāt 
ucyate 
bhavitavyamevātra satveneti manyate 
atha vā so'padādau ityatra pāśakalpakakāmyeṣviti parigaṇanānna bhavati 
yadyeva pāśakalpakakāmyeṣviti parigaṇana na kriyatām 
bhāskārāntetyatra yatsatvanipātana tatsāmarthyāduttarapade satva na bhavatītyevāstu 
tata evāyaḥkrītītyādau satvābhāvaḥ siddha iti pāśakalpakakāmyeṣviti parigaṇanamanarthakameveti   
iti paribhāṣāvṛttāvaparapādaḥ   
kva cidapavādaviṣaye'pyusargo'bhiniviśate   
tena kāñcanī vāsayaṣṭiriti nitya vṛddhaśarādibhya iti mayaṭo viṣaye'nudattādeśca ityañ bhavati 
tathā pradīyatā dāśarathāya maithilītyatrāta iñ ityasya viṣaye prāg dīvyato'ṇ ityaṇ bhavati 
anyastvāha 
samarthānā prathamadvā ityato vanuvṛtteriño'bhāvapakṣe tasyāpatyam ityaṇā dāśarathāyeti siddham 
etaccāyuktam 
yatrotsargo vibhāṣā'pavādo'pi tatrāpavādenavinirmukte viṣaya utsargo na pravarttate 
pīlāyā vā iti jñāpakāt 
vāgrahaṇa tu vākyārtham 
 daśarathāpatyamityādisamāsārtha daivayajñiśaucivṛkṣisātyamugrikāṇḍeviddhibhyo'nyatarasyām ityate dvitīyānyatarasyā grahaṇa'nuvṛttiruktā nyāsakṛtā 
jñāpaka cātra kaṭa kārako vrajatītyatrākenorbhāviṣyaḍhādhamarṇyayoḥ iti bhaviṣyadakaprayoge karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhīniṣedhavidhānam 
taddhi yadyaṇ karmaṇi ca ityapavādaviṣaye tumunṇvalau kriyāyā kriyārthāyam ityutsargaḥ pravarttate tadopapadyate nānyathā 
nanu vāsarūpavidhinā'ṇ karmaṇi ca ityapavādaviṣaye ṇvulapi siddha eva 
tatkuto jñāpakam 
ucyate 
kriyāyā kriyārthāyāmupapade vā'sarūpavidhirna bhavati 
ṇvultṛcau iti ṇvuli siddhe punastumunṇvulau kriyāyām iti lṛṭ śeṣe ca iti viṣaye ṇvulo vidhānādavagamyate 
anyathā vā'sarūpavidhinaiva lṛḍviṣaye ṇvulaḥ siddhatvātpunastanna kuryāt 
kṛta cāto'vasīyate'sminviṣaye vāsarūpavidhinā tṛjādayo na bhavantīti 
nanvasati prayojane jñāpakam 
asti ca tumunṇvulau kriyāyām ityasya prayojana bhaviṣyatkāle ṇvul yathā syāt 
 tenākenorbhaviṣyadādharmaṇyayoḥ ityatra bhaviṣyadadhikāravihitasyākasya grahaṇād varṣaśatasya pūrakaḥ putrapautrāṇā darśaka ityatra ṣaṣṭhīniṣedho  
na bhavati  
ucyate 
bhaviṣyatkāle vihitasyākasya tatra gṛhaṇādiha doṣo nāstīti jñāpakavādino'bhiprāyaḥ 
tathāhi 
varṣaśatasya pūraka ityatra pūraka iti pada na bhaviṣyatkāle 
prakaraṇādevaina sarvatrāpavādaviṣaya utsargāḥ pravarttante 
ata eva gatyarthakarmaṇi dvitīyācarturthyau ceṣṭāyāmanadhvani ityatra dvitīyāgrahaṇa kriyate 
anyathā caturthī cetyevocyeta 
cakārakaraṇasāmarthyātkṛdyogalakṣaṇā ṣaṣṭhī na bhaviṣyati grāma gantā grāmāya gantā 
bhāṣye tu sūtrameva pratyākhyātam 
taduktam 
kimarthamidamucyate 
caturthī yathā syāt 
dvitīyā tu siddhā karmaṇītyeva 
caturthyapi siddhā sapradāna ityeva na sidhyati 
karmaṇā yamabhipraiti sa sapradānam ityucyate 
na ca karmaṇātra grāmamabhipraiti ki tarhi kriyayā 
kayā kriyayā gatikriyayā 
kriyāgrahaṇa ca tatrātidiśyata iti 
tatraitasminbhāṣye rakṣitenoktam 
yathā bhāṣye sūtra pratyākhyātam 
tathā śobhana grāma gacchatīti kriyāviśeṣaṇasya karmatva na syāt 
grāmāya gamyata iti cākarmakatvādbhāve lakāraḥ syāt 
atrocyate 
nanu keya vāco yuktiḥ 
gatyārthādi sūtre sati kriyāviśeṣaṇasya karmatvāt 
śobhana grāma gacchatīti sidhyati 
tadaiva ca bhāve lakārābhāvādgrāmāya gamyata iti na bhavati 
grāmo gamyata ityeva bhavatīti 
ucyate 
 gatyārthādi sūtre sati prārthanādhyavasānādikriyābhedena karmabhūtāyā gatikriyāyā viśeṣaṇatvācchobhanasya karmatvena kriyāgrahaṇa karttavyamityasyāsarvaviṣayatvācchobhana  
grāma gacchatīti bhavati  
tathā gamikriyāvyāpyatvādgrāmasya karmatvena karmaṇi lakāreṇa karmaṇo'bhihitatvādgrāmo gamyata ityeva bhavati 
nākarmakatvādbhāve lakāreṇa grāmāya gamyata iti 
tatyarthādi sūtrābhāve tu grāmāya gacchatīti siddhaye kriyāgrahaṇa karttavyamityanena sapradānatva vaktavyam 
asya cārtha kriyayā karmaṇā yamabhipraiti sa sapradāna bhavatīti 
atra grāmāya gacchatītyatra yā gatikriyā tasyāḥ prārthanādhyavasānādikriyāvyāpyatvātkarmatvam 
tathāhi 
kaścitphalaprepsuḥ phala paśyatyetasyā etatphalamiti 
dṛṣṭvā prārthate 
tatastā karttumadhyavasyati 
gamamanā ca kriyā kāraṇā nimittamiti gamyamānayāpi prārthanādhyavasānādikriyāyayā gatikriyayāḥ karmatvam 
tathā ca karmabhūtayā gatikriyayā grāmasyābhisasambandhātsapradānatvam 
ata evātra pakṣe rakṣitena grāmāya gamyata iti cākarmakatvādbhāve lakāraḥ syādityuktam 
eva ca śobhana grāma gacchatītyatra karmaṇi dvitīyānurodhena prārthanādikriyābhedo vyākhyeyaḥ 
 tataśca gatikriyāyāḥ karmatvābhāvāttadviśeṣaṇasya kutaḥ karmatvamiti yuktamukta kriyāviśeṣaṇasya karmatva na syācchobhana grāma gacchatītyatra 
nanu prārthanādikriyābhedavivakṣāyāmapi grāmasya gatikriyāvyaptatvātkartturīpsitatama karma iti karmatva prāpnoti 
kriyāgrahaṇa ca karttavyamiti sapradānatva ca 
tatra paratvātkarmasajñayā siddha śobhana grāma gacchatīti dhātorapi sakarmakatve bhāve lakāro na bhaviṣyati 
ucyate 
eva hi śobhana grāmāya gacchatītyatrāpi karmatvena sapradānasya bādhanāccaturthī na syāt 
katha tarhi bhāṣye sūtra pratyākhyātam 
ucyate 
gramāya gacchatītyatra purvavipratiṣedhena sapradānasajñaiva 
 tathā grāmo gamyata iti karmaṇi lakārārtha prārthanādikriyābhedābhāvācchobhana grāma gacchatītyatra śobhanamityasya karmatvātha bheda eva  
vyākhyeyo grāmamityasya tvabheda eveti bhāṣyakārābhiprayaḥ    
iti paribhāṣāvṛttāvanabhihitapādaḥ   
antaraṅgānapi vidhīn bahiraṅgo lyab bādhate   
samāsasya dvipadāśrayatvād bahiraṅgo lyabantaraṅgānvidhīn bādhate 
tena pradhāyetyatra dadhāterhiḥ iti hyādeśo na bhavati 
pradāyetyatra cā'caupasargātta iti 
jñāpaka cātrādau jagdhirlyapti kiti ityatra lyabgrahaṇam 
anyathā hi prajagdhyetyatrāntaraṅgatvāt tkāvasthāyā takārādau kitītyeva jagdhau siddhe lyapīti na kuryāt 
taduktam 
jagdhau siddhe'ntaraṅgatvātti kitīti lyabucyate 
jñāpayatyantaraṅgāṇā lyapā bhavati bādhanamiti 
nanu yathā jagdhyādeśasyāntaraṅgatva tathā lyabādeśasyāpi nityatvam 
kṛtākṛtaprasaṅgitvāt 
tadeva nityāntarañgayoḥ paratvāllyapā bhavitavyam 
tato lyapi jagdhyādeśo yathā syādityevamartha lyagrahaṇa tatkuto jñāpakam 
ucyate jagdhyādeśasyāpi nityatvam 
lyabādeśe kṛte'siddhaparibhāṣayā tasya prāpteḥ 
atha prajagdhyetyatra katha lyapo lakārasyetsajñā yāvatā lyavādeśasya pratyayādhikāre'vidhānāt pratyayatva nāsti 
pratyayasyetyanuvṛttau pratyayāderitsajñā 
anyathā śīṅaḥ śakārasyetsajñāyā śīṅaḥ sārvadhātuke ityatra viśeṣaṇārthatā syāt 
īṅ iti hi kṛte īṅ gatāvityasyāpi grahaṇa syāt 
ṅī gatāviti divādau paṭhite śīṅo ṅakārpadeśavaiyarthyāyetsajñā 
tarhi śāseḥ śakārasyetsajñāyā śāsa idaṅhaloḥ ityatra viśeṣaṇārthaḥ syāt 
tadapi nāsti 
aṅgā sāhacaryādāsa upaveśana ityasyāgrahanāt 
sthita eva yathā āṅaḥ śāsu icchāyāmityasyāgrahaṇam 
ṅuṅ śabda ityatra tarhi āderṅakārasyetsajñā syāt 
etadapi na 
antaraṅgatvādantyaṅakārasyetsajñāyāmiṣṭasiddheḥ 
yadi vā ṅakāradvayamādau kṛtvā ṅaṅu śabda iti paṭhite ṅuvata ityatra na dūṣaṇam 
śā hau ityatra tarhi śādeśe śakārasyetsajñāyā sarvādeśārthaḥ syāt 
paramakhaṇḍaḥ paramakhaṅga ityādau prātipadikakhakārasyetsajñāyā khityanavyayasya iti mum syāt 
ucyate 
sthānivattvenāsya pratyayatvāditsajñā bhavati 
 yadyeva dvigurekavacanam ityatra yadukta rakṣitena pāribhāṣikaikavacanagrahaṇe pratyayādhikāre'syāvidhānādasati pratyayatve pañcamyādyekavacanaṅakārasyetsajñā  
na syāt iti tadayaktam  
 tathāhi pañcapalīśabdādanattyapakṣe bahvarthatvāt bhyasādiṣu kṛteṣu teṣā sthāne pañcamyādyekavacaneṣu kṛteṣu tatra pūrvavatsthānivattvamastyevetītsajñāprāpteḥ 
ucyate 
yathā tkāpratyayasthāne lyap vidhīyate na tathā bhyasādiṣu kṛteṣu ṅasyādayo vidhīyante 
ki tarhi bahuṣu bahuvacane prāpte ekavacana ṅasyādi vidhīyate 
kuto'tra sthānyādeśabhāvaḥ 
nanu tathāpi rakṣitoktiraktirasaṅgatā 
ṅasyādiṅkāravaccaturthīṅakārasyāpītsajñāprāpteḥ 
ucyate 
 pañcamyādiryasya sa pañcamyādiḥ pañcamyā ādiḥ pañcamyādiriti ca pañcamyādiśabdasya bahubrīhitatpuruṣayorekaśeṣeṇa caturthyāḥ sākṣādeva grahaṇamākhyātam 
nanvevamapi ṭakārasya cuṭū itītsajñā na syāt 
eva tarhi pañcamyāderityādiśabdaḥ prakāre 
yadyeva ṅakārasya na syādityayuktam 
ṭakārasyāpi na syāditi vaktavyam 
ucyate 
ṅakārasyeti doṣopalakṣaṇamidam 
tena pratyayatvābhāve paradeśe niyamena prayogo na syādityapi draṣṭavyam 
nanu tathāpi labdhapratyayaikavacanasajñakasya ṅasyādervidhānādastyevetsajñā 
ki caikavacanādisajñānubandharahitasyaiva vidhīyate na sānubandhakasya 
ekavacanādisajñāyāḥ prāgevetsajñakatvāllopapravṛtteḥ 
ucyate 
ekavacanādisajñā svādi sūtra eva vidhīyate 
atra pratyayatvābhāvāditsajñā nāsti 
ataḥ sanubandhakasyaivaikavacanādisajñā 
na ca svādi sūtra eva pratyayasajñā śakyate karttum 
arthavattvābhāvāt 
prayoga evārthavattvāt pratyayasajñā 
na cātra pratyayādhikāro nāstīti vācyam 
yato'rthavataḥ pratyasajñāvidhānasāmarthyāt śāstradvāreṇa prayoga eva pratyayasajñā pravarttate 
yattu dvigu sūtre bhāgavṛttikāreṇoktam 
māharaṇa samāhāra iti bhāve ghañ iti sthite 
yadukta karmasādhane pañce kumāryaḥ samāhṛtāḥ pañcakumāri iti gostriyorupasarjanasya iti na prāpnoti 
eva tarhi bhāvasādhana iti tadayuktam 
yato gostriyorupasarjanasya ityasyābhāve hrasvo napusake prātipadikasya iti vidyata eva 
napusakatva tu sa napusakam ityanena 
ata eva svamornapusakāt iti lukā na vibhaktiśrutiḥ   
iti paribhāṣāvṛttau dvigupādaḥ   
iti dvitīyo'dhyāyaḥ   
asati sabhave bādhana bhavati   
asti ca sabhavo yadubhaya syāt   
kāryayorvirodhādasati samāveśaśadbhāve balavataikenāparasya bādhana bhavati 
tadyathā goda iti kapratyayenāṇpratyayasya bādhana bhavati yathā vṛkṣebhya ityatraittvena dīrghasya 
yadi tvasti sambhavastadobhayamapi bhavati 
yaccabdo yadyarthe tadāśabdaścādhyāhāryaḥ 
yathā kekayamitrayupralayānā yāderiya ityatreyādeśe'pi kṛte vṛddhiḥ 
kaikeyaḥ 
prāleyaḥ 
 tathā yathājātīyastathājātīya ityatra prakāravacane jātīyar ityanena svabhāvāt prakāravati vidhīyamānena jātīyarā prakāravacane thāl ityanena  
svabhāvāt prakāramātre vidhīyamanasthālpratyayo na bādhyate  
tathā corayati dhārayati cikīrṣayatītyādāvārddhadhātukasajñā pratyayasajñā na bādhate 
tatra corayati cikīrṣayatītyādāvārddhadhātukatvena laghūpadhaguṇāllopau prayojanam 
dhārayatītyatrācoñṇiti iti vṛddhirārddhadhātukatvābhāve'pi sidhyati 
tasyānārddhadhātukādhikārīyatvāt 
ata eva priyamācaṣṭe prāpayatītyādau vṛddhiḥ 
 yasmādeva tato yadukta satyāpapāśādi sūtre'nunyāsakāreṇa corayati dhārayati cikīrṣayatītyādāvārddhadhātukatvābhāve guṇavṛddhyallopā na syuriti 
tatra dhārayatītyayuktam 
nayuktam 
dhārayatītyatra hetumiti ca ityanena dvitīyo ṇijvaktavyaḥ 
tathā ca corayatīti satyāpapāśādi sūtreṇa vihitasya prathamasya ṇica ārddhadhātukasajñā prayojanamuktam 
dhārayatītyatra hetumati ca ityasya 
yadi tasyārddhadhātukasajñā na syāttadā pūrvasyā ṇeraniṭi iti ṇilopo na syāt 
nanu vṛddhyabhāvo doṣa uktastatki ṇeraniṭi ityasyābhāvenokta syāt 
ucyate 
guṇavṛddhyallopā iti vṛddhiścācceti vṛddhyatau tayorlopau vṛddhyallopau 
atha vā lupyete iti lopau vṛddhyatau ca tau lopo ceti vṛddhyallopāviti karmadhārayaḥ 
tato guṇaśca vṛddhyallopau ceti dvandvaḥ 
tena guṇavṛddhyallopā na syurityasyāyamarthaḥ 
guṇo na syāt 
vṛddhilopo na syāt 
ato lopaśca na syāt 
nanu kathamatra vṛddherlopaḥ 
yāvatā ṇeraniṭi ityanena ṇereva lopaḥ 
ucyate 
paratvādvṛddhau kṛtāyā ṇeraniṭi iti vṛddereva lopaḥ 
atha vā lopaśabdenatrābhāvo'bhidhīyate 
tenāyamarthaḥ 
vṛddherabhāvo na syāt 
aikārasya śravaṇāt 
lope nu kṛte vṛddherabhāvo bhavati 
aikārasyāśravaṇāt 
jñapaka cātra nitya kauṭilye gatau ityatra nityagrahaṇam 
taddhi gatyarthebhyaḥ kauṭilye eva yaṅ yathā syāt 
kriyāsamābhihāre mā bhūdityevamartha kriyate 
yadi tu satyapi sabhave bādhana bhavet 
tadā nityagrahaṇamanarthaka syāt 
kauṭilyayaṅā kriyāsamabhihārayaṅo bādhasya siddhatvāt 
nanu kuṭila krāmatīti vākya mā bhūdityevamartha nityagrahaṇa kriyate tatkuto jñāpakam 
ucyate 
kuṭila kramatītyādika vākyamiṣyamāṇameva 
tathā ca rakṣitaḥ 
nityagrahana vākyanivṛttyartha na bhavati vākyasyeṣyamāṇatvāt   
ktalyuṭtumunkhalartheṣu vā'sarūpavidhirnāsti   
tena napusake bhāve ktapratyayo lyuṭapratyayaśca nitya bhāve ghaña bādhate 
hasana hasitamiti hāsamiti na bhavati 
tathā samānakarttṛkeṣu tumun icchārtheṣūpapadeṣu liṅloṭāvitīmau nityameva bādhate 
icchati bhoktumiti 
tathā''to yuc itīṣadduḥsuṣu iti khala nityameva bādhate 
īṣatpānaḥ somo bhavateti 
yatra tu ktādaya evāpodyā utsargā iti yāvat 
yo'nyo'jādipratyayo'pavādaḥ stryadhikārāt prāgbhūtastatra vāsarūpavidhirbhavatyeva 
yathā ajvidhau bhayādīnāmupasakhyānamityajviṣaye vā'sarūpavidhinā lyuḍapi bhavati bhaya bhayanamiti varṣa varṣaṇamiti 
pramāṇa cātra vṛṣabho varṣaṇāditi bhāṣyakṛdvacanam 
ata evā''śite bhuvaḥ karaṇabhāvayoḥ ityatra yadukta nyāsakṛtā ghaña sārūpyādbādhate khac 
lyuṭpratyayaḥ punarvā'sarūpavidhinā bhavatyeva 
āśitabhavam 
āśitabhavanamiti 
tadupapadyate 
etasminvākya indumaitreyayoḥ śāśvatiko virodhaḥ 
tathāhi 
pratyayasūtre'nunyāsakāra uktavān pratiyantyanenārthāniti pratyayaḥ 
erac pusi sajñāyā ghaḥ prāyeṇa iti vā gha iti 
maitreyaḥ punarāha 
pusi sajñāyām iti ghapratyaya eva 
erac ityacpratyayastu karaṇe lyuṭā bādhitatvānna śakyate karttum 
na ca vā'srūpavidhirasti ktalyuḍityādivacanāt 
tatrāya maitreyābhiprāyaḥ 
ktalyuṭtumunkhalartheṣvityatra ktagrahaṇena napusakakto gṛhyate 
lyuṭā sāhacaryāt 
lyuṭsahacaritasya ktapratyayasya grahaṇāt 
tadadhīte tadveda iti matibuddhipūjārthebhyaśca iti ktaviṣaye laṭo vidhānācca 
anyathā ñītaḥ ktaḥ ityanena laṭo bādhanānmedyatīti na syāt 
na caiva miderguṇaḥ ityasyānarthakya bhūte laṅyamedyadityatra kṛtārthatvāt 
eva ca matibuddhipūjārthebhyaśca ityatra najiṅbādhanārthaḥ suptaśabdasya pāṭho'narthakaḥ 
nānarthakaḥ syaṣṭārthatvāt 
avaśya caitat 
anyathā sāmānyagrahane'pi svapeḥ kto bādhitu na śakyate ñisvapo ñītkaraṇasāmarthyāt 
ktādīnāmapodyāna vā'sarūpavidheravasthāpitatvācca 
tadeva yadi bhāvavihitaktapratyayagrahaṇavijñānāllyuḍapi bhāvavihito gṛhyate tadā ktagrahaṇamakṛtvā lyuḍgrahaṇameva kuryāt 
ata eva hāsamiti na bhaviṣyati 
lyuḍgrahana tu na pratyākhyeya sakarmakebhyo bhāve ktapratyayasyābhāvāt 
tatrobhayorūpādānasāmarthyād sāmānyavihito lyuḍ gṛhyate 
ato yuktamukta karanalyuṭā vā'sarūpavidherabhāvādacpratyayo nāstīti 
avaśya caitat 
anyathā vuñchaṇādi sūtre saptadaśa pratyayā iti vṛttigrantho'sādhuḥ syāt 
parimāṇākhyāyām ityanenāca bādhitvā ghaño vidhānāt 
nanveva vā'sarūpo'striyām ityatra yadukta rakṣitena lyuṭsahacarito napusakakto nitya bādhaka iṣyata iti 
tathā matibuddhipūjārthebhyaśca ityatra yadukta ktalyuṭtumunkhalartheṣviti lyuṭsahacarito napusakakto gṛhyata iti tadayukta syāt 
ucyate 
nātra napusakabhābārtha kṛta lyuṭsahacaritatva ki tarhi lyuṭā saha vidhānam 
napusake bhāve kto lyuṭ ca iti yāvat 
anunyāsakārasya tvayamabhiprāyaḥ 
ktalyuḍityatra lyuḍapi bhāvavihita eva gṛhyate tumunā sāhacaryāt 
ubhayopādāna tu spaṣṭārtham 
etacca tvayāpi vācyam 
yataḥ sāmānyagrahanapakṣe'pi ktagrahaṇamanarthakameva 
yathā karaṇādhikaraṇayorlyuṭā vā'sarūpavidherabhāvadacpratyayo nāstītyuktam 
tathā bhāvalyuṭāpi saha vā'sarūpavidherabhāvād ñagha nāstītyato hāsamiti na bhaviṣyati 
na ca vaktavya grahaṇopādānāt karaṇādhikaranalyuṭaiva vā'sarūpavidherabhāva iti 
eva hi vijñāyamāne prayojanābhāyāt 
nanvidamasti prayojana sakarmakebhyo bhāve kto nāstīti kāramiti yathā syāt sāmanyalyuḍgrahaṇe tu kāramiti na syāt 
lyuṭā ghaño bhādhanāt 
ucyate 
na hi jñāpakādaniṣṭa kriyate jñāpakādācāryeṇeṣṭasūcanāt 
ata eva nātrobhayorupādānāt sāmānyavihitaḥ ktī gṛhyate 
tadeva karaṇe lyuṭā vā'sarūpavidhināstyevācpratyayaḥ 
na cāsminvyākhyāne saptadaśa pratyayā iti vṛttigrantho'saṅgataḥ syāt 
padasaskārapakṣe pratyayaśabda vyutpādyottarakāla parimāṇākhyāpratīteḥ 
ghapratyayena vā saptadaśa pratyayā iti bhaviṣyati 
atha vā pratyaya iti sūtrasādhane kāyabādhāpakṣe'ckārya lyuṭśāstreṇa bādhyate 
lyuṭśāstra ca śāstrabādhapakṣe ghaśāstreṇa bādhitam 
pratyayapravṛttau tvantaraṅgatvādac pratyayaḥ 
acpravṛttau lyuṇ nāsti lyuṭśāstrasya ghaśāstreṇa prāgeva bādhitatvāt 
eva ca na cakrakamiti 
etasyāḥ prāmāṇa vā'sarūpo'striyām ityatra vāgrahaṇasya vyavasthitavibhāṣāvijñāna nyāsakāreṇoktam 
jayādityena ta praiṣātisarga ityatra kṛtyagrahaṇamuktam 
ke cidvibhāsāgreprathamapūrveṣu ityatra vibhāṣāgrahaṇādityāhuḥ   
sāpratikābhāve bhūtaprvagatiḥ   
varttamānābhāve bhūtapūrvasyāśrayaṇa bhavati 
yathā vṛkṣairityatra bahuvacanae jhalyet ityettve'pi kṛte'to bhisa ais prapnoti 
taduktam 
kṛte'pyettve bhautapūrvyādais tu nityastathā satīti 
 tathā āchi āyāma ityasmālliṭi dvirvacane'bhyāsasya hrasvatve ca kṛte bhūtapūrvagatyā dvimātro'yamākāra ityata ādeḥ iti taparakaraṇāddīrgho  
na bhavati  
tathā ca āñcha āñchatuḥ āñchuriti tasmānnuḍ dvihalaḥ iti nuḍāgamo na bhavati 
 na caiva pibateḥ sani dvirvacane'bhyāsahrasvatve ca kṛte bhūtapūrvagatyā dvimātro'yamākāra iti taparakaraṇāt pipāsatītyatrettva na prāpnotīti  
vācyam  
yaṅlugantātpāpaṭheḥ sani pāpaṭhiṣatītyatra sāpratikasya dvimātrasya vyāvṛttau taparakaraṇasya kṛtārthatvāt 
sāpratikābhābagrahaṇādve gaurityatra bhūtapūrvaiṅantādeṅhrasvātsabuddheḥ iti sabuddhilopo na bhavati 
he paṭo ityatra sāpratikasya vidyamānatvāt 
 jñāpaka cātrāco yat ityajgrahaṇa taddhi halantāṭṭahalorṇyat iti ṇyata vakṣyatīti pāriśeṣyādajantādeva yati siddhe dhitsya ditsyamityatrārddhadhātuka  
iti viṣayasaptamyāmato lope kṛte'jantabhūtapūrvādapi yathā syādityevamartha kriyate  
etadarthatā ca tadā yadeha bhūtapūrvagatiḥ syāt   
nānubandhakṛtamasārūpyam   
anubandhakṛtamasarūpatva nāśrīyate 
tena goda iti kaviṣaye'ṇ na bhavati 
jñāpaka cātra dadātidadhātyovirbhāṣā iti ṇasya viṣaye vikalpena śavidhānam 
yadvyanubandhakṛtamasārūpya syāttadā vā'sarūpavidhinaiva dāyo dada iti ṇaśābhyā siddha syāt 
nana yadyanubandhakṛtamapi vairūpya syāttadā vā'sarūpo'striyām ityatrārūpagrahaṇamanarthakam 
ataḥ sāmarthyātmavogagatamasārūpyamāśrayaṇīyam 
na ca kāṇoḥ prayoge'sārūpyamasti 
ato na bhaviṣyati vā'sarūpa vidhiriti 
staccāpyuktam 
anubandhasārūpye vā'sarūpavidhirmā vijñāyītyevamarthamasarūpagrahaṇa syāt 
igupagajñāprīkiraḥ kaḥ mūlavibhujādibhya upasakhyānamiti kaḥ 
pacādyac harateranudyamane'c 
yadi hi syāt tadā nityopapadasamāsābhāvānmūlānā bhibhujo'śasya hara ityapi syāt 
asadetat 
mūlavibhujādibhya ityasyānarthakatvāt 
akārādanupapadātsopapado bhavati vipratiṣedheneti vacanācca 
astvantaraṅgatvānnirūpapadaḥ 
vā'sarūpavidhinā sopapado bhaviṣyati eva tarhi kkibaṇośca śāstrakṛt śāstrakāra ityatra vā'sarūpavidherabhāvāt samāveśo na syāt 
na kvipaḥ prayogo'sti aśrāvitvāt   
iti śrīsīradevakṛtāyā paribhāṣāvṛttau pratyayapādaḥ   
lakṣaṇapratipadoktayoḥ pratidoktasyaiva grahaṇa na tu lākṣaṇikasya   
lakṣaṇa lākṣaṇikamupacārāt 
pratipadokta viśeṣeṇa pratipāditam 
tayormadhye pratipadoktasyaiva grahaṇa bhavati na tu lākṣaṇikasya khaṇḍato vyutpāditasya 
tadyathā 
īṅo ṇici krīṅjīnā ṇau ityāttve pukri ca kṛte āprūpe sampanne lyapi parato vibhāṣāpa ityanenāyādeśo na bhavati 
adhyāpya gata iti 
pratipadoktasya tvāperdhātorbhavati prāpya prāpayyeti 
tathā vaseḥ kvipi usiti 
uṣā caratītyatrārthe carati iti tṛtīyāsamarthāt ṭhaki kṛte usśabdasya lākṣaṇikatvādisusuktāntāt kaḥ iti ko na bhavati 
auṣikamiti 
pratipadoktospratyayāntādbhavati 
dhānuṣka iti 
nanveva sati hvāvāmaśca ityatra māgrahaṇena meṅo grahaṇa na syāt  na 
gāmādāgrahaṇaparibhāṣayā lākṣaṇikasyāpi bhavati 
na caiva mā māna ityasyāpi grahanamiti vācyam 
gāmādāgrahaṇaparibhāṣayā lugvikaranaparibhāṣābādhasyāniṣyamāṇatvāt 
yattu ghumāsthāgādi sūtre nyāsakāreṇa lugvikaraṇaparibhāṣāyā api bādha uktaḥ 
tatkeṣā cinmatamiti 
 yattu hvāvāmaśca ityatra maitreyeṇokta yeṣā darśana gāmādāgrahaṇeṣvaviśeṣa iti lakṣaṇapratipadoktaparibhāṣābādhanārthamida niranubandhakaparibhāṣābādhanārthamida  
vā teṣā mā māna ityasya lumvikaraṇatvād grahana veditavyam  
tatra yadukta lakṣaṇapratipadoktaparibhāṣābādhanārthamiti tadayuktam 
eva hi sānubandhakatvānmāṅmeṅoreva grahaṇa na syāt 
mā māna ityasyaiva niranubandhakasya syāt 
niranubandhakalugvikaraṇavicāre cāntaraṅgatvānniranubandhakaparibhāṣaiva pravattate 
anyathā vyākhyāne tvasterbhū iti śtipā nirddeśo vaicitryārtha iti yadukta tadasagata syāt 
asati śtipā nirddeśe lugvikaranaparibhāṣayā asukṣepaṇa ityasyaiva grahaṇaprasaṅgāt 
atha niranubandhakaparibhāṣāyāḥ pratyayaviṣayatvādiha dhātugrahaṇe tadvyāpārābhāvaḥ 
yathā na kavateryaṅi ityatra vyākhyāta nyāsakṛtā 
lumvikaraṇaparibhāṣayā kautairagrahaṇamiti 
tathāpi yadukta niranubandhakaparibhāṣābādhanārthamida ceti 
tadasaṅgata yato niranubandhakaparibhāṣābādhe lākṣaṇikatvānmeṅo grahaṇa na syāt 
māṅ māna ityasyaiva grahaṇa syāt 
ucyate 
neda rakṣitena vyavasthārthamuktam 
ki tarhi sarvathā lugvikaraṇaparibhāṣā gāmādāgrahaṇaparibhāṣayā na bādhyata iti pradarśanārtham 
tathāhi 
ida keṣā ciddarśana lakṣaṇaparibhāṣā bādhyate keṣā cidubhayaparibhāṣā na tu lugvikaranaparibhāṣāpīti yāvat 
etaccāyuktam 
ghumāsthāgādi sūtre nyāsakārena lugvikaraṇaparibhāṣābādhasyāpyuktatvāt 
eva tarhi niranubandhakaparibhāṣābādhanārtha veti 
nāya vāśabdaḥ pakṣāntare ki tarhi samuccaye 
tadayamarthaḥ 
gāmādāgrahaṇaparibhāṣā lakṣanaparibhāṣā bādhate niranubandhakaparibhāṣāmapīti 
samuccaye'pi vā śabdo dṛśyata eva 
yathā sagrahaśabdasya vyutpattau nyāsakṛtokta samyak samantādveti 
asyāyamarthaḥ 
samyaksamantācceti 
khaṇḍaśo vyutpanna hi lākṣaṇikamiti na sarvasamatam 
 tena vibhāṣā diksamāse bahuvrīhau ityatra sarvanāmavidhau pratipadoktasya diṅgāmānyantarāla iti bahuvrīhergrahaṇa dakṣiṇapūrvasyai dehīti 
na tvanekamanyapadārtha ityatrasya 
yā pūrvā sottarāsyonmugdhasya tasmai purvottarāyeti 
tathā ca ṝta iddhātoḥ ityatra ṝvarṇagrahaṇepīyamuktā 
jñāpaka cātra karttari bhuvaḥ khiṣṇuc khukañau ityatra khiṣṇuca ikārāditvam 
taduktam 
udāttatvādbhuvaḥ sidvamikārāditvamiṣṇucaḥ 
nañastu svarasiddhyarthamikārāditvamiṣyate 
anityā ceya paribhāṣā 
taccānityatva yāvatpurānipātayoḥ iti viśeṣaṇādavasitam 
tena dādhāghvadāp ityatra ghāgrahaṇena dheṭo'pi grahaṇa bhavati 
etattvapiditi karttavye'dābiti yat kṛta tallakṣaṇaparibhāṣāyā abhāve heturiti tata eva siddham 
ida tu vaktavyam 
adhyāpayatītyatra lākṣaṇikasyākārasya pugiti   
ekadeśavikṛtamananyavat   
tenābhavadityatretaśca itīkāralope kṛte tiṅāśrayā sārvadhātukasajñā padasajñā ca 
tathā kariṣīṣṭetyatra syasicsīyuṭ iti soyuḍgrahaṇena sīmātrasya grahaṇam 
grahiṇotītyatra tvacaḥ parasmin ityādina syānivadbhāvenāpi hinumīnā iti ṇatva sidhyati 
nyāyasiddheyam 
tathāhi karṇacchede'pi śvā śvaiva nāśvo nāpi garddabha iti 
jñāpakamapyāhuḥ 
āḍhyādi sūtre'ttvāviti pratiṣedhaḥ   
kva cidvikṛtirapi prakṛti gṛhṇāti   
tena nisamupavibhyo hvaḥ iti hvādhātorātmanepadamucyamāna prakṛtibhūtādapi bhavati 
nihvayate sahvayate 
jñāpakañcātra na vyo liṭi iti vikṛtasya vyeñitvasya nirddeśena vyeña āttvaniṣedhavidhānam 
atrāhuḥ 
na vyo liṭi ityatra nisamupavibhyo hvaḥ ityatra caikārāntāyā eva prakṛterupādānam 
vikṛtistu lakṣaṇagatenāttvena 
tasmāddādhāghvadāp ityatra dādhāgrahaṇe prakṛtibhūtayorapi deṅdhergrahaṇam 
praṇidayate praṇidhayatīti   
bahuvrīhau tadguṇasavijñānamapi   
guṇo viśeṣaṇamupalakṣaṇam 
citragavādiḥ sa guṇo yasyāsti sa tadguṇaḥ 
bahuvrīhisamāse viśeṣaṇasahitasyaiva śāstre savijñānam 
tadyathā 
sarvādīni sarvanāmānīti sarvasyāpi sajñā siddhyati sarvasmāyiti 
tasau matvarthe ityatra tūdaśvittvānityacopalakṣye matvarthe matupo'ntarbhāvāttaddvāreṇaiva matupi sajñākārya siddham 
na tatreyamapekṣyate 
yathā kākebhyo dadhi rakṣyatāmityatropalakṣanāt kākādapi rakṣyate 
sūtre'piśabdāt kva cidatadguṇasavijñānamapi veditavyam 
tadukta siddha gadguṇāguṇābhyā pāṇineryathā loka iti 
loke hi tadguṇe'tadguṇe ca bahuvrīhirdṛśyate 
yathā lambakaramānaya 
citragumānayeti 
jñāpaka cātrāḍhyādi sūtre cvyartheṣvityutkā'cvāviti niṣedhavacanam 
yuktirapyatra vidyate 
tathāhi 
sarva ādiryeṣāmiti na viśvādayo'nyapadārthāḥ 
na hi teṣāmavayavaḥ sarvaśabdo bhavati 
tasyānārambhakatvāt 
na ca samīpārthe bahuvrīhirasti 
anabhidhānāt 
na hi lambakarṇa ityanena yasya samīpau lambau karṇau so'bhidhīyate 
ki tarhi yasyāvayavau sa eva 
tasmāt samudāya evānyapadārthaḥ na ca samudāyasyaikatvāt sarvādīni ityatra bahuvacanānupapattiḥ 
udriktāvayavabhedaḥ samudāyo'nyapadārtha ityāśrayaṇāt 
ato bahuvacana yuktameva 
tadeva samudāye sarvaśabdo'ntarbhūta iti tasyāpi sajñā bhavati   
tācchīlikeṣu vā'sarūpavidhirnāsti   
tadyathā'laṅkṛñ itīṣṇucā'laṅkariṣṇurityeva bhavati 
na vā'sarūpa vidhinālaṅkāraka iti 
jñāpaka cātra tṛjbādhanārtha nindahisādi sūtra vuño vidhānam 
yadi hi vā'sarūpa vidhinā ṇvulādayastācchīlikeṣu bhaveyuḥ 
tadā ṇvultṛcau iti ṇvuli kṛte nindako hisaka ityādayaḥ siddhāḥ 
ki vuño vidhānena 
tatkṛta jñāpayati tācchīlikeṣu va'sarūpa vidhinā tṛjādayo na bhavantīti 
tadeva tācchīlikānāmatācchīlikaurvā'surūpa vidhirnnāstīti jñāpitam 
idānī tu tācchīlikanā tācchīlikaireva vā'sarūpa vidhirnnāstīti jñāpyate 
jucaṅkramyadanndramyasūgṛdhijvalaśucalaṣapatapada ityatra paderdhātīryujartha padagrahaṇamanarthakam 
anudāttetaśca halādeḥ ityanenaiva yu cā padana ityasya siddhatvāt 
eva tarhi laṣapatapada iti padyateryuco bādhaka ukañ syāt  na 
vā'sarūpa vidhinā yujapi bhaviṣyati 
tadeva yujvidhāna jñāpayati tācchīlikanā tācchīlikairvā'sarūpa vidhirnnāstīti 
tenālapūrvātkarotestṛnna bhavati alakattati 
prāyika caitatat 
sūdadīpadīkṣaśca iti dīpo yucpratiṣedhena jñāpitam 
yadi tācchīlikeṣu vā'sarūpa vidhirnnāstyeva 
tadā namikampismyajasakamahisadīpo raḥ iti rapratyayenaiva viśeṣavihitena yuj bādhiṣyate ki pratiṣedhena 
tat kurvan jñāpayati kva cidasti samāveśa iti kamrā kamanā yavatiriti rayucoḥ samāveśaḥ siddhaḥ 
gantā'khilaḥ gāmuka iti tṛjukañorvikatthī vikatthana iti ghinuṇyucoḥ samāveśaḥ siddhaḥ   
iti paribhāṣāvṛttau karmaṇipādaḥ   
purastādapavādā anantarān vidhīn bādhante nottarān   
pūrvasthā apavādā anantarān samīpasthānevotsargān bādhante nottarān 
vyavahitārtho'trottaraśabdaḥ 
tadyathā 
hvāvāmaśca ityapavādaḥ samīpamevānupasarge ka bādhate na vyavahita tācchīlikaṇini svargahvāyīti 
bādhyaviśeṣacintāyā caiṣā paribhāṣā pravarttate na samudāyāpekṣayetīko jhal ityatra nyāsakṛtoktam 
tena niṣṭhāyā seṭi ityanena ṇilopena yathā bhakṣitamityatreyaṅ bādhyate tathā kāritamityatrairanekāco'sayogapūrvasya iti yaṇādeśaśceti 
jñāpaka cātra parimāṇākhāyā sarvebhya ityatra sarvagrahanam 
taddhi dvau kārau trayaḥ kārā ityatrāpo bādhanārtham 
anyathā purastādapavādanyāyena samīpasyairac ityasyaiva bādhaka syāditi 
anantarasya vidhirvā bhavati pratiṣedho vetyetsvarūpayā'nayaiva ca paribhāṣayā votāpyoḥ ityatra sūtre nyāse yaduktam 
yadyatrāṅo nirddeśastadā vautāpyo iti prāpnoti 
pareṇa saha guṇe kṛte pūrveṇa saha vṛddhyā bhavitavyam 
sautratvādadoṣa iti 
tadupapadyate 
tathā hyomāṅośca ityanena pararūpatvena samīpabhūtamakaḥ savarṇe dīrghatva bādhyate 
na tu vṛddhireci ityapi 
 anyathā hyomāṅośca ityanena vṛddhidīrghayorapavādena pararūpatvena votāpyoḥ itinirddeśasya siddhatvānnirddeśādasya siddhirityayuktamukta syāt 
etaccāsamyak 
sarvaṇadīrghabādhane u omāṅośca iti pararūpavidhānavaiyarthyāt 
naitat 
achāchādanamityādau pararūpatvenānunāsikākāranivṛtteḥ prayojanatvāt 
anyathā savarnadīrghatvenātra pakṣe'nunāsikopyākāraḥ syāt 
tadevamomāṅośca ityatra yanmaitreyeṇoktam 
āṅa saha yatraikādeśo nāsti tatra pararūpatvena sarvanadīrghatvena viśeṣa ityekādeśa udāhriyate āūḍhā oḍhā adyoḍheti 
taccintyam 
 tadetadanantaroktanyāsasamarthanamayuktam tatra vṛttikārādibhiḥ pararūpatvasya sarvāpavādatvena vyākhyātatvāt ata evādyoḍhetyudāhṛta vṛttau 
iti paribhāṣāvṛttau bahulapādaḥ   
nānubandhakṛtamanejantatvam   
tena dādhā ghvadāp ityatra dādhāgrahaṇena deṅdheṭorapi grahaṇam 
anyathā gatepyanubandha upadeśa ejantatvābhāvāccetā stotetivadāttvābhāvāttayorgrahaṇa na syāt 
etaccāyuktam 
syasicsīyuṭtāsiṣu ityatrājgrahana kṛtvā yad graherupādana karoti tenopadeśāśrayakāryaviṣaye'nubandho nāśrīyata ityasya jñāpitatvāt 
yathā piṣlṛdhātau pranipeṣṭetyatra śeṣe vibhāṣā kakhādāvaṣanta upadeśe iti pratiṣedhāṇatva na bhavati 
tathātrāpyanubandhe gate'pyejantāśrayeṇāttvena bhavitavyameva 
ida tūdāharaṇam 
adābiti dāpgrahaṇe daipo'pi ghusajñāpratiṣedhaḥ siddhaḥ 
avadāta mukhamiti 
bhāṣye punarddivādau dāp śodhana iti paṭhitavyamityuktam 
nanvetadyadi prayojana tadā dādhā ghvapiditi kriyatām 
eva hi daipopi pitvād ghusajñāpratiṣedhaḥ siddhyati 
lāghavañca bhavati 
nānubandhakṛtaparibhāṣāpi nāśrayitavyā bhavati 
ucyate 
dādhā dhvapiditi kṛte lakṣaṇaparibhāṣātra na pravarttata ityatrārthe pramāṇa na syāt 
adāviti tu kṛte yathā pratiṣedhe lākṣaṇikasyāpi daipo grahaṇam 
tathā vidhāvapi dādhāgrahaṇena lākṣaṇikasyāpi grahaṇamupapadyate 
tathā codīcā māṅo vyatīhāre ityatra rakṣitenokta jñāpakaphalamida dādhā ghvapidityanena yadyapi sidhyati 
tathāpi tathā nirddeśo na kṛta iti tatraiva pratipāditamiti 
 ki tvapāviti dvivacanena nirddeśe kṛte'vidyamānaḥ pakāro yayostāvapāviti pratiṣedhe dābdaiporgrahaṇasāmarthyādvidhāvapi dādhāvapi dādhāgrahaṇe  
lakṣanaparibhāṣātikramaḥ śakyata eva vyākhyātum  
tathā tu na kṛta praṇidāpayatītryatrāpi puki kṛte'pāviti pratiṣedhāśaṅkāprasaṅgāt 
apitāviti tu kṛte yadyapyetatparihriyate tathāpi tathā na kṛta vaicitryārthatvāt 
jñāpaka cātrodīcā māṅo vyatīhāre iti kṛtāttvasya nirddeśaḥ 
anejantatve hi sa na syāt 
na ca māṅ māna ityasyaiva nirddeśastasya vyatīhāre vṛttyasabhavāt   
cānukṛṣṭa nottaratra   
cakāreṇānukṛṣṭamuttaratra nābhisambadhyate 
tena vadaḥ supi kyap ca iti cakāreṇānukṛṣṭasya yato bhuvo bhāva ityatrānuvṛttirnna bhavati kyapastu bhavati brahmabhūyamiti 
yatra svaritatvenānuvṛttau siddhāyā cakāreṇānukarṣaṇa kriyate tatrāsyā vyāpāraḥ 
yatra tu pratiyogina dṛṣṭvā nivṛttau prāptāyā cakāreṇānuvarttana tatreya nopatiṣṭhate 
tenāntarāntareṇayukte ityatra dvitīyānuvarttate 
maitreyaḥ punaḥ sāmānyenaitā manyate 
yadāha 
iko jhal ityatra cānukṛṣṭatvādityapi siddhānta iti 
 jñāpaka cātrā'vyaye'yathābhipretākhyāne kṛñaḥ tkvāṇamūlau ityatra ṇamuladhikāreṇa ṇamulvacana yadi cānukṛṣṭamapyanuvarttate tadā tkvā cetyovocyate 
anityā ceyam 
taccānityatva prātipadikāntanumvibhaktiṣu ca iti cānukṛṣṭamapi vikalpa nivarttayitumekājuttarapadeṇa iti punargrahaṇādavasīyate   
iti sambandhapādaḥ   
iti tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ   
madhye'pavādāḥ pūrvān vidhīn bādhante nottarān   
tadyathā 
kṛño hetutācchīlyānulomyeṣu iti pūrvamaṇa bādhayte 
vidyā yaśaskarī 
na para tācchīlikaṇini śrāddhakārīti 
evamiṇo yaṇ iti pūrvamiyaṅa bādhate 
na parau vṛddhiguṇau āyakamayanamiti 
 na saprasāraṇe saprasāraṇam ityatra saprasāraṇagrahaṇānuvṛttau yat saprasāraṇagrahaṇa tatsāmarthyāduttarasyāpi śvayuvamaghonāmataddhita  
ityetasya pratiṣedho bhavati  
yūnaḥ paśya yūnā yūnā iti 
 ata eva saprasāranagrahaṇasāmarthyāt saprasāraṇapratiṣedhe karttavye'ca parasmin iti sthānivadbhāvo'pi na pravarttate sthānivatkṛta vyavadhāna  
vā nāśrīyate  
nanu tatra vyatho liṭi iti yatsaprasāraṇamavyadhāne prāpnoti tadbādhanārtha saprasāraṇagrahaṇa syādvivyatha iti 
naitat 
yadyetāvatprayojana syāttadā saprasāraṇagrahaṇamakṛtvā vyatha ityeva kuryāt 
vyathaśca saprasāraṇe saprasārana na bhavatīti siddha vivyatha iti 
vyatho liṭi ityatraiva vā vyatho yo liṭoti kuryāditi 
jñāpaka cātra bahuvrīherūdhaso ṅīṣ ityatra svaritatvāsañjana vṛttinyāsapratipāditam 
taddhyana upadhālopino'nyatarasyām ityatra svaritatvādanuvarttate 
tenāna upadhālopino'nyatarasyām iti paratvād bhaviṣyanta ṅīpa bādhitvā bahuvrīherūpadhaso ṅīṣ iti ṅīṣeva bhavati 
ghaṭodhnīti 
anyathā ṅoṣ madhyepavādatvātpūrvayoreva ḍāppratiṣedhayorbādhakaḥ syāt 
ṅīṣṅīpośca svare bhedaḥ 
svaropi bhedako bhavati 
yadāhuḥ 
tridhā śabdo bhidyate rūpato'rthataḥ svarataśceti 
tathā ca taddhitā ityatra maitreyaḥ pratipāditavān 
yadi stryadhikārāt pūrvamida syād tadā dūṣaṇāntaram 
īhā ceṣṭeti 
yasyeti ceti lope kṛte ekādeśa udāttenodātta ityudātto na syāt 
atra codayanti 
 īhā ceṣṭetyatrākāralope kṛte yadyapyekādeśa udāttenodātta ityudāttatva nāsti tathāpyanudāttasya ca yatrodāttalopa ityanenodāttatva vidyata  
eveti  
na cānayorudāttayorviśeṣosti 
astītyucyate 
tathāhi 
 yadaikādeśa udāttenodātta ityanenāsiddhādhikārīyeṇodāttatva kriyate tadā pūrvatrāsiddham iti tasyāsiddhatvādudāttasvaritaparasya sannatara  
ityanenekāraikārau sanatarau na bhavataḥ sannataro'nudāttatara ityarthaḥ  
yadā tvanudāttasya ca yatrodāttalopa ityanena kriyate 
tadā tasya siddhatvādudāttasvaritaparasya sannatara sati sannataraḥ syāt 
ekādeśasvarasyāsiddhatve'pyakārapratyayasyodāttatvamāśritya sannatareṇa bhavitavyameveti na vācyam 
yata ekādeśena pratyayasya nivarttitatvāt 
kutastasyādyudāttatvam 
asiddhatva tvekādeśasvarasya na tvekādeśasya 
nanvevamapyekādeśasvaro'ntaraṅgasiddho vaktavya ityanenaikādeśasvarasya siddhatvāt sannatareṇa bhavitavyameva 
ucyate 
tatra hi parigaṇanamasti 
ayavāyāvaikādeśaśatṛsvaraikānudāttasarvānuḍhāttārtha iti 
nanvevamapi svaritaparatvāt sannatareṇa bhavitavyameva 
ekādeśasvarasyā'siddhatvādudāttānudāttayorekadeśa āntaratamyāt svaritaḥ 
naitat 
antaratamasvarasyodāttatvena bādhitatvāt 
atha tasyāsiddhatvāt kutastena bādheti cet  na 
parihṛtyāpavādaviṣayamutsargaḥ pravarttata iti svarita udāttaviṣaye na pravarttate 
nanvasiddhatvāt kutastasya viṣayo'yamucyate 
ucyate 
asiddhatvena tatkāla udāttatvasya pravṛttirnirākriyate 
na tvaviṣayatva kriyate 
viṣaye ca pravarttamāno'pavāda utsarga bādhata eva 
dadatītyatrādādeśo yathā 
evañcātrāpi svaritasyodāttatvena bādhā karttavyā 
nanvevamapi sannataro'trānivāryya eva 
īhaceṣṭibhyā gurośca hala ityakārapratyaye kṛte ṭabutpatteḥ prāgeva sannatareṇa bhavitavyamantaraṅgatvāt 
tasmādboddhavyo'ya rakṣitaḥ 
boddhavyāśca vistarā eva rakṣitagranthā vidyante 
tathāhi 
ṅyāp sūtre ābanteṣvapi ḍāpcābantayoḥ pūrvoktāt kāraṇāditi 
tathā tatraiveha cenaḥ striyām itīnnantādbahudaṇḍinīkā ceti vibhāṣā kabvidhiriti 
tathā ṛnnebhyo ṅīp ityatra kartrī hartrīti gherṅiti iti na guṇaḥ supi ca ityanuvṛtteḥ supi ṅiti tadvidhānāditi 
na krīḍādibahuca ityatra tathā kroḍāśabdāt strīliṅgāt pratiṣedha uktastathā pulliṅgādbhavativyameveti lakṣyata iti   
anantarasya vidhirvā bhavati pratiṣedho vā   
vidhirvā prateṣedho vā'nantarasyaiva bhavati 
yathā vā cchandasi ityanena serhyapicca ityanantaramapittva vikalpyate na tu vyavahito hirādeśaḥ 
yuyuhi yuyohi 
tathā neṭi iti vṛddhipraṣedho'nantarasyaiva vadavrajahalantasyācaḥ ityasya bhavati 
adevīditi 
na sici vṛddhernāpi mṛjervṛddhiḥ ityasya alāvīdamārjjīditi 
kva cittu svaritatvapratijñānasāmarthyādvyavahitasyāpi vidhiniṣedhau bhavataḥ 
yathā ṭiḍḍhāṇañ iti ḍāpā vyavahitasyāpi ṅīpo vidhiḥ 
tathā kālādhvanoratyantasayoge iti dvitīyā vyavahitāpi vidhīyate 
tathā na ṣaṭsvasrādibhya iti dvayorapi ṭāpṅīpoḥ pratiṣedhaḥ 
aya cārthaḥ prattyāsattinyāyalabdhaḥ padvyate 
jñāpakamapyāhuḥ 
sakhyāvyayādeḥ iti ṅībvacanam 
taddhi bahuvrīherūdhaso ṅīṣ iti ṅīṣā vyavahito ṅībiti punaḥ kriyate 
pratiṣedho'pyanantarasyaiva bhavatītyatra na ktici dīrghaśca iti dīrghagrahaṇa jñāpakam 
tadapyanayā paribhāṣayā yantiḥ santirityatrānantarasyānudāttopadeśa ityasyaiva pratiṣedhaḥ syāt 
na vyavahitasya kkijhaloḥ kṅiti ityasyetyevamartha kriyata iti   
akṛtavyuhāḥ pāṇinīyāḥ   
kṛtamapi śāstra nivarttayanti   
viśiṣṭa ūho niścayo vyūhaḥ 
viśeṣaṇākṛtaniścayāḥ 
pāṇinīyāḥ kṛtamapi lakṣaṇa vyabhicārayantītyarthaḥ 
tena papuṣaḥ paśyetyatra yadyapi papivasśabdācchas vihitastathāpyakṛtavyūhā iti vacanāt 
papāvas asiti sthite saprasāraṇa saprasāraṇāśraya ca kārya balīyo bhavatītīḍāgama bādhitvā saprasāraṇam 
tato valāditvābhāvādiṇ na bhavati 
atrahuḥ 
astviṭ 
usyapadāntāt iti pararūpatve siddha papuṣa iti 
etaccāyuktam 
usyapadāntāt itya trādityanuvṛtteḥ 
nanu tathāpīṭo yaṇādeśe kṛte bahiraṅgaparibhāṣayā saprasāraṇasyāsiddhatvādvali lopena siddham 
asāhitikatvādvali lopasyācoranānantaryye'vidhānānnājanantarya ityatra nāsti 
na ca bahiraṅgaparibhāṣayā yaṇādeśa eva na prāpnotīti vācyam 
nājānantaryya iti vacanāt 
atrocyate 
antaraṅge vali lope karttavye bahiraṅgasya yaṇādeśasyāsiddhatvādyaṇeva nāsti kuto vali lopa iti 
bahiraṅgatva tu yaṇādeśasya sahitāpekṣatvāt 
ki tveva varttate varddhete ityatrāto ṅitaḥ iti bahiraṅgasyaikādeśasyāsiddhatvādvali lopo durghaṭaḥ 
anye tu prayojanamida nimittāpāyaparibhāṣayā siddhamityācakṣate 
na cāsiddhaparibhāṣayā nimittasadbhāvo'stīti vācyam 
 asiddhavadatrāmāt iti bhādhikārīyāyā paribhāṣāyā karmavyāyā bahiraṅgasya bhādhikārīyasya saprasāranasyāsiddhatvādaṅgavaikalyena paribhāṣāyā  
vyāpārābhāvāt  
nanu ca vyāśrayatvāt kathamasiddhavadatrābhāt ityasya vyāpāraḥ 
ucyate 
paribhāṣāyā yannimitta bahiraṅga saprasāraṇādi tasya yannimitta svādi tadvasoḥ saprasāraṇam ityasyāpi 
paramparayāpi yannimitta tadapi paribhāṣāyā nimittamāśrīyate 
bhādhikārīyakāryametadarthameva siddhādhikāra iṣyate 
atī'styeva samānanimittatvamiti 
avaśya caitat 
papuṣaḥ paśyetyādāvāto lopa iṭi ca iti lopārtha vyākhyeyam 
na cātrosyapadāntāt ityasti
tatkarttavyatāyā saprasāranasyāddhatvāt 
etaccāsamyak 
acorānantarye sahitādhikārīya usyapadāntāt iti karttavye nājānantarya ityanayā asiddhaparibhāsāpratiṣedhāt 
eva tarhyusyapadāntāt ityatra pratipadoktasyoso grahaṇe papuṣa ityatra lākṣaṇika usi pararūpatva nāsti 
ata evāsiddhavadatrābhāt ityatra nyāsakṛtokta pratipadoktasya hyustatra grahaṇamiti 
nanūsyapadāntāt ityatra lākṣaṇikaparibhāṣābādhāt sāmānyagrahaṇamuktam 
ucyate 
eva manyate 
lakṣaṇaparibhāṣābādho na karttavyaḥ 
prayojanābhāvāt 
astu lakṣaṇaparibhāṣā 
 na caiva papuṣaḥ paśyetyatra chāndasodāharaṇe sārvadhātukasajñāpakṣe āto lopa iṭi ca ityasyābhāllākṣaṇika usyusyapadāntāt ityasyābhāvādākāraśrutirdūṣanam 
śnābhyastayorāt ityākāralopaśchāndasatvāt 
yat evāsiddhaparibhāṣā nāsti 
tata evāpṛkta ekālpratyaya ityatra rakṣitenoktam 
vopṛktasyetyucyamāne na doṣo darvirityādāvapṛktatvepīti na vācyam 
tathā ca rājakṛtvānamācaṣṭe rājakṛtvayatītyatrāpi prasañga iti 
tathā janasanakhanakramagamo viṭ ityatra rakṣitenoktam 
ikāro verapṛktasya iti viśeṣaṇārtha iti 
asati tasmin paralokadṛśvayatītyatra ṇici ṭilope kṛte vakāralopaḥ syāt 
tasmādikāro viśeṣaṇārtha iti 
etadasiddha bahiraṅgamantaraṅga ityasya ṭilopasyādiddhavadatrābhāt ityasiddhatvenāpravarttanādupapadyate 
 yadyeva yuvoranākau ityatra yadukta rakṣitenāṅgasajñānimittayoryakāravakārayorgrahaṇe'nunāsikayoryakāravakārayorgrahaṇamanarthakameveti 
tadayuktam 
pūrvoktakrameṇa rājakṛtvayati paralokadṛśvayatītyatrādeśaprasaṅgāt 
ucyate 
bhādhikārātprāgya asiddhādhikāramāhuḥ 
tanmatena vāha uṭhaṭilopayorābhācchāstrīyatvannāsti 
ato'siddhaparibhāṣāyā karttavyāyāmasiddhavadatrābhāt ityasyāpravṛttirityadoṣaḥ 
jñāpaka cātra samarthānā prathamādvā ityatra samarthagrahaṇam 
tathāhi 
yadyeṣā na syāt 
tadā samarthitasarvakāryāttaddhito yatha syādityemartha samarthagrahaṇamanarthaka syāt 
gorataddhitaluki ityatrātaddhitagrahana ke cidāhuḥ 
taddhi subluki mābhūdityevamartha kriyate rajagavīyatīti 
atra ca prāgeva niṣpannaṣṭac taduttarakāla kyaci subluki yadā pravṛtto'pi ṭac nivarttate tadā bhavati   
iti sīradevakṛtāyā paribhāṣāvṛttau ṅyāppādaḥ 
niranubandhakagrahaṇe na sānubandhakasya   
ekānubandhakagrahaṇe na dvyanubandhakasya   
tena sadavyayatavya iti ṣaṣṭhīsamāsaniṣedhe niranubhandhakasyaiva tavyasya grahaṇa na tavyataḥ 
tathā diva ut ityatra divdhātoruttva na bhavati 
akṣadyūriti 
yato nāva ityatraikānubandhakasya yato grahaṇa na dvyanubandhakasya ṇyataḥ 
jñāpaka cātra vāmadevāḍ ḍyaḍḍyau iti ḍyaḍyatorḍitvam tacca na karttavyam 
yasyeti ca iti lopenaiva vāmadevyasya siddhatvāt 
tatkṛtamanayorastitva jñāpayati 
taduktam 
siddha yasyetilopena kimartha yayatau ḍitau 
grahaṇa mā tadarthe bhūdvāmadevyasya nañsvara iti 
ke citpratyayaviṣayā niranubandhakaparibhāṣāmāhuḥ 
etattu jṛvraścyoḥ tkvi ityatrānunyāsakāreṇoktam 
 tathā na ca kavateryaṅi ityatra nyāsakāreṇa lugvikaraṇaparibhāṣayā''dādikasya kauteragrahaṇe siddhe kavateriti śtipā nirddeśastaudādikasya  
kuvartergrahaṇanirāsārtha iti yadukta tadupapadyate  
anyathā'ntarañgāyā niranubandhakaparibhāṣāyā viṣaye lugvikaraṇaparibhāṣā kathamabhidhīyate 
antaraṅgatva tu niranubandhakaparibhāṣāyā upadeśa eva itsajñāpravarttanāt
lumvikaraṇaparibhāṣāyāstu bahiraṅgatvamuktarakāla vikaraṇaluko vidhānāt 
gaṇapāṭhaviśeṣaparijñānācca 
anye tu sāmānyena niranubandhakaparibhāṣāmāhuḥ 
ata evāsterbhūrityatra śtipā nirddeśo vaicitryārtha ukto nyākṛtā na tvasu kṣepeṇa ityasya nirāsārtha iti 
tannirāsasya niranubandhakaparibhāṣayā siddhatvāt 
iya ca ekānubandhakaparibhāṣā vasoḥ saprasāranam ityatra nopatiṣṭhate 
vasurugitkaranasāmarthyāt 
tena vasugrahaṇe kvasuvasvorubhayorgrahaṇa bhavati 
nanu cāsati vasurugittve vasaḥ saprasāraṇamityucyamāne vasa ācchādana ityasya varmmavasaḥ paśyetyatrāpi saprasāraṇa prāpnoti 
naitat 
vasa ācchādana ityasya sānubandhakatvāt 
na ca vasa nivāsa ityasya niranubandhakasya grahaṇamāśaṅkanīyam 
tatra kvibāśrayasyaiva saprasāraṇasya siddhatvāt 
 nanu vasīrugittva vidvānivācaratīti kvibantāt tkvāpratyaye vidvasitvetyatrodito vā iti vikalpeneḍāgamārtha kasmānna bhavati pratyayanubandho  
hyeṣa samudāyānubandha eva  
ucyate 
anabhidhānāt kvibatra nāstīti na tadarthamugittvamiti videḥ śaturvasuḥ ityatra rakṣitaḥ 
bhāṣye tu vasorapi dvyanubandhakatvamuktam 
tathā ca videḥ śaturvasuḥ ityatra bhāṣyam 
vasuriti dvisakārako nirddeśa iti tatraikaḥ śrutyartho'parastu dvyanubandhakatvārtha iti 
anye tvāhuḥ 
anubandhasya sthānivadbhāvena vasurapi naikānubandha iti 
naitat 
sthānivadbhāvena hyanubandhakāryāṇāmatideśo nanubandhasyaiva 
syādetadekānubandhakagrahaṇe na dvyanubandhakasyeti pratiṣedhānna hyatra ki cidekānubandhakamastīti vasoḥ saprasāraṇam ityatra rakṣitaḥ 
 yadyeva yadvyākhyātamauṅa āpaḥ ityatra rakṣitena na hi sthānivadbhāvenānubandho bhavatyapi tu kārya sthanivadbhāvaśāstrasya sthānikāryārthatvādanubandhāśca  
kāryārthā na tu kāryāṇīti  
tadayuktam 
yatastatrāpi pūrvoktakrameṇa dvyanubandhakapratiṣedhādauṭsthānikasyauṅo grahaṇa na syāt 
etannyāyānusāreṇaiva gaṅkuṭādisūtre kai gai śabda ityasyaiva grahaṇa syādityavadhāraṇa yujyate 
tathā hīṇsthāniko yo gādeśaḥ sthānivadbhāvena sānubandhaka iti tasyāpyagrahaṇam 
na caiva vācyameva hi gāṅādeśaṅakāro na karttavyaḥ 
sthānivadbhāveneṇdhātoriveṅādeśagāśabdasyāpyagrahaṇāt 
yato'sati ṅakāre niranubandhakaparibhāṣāyā ihāvyāpāre pramāṇa na syāt 
 nanvasyā paribhāṣāyā satyāmutkarādibhyaśchaḥ naḍādīnā kuk ca iti naḍakīya ityādāveva niranubandhakatvādāyannādi sūtreṇeyādeśaḥ prāpnoti  
na tu chaṇādau sānubandhakatvāttauttirīyamiti  
ucyate 
āyannādi sūtre na pratyayagrahaṇamapi tu varṇagrahanam 
nanu naḍakīyādisiddhyartha naḍādīnā kuk ca ityanena kimartha chapratyaya kṛtvā kugāgamaḥ kriyate na naḍādibhyaḥ kuṭ cetyevocyeta 
eva hi naḍādibhya iti pañcamīnirddeśena lāghava bhavati 
takṣṇo nalopaśceti gaṇasūtra na karttavya bhavati 
padasajñayaiva lopasya siddhatvāt 
tathā ca tatra rakṣitaḥ 
parādau kuṭi kṛte takṣṇī nalopaśceti vacanamarthakam 
pratyayādestu vidhīyamāna īyādeśo na syāditi 
atrocyate 
nanu parādau kuṭi kṛte svādiṣu iti padasajñayā'vagrahaḥ prāpnoti 
yathoktamekādākiniccāsahāya ityatrākinici karttavya ākinico vidhānamavagrahanirāsārthamiti 
ucyate 
ayasmayādipāṭhāt bhasajñā manyate maitreyaḥ 
nanu ceda na chandaḥ 
ucyate 
tatra pāṭhabalādbhāṣāyāmapi bhasajñā bhaviṣyati 
ata eva ṭāṅasiṅasāminātsyā ityatra nādeśe karttavye inādeśavidhānamatijarasineti siddhyartha nyāse vyākhyātam 
nanu tathāpīyādeśo na syāditi katha yāvatā pratyayopadeśakāla ekyodeśena bhavitavyam 
naitat 
gṛhītāgamā evāgamina upajāyanta iti kakārāditva syāditi 
nanu yadīyādeśena na bhavitavyam 
tadā kuḍāgamamakṛtvā chapratyayameva kuryāt naḍādibhyaścha iti 
tasmākuṭyapi kṛte īyādeśena bhavitavyam 
ucyate 
evahi pratipattigaurava syāt   
tadanubandhakagrahaṇe nātadanubandhakasya   
sa evānubandho yasya sa tadanubandhakaḥ tasya grahaṇe'nyasya tacchūnyasya grahaṇa na bhavati 
tena caṅi iti cakārānubandhe dvirvacana kriyamāṇa tacchūnye'ṅi na bhavati 
adarśaditi 
anubandhoccāraṇasāmarthyalabdho'yamartha iti 
so'nubandho yasya tasya grahaṇe sa yatra nāsti tasya grahaṇa na bhavatītyaparo'syārtha ityāhuḥ 
tathā ca svādiṣvasarvanāmasthāne ityatrānayā prathamaikavacanagrahanamukta bhavati rakṣitena   
iti sīradevakṛtāyā paribhāṣāvṛttau raktapādaḥ 
svaravidhau vyañjanamavidyamānavat   
udāttādisvaravidhau vyañjanamavidyamānavat syāt 
tena tavyapratyayādestakārasyāvidyamanatvāt pratyayāderakārasyodāttatva bhavati 
karttavyamiti 
rājadṛṣadityatra halantatve'pi samāsasya ca ityantodāttatvam 
udaśvitvānityatra hrasvanuḍbhyā matup ityanena takāreṇa vyavadhānāddhrasvātparo matub na bhavatīti tasyodāttatva na bhavati 
anayā tu paribhāṣayā prāpnoti 
tatrāsyā lakṣyasthityā'nāśrayaṇena vṛttikṛtā samāhitam 
samāsasya ityatra tu bhāṣye'pyetaddoṣaparihārārtha halsvaraprāptāvityuktam 
atrocyate 
acaḥ svaravidhānāddhalsvaraprāptireva nāsti 
tatkimucyate halsvaraprāptāviti 
tatroktam 
uccairudātta ityādāvaca iti ṣaṣṭhīnirddiṣṭa nivṛttamiti 
codyañca yadatrāpadyate tattatraiva parihṛtamiti 
 jñāpaka cātrānudāttādeḥ ityasyāño bādhanārtha bilvādibhyo'ṇ iti vacana yadi vyañjana vidyamāna syāttadā bilvādayo'nudāttādayo na bhaveyuḥ 
anudāttasyājdharmatvāditi prāptireva nāsti 
mayaṭo bādhanārtha tu na vācyam 
mayaḍbādhanārthe hyasminbilvādibhyo'ṇ ityaṇgrahaṇamanarthaka syāt 
tasya hīda prayojanam 
pāṭaliputraśabdo'tra paṭhyate 
tasmādaṇ yathā syāt 
yathāprāptābhyanujñāne'nudāttādeśca ityañ mābhūditi 
añaśca halāditvādaprāptirityuktam 
imanijādīnāñca citkaranamasyā liṅgamupapadyate 
anyathemanico halantatvādetadantasya svarāprāpteścittvamanarthaka syāt 
udāharaṇāntara cāsyāḥ paurvārddhika dākṣiṇārddhikamityatra ṭhañi ñnityādinniratyam ityanena 
asyārthaḥ 
dikpūrva padādarddhaśabdāṭṭhañbhavati cakārādyacceti 
yadyeva pūrvapadagrahanamiha na kriyatā
diśaṣṭhañityeva vaktavyam 
aya cārthaḥ 
diśa uttarasmādarddhaśabdāṭṭhañ bhavatīti  na 
diśaṣṭhañityucyamāne diśaḥ svarūpagrahaṇa syāt pūrvapadagrahaṇe tu kṛte digityarthagrahaṇam 
tarhi pūrvagrahanameva kriyatām 
ata evārthagrahaṇa bhaviṣyati 
 yathā parāvarādhamottamapūrvācca ityatra parāvarādhamottamebhya iti karttavye pūrvagrahaṇa parārddhyamityatra ṭhaño bhādhanārthamiti vṛttāvuktam 
naitat 
padagrahaṇe sati pūrvagrahaṇādarthagrahaṇe vyavasthāpite bahupūrvārddhyamiti bahupūrvādarddhaśabdādapi ṭhañ syāt 
atrāpi dikpūrvasyārddhaśabdasya vidyamanatvāt 
na hi pūrvagrahaṇenārthagrahaṇa bahupūrvādibhyaḥ pratyayasya nirākaraṇa cobhaya śakyate karttum 
padagrahaṇe tu kṛte pūrvādiśabdebhya eva bhavati 
tatraiva diśaḥ pūrvapadasya vidyamānatvāt 
bahucpūrvādarddha śabdāttu na bhavati 
tasyāpūrvapadatvāt 
tasmātpūrvagrahaṇa padagrahaṇa cobhayamapi karttavyamiti 
eva ca sati dikpūrvapadāṭṭhañ ityatra yanmaitreyeṇoktam 
yathā pūrvasūtre pūrvagrahaṇasya prayojana vyākhyātam 
tathātrāsatyapi padagrahaṇe pūrvagrahaṇādeva svarūpagrahaṇannirastamiti tanna śobhanam   
yuṣmaṭpādaḥ samāptaḥ   
kriyāviśeṣaṇānā karmatva napusakaliṅgatā ca   
tadyathā 
mṛdu paṭhati 
śobhana pacati 
nanu kimartha napusakatva karmatva cobhayamāśrīyate 
na napusakatvamevāstu tata eva mṛdu pacatītyādi siddhyati 
satyam 
 ki tva sati karmatve mṛdvādīnā prathamāntatvāt sapūrvāyāḥ prathamāyā vibhāṣā ityanena grāme mṛdu te pacatītyādau vikalpena temayādividhayaḥ  
syuḥ  
dvitīyāntatve tu mṛdvādīnā temayādividhayo nityā bhavanti 
atha ki na bhavitavyameva grāme mṛdu te pacati grāme mṛdu tava pacatīti rūpadvayena
bhavitavyamevānanvādeśe
sarva eva vānnāvādayo'nanvādeśe vibhāṣā vaktavyā iti vacanāt 
 anvādeśe tvatho grāme mṛdu te pacatītyeva nitya bhavati tadyadi mṛdvādīnā prathamāntatva syāt tadā'nvādeśe'pi sapūrvāyāḥ prathamāyā vibhāṣā  
ityanena vikalpaḥ syāt  
yathā atho grāme kambalaste svam 
atho grāme kambalastava svamiti 
tasmāt karmatva napusakatva cobhaya karttavyam 
aya cārtho nyāsiddha ityāhuḥ 
tathāhi mṛdu pacatītyatra pākakriyāyāḥ prārthanādhyavasānādikriyayā vyāpyatvāt karmatvam 
tathāhi 
kaścitphalamīpsuḥ phala paśyati etasyā etatphalamiti dṛṣṭvā prārthayate tatastā karttumadhyavasyati 
gamyamanā ca kriyā kārakāṇā nimittamiti gamyamānāyāḥ prārthanādikriyāyāḥ pākakriyā karma bhavati
atastadviśeṣana karmaiva 
kriyāyāścāsattvabhūtatvāttadviśeṣaṇa sāmānyena liṅgena napusakenaiva nirddeṣṭu yujyata iti 
nanu kriyānimittasya karmmatvamukta nimitta ca siddhasvabhāvam 
kriyā ca sādhyasvabhāvā tatkatha karmatva syāt 
tarhi tatpratyanupūrvamīpalomakūlam iti kriyāviśeṣaṇakarmadvitīyāntāṭṭhāmvidhāna jñāpayati 
sādhyasvabhāvāpi kriyā prārthanādhyavasānādikriyā prati sādhanatvenāśrīyate   
iti paribhāṣāvṛttau ṭhakpādaḥ   
iti caturtho'dhyāyaḥ   
grahaṇavatā prātipadikena tadantavidhirnnāsti   
vyapadeśivadbhāvo'prātipadikena   
grahaṇavatyuccāravatā prātipadikena tadantavidhiḥ pratiṣiddhyate 
tena naḍādibhyaḥ phak iti kevalādeva bhavati 
nāḍāyana iti 
na tadantāt 
sautranāḍiriti 
vyapadeśivadbhāvaśca prātipadikena na bhavati 
kratūkthādisūtrāntāṭṭhak itīhaiva bhavati sagrahasūtramadhīte sāgrahasūtrikaḥ 
vyapadeśivadbhāvena kevalānna bhavati 
sūtramadhīte sautra iti 
jñāpite ete paribhāṣe yenavidhiḥ iti sūtre bhāṣyakṛtā 
pūrvādiniḥ ityasyānantara sapūrvācca ityanena 
taduktam 
kimartha sapūrvādinirvidhīyate 
pūrvaśabdena prātipadike viśeṣite tadantavidhinā sapūrvādapi bhaviṣyati 
kevalācca vyapadeśivadbhāveneti nārtho'nena tat kṛta jñāpanārtham 
etacca jñāpayati ete paribhāṣe grahaṇavatetyādike sta iti 
 ata eva pratyayavidhau jñāpitatvādgrahanavatetyādiparibhāṣādvaya pratyayavidhiviṣayamākhyāya gostriyorupasarjanasya ityatra tadantavidhinā  
gośabdāntagrahaṇa vyacakṣate  
anye ca sāmānyena pratyayavidhau cāpratyayavidhau ca paribhāṣāmāhuḥ 
tathā ca śeṣo ghyasakhi iti pratiṣedhaḥ kevala eva na tadante atisakherāgacchatīti 
punaścaitayorbhāṣye pratyākhyānamuktam 
taduktam 
ādyāyāstāvatsiddha viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāva prati yatheṣṭatvādviśeṣaṇena hi tadantavidhirbhavati na viśeṣyeṇa 
tatra samāsavidhau dvitīyāśrita ityādau yatsupsupeti prakṛta na tacchritādibhirviśeṣyate
api tu tenaiva śritādayo viśeṣyante śritādibhiḥ subantairiti
tena tadantavidhyabhāvānna bhavati kaṣṭa paramaśrita ityatra samāsaḥ 
 pratyayavidhau naḍādibhyaḥ phak ityatra yatprātipadikāditi prakṛta tenaiva naḍāḍhyo viśeṣyante naḍādibhyaḥ prātipadikebhya iti teneha na bhavati  
sūtranaḍasyāpatya sautranāḍiriti  
yatra tu gṛhyamāṇena prakṛta viśeṣyate tatra bhavatyeva tadantavidhiḥ 
yathopapada prakṛta bhayagrahaṇenāḍhyādibhiśca viśeṣyate 
atastadantavidhinā'bhayakaro'nāḍhya bhaviṣṇuriti
svagrahaṇānuvṛttyā vyapadeśivadbhāvācca kevale'pi bhavati bhayaṅkara ityāḍhyaṅkaraṇa iti ca 
kratṛvasthādisattrāntāṭṭhak ityatra tadantavidhinaiva tadantatve labdhe'ntagrahaṇa kevalānmābhūdityevamartham 
anyathā svamityasyānuvṛtyā kevalādapi syāt 
ata eva vyapadeśivadbhāvo na pravarttate 
 ki tveva gokulamityatra svagrahaṇānuvṛttyā vyapadeśivadbhāvāccopasarjanahrasvatva prāpnoti tatra tadantagrahaṇasāmarthyādvyapadeśivadbhāvo  
na bhavatīti bhāgavṛttikṛtā gostriyorupasarjanasya ityatra samāhitam  
svagrahaṇānuvṛttiśca na sarveṣā matā   
samāsapratyayavidhau tadantavidhiniṣedha ugidvarṇagrahaṇavarjam   
tena śritādīnā subantaviśeṣaṇatve'pi tadantavidherabhāvākaṣṭa paramaśrita ityatra samāso na bhavati 
tathā pratyayavidhau sautranāḍirityatra phagna bhavati 
ugidvarṇagrahaṇavarjamiti vacanāttaḍhantavidhinā'tibhavatīti dākṣiriti bhavati 
anyathā viṣṇuvācino'śabdātsyāt 
yenavidhi sūtre vārttikamida paribhāṣārūpeṇa kaiścitpadyate 
siddha tu viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvayoryatheṣṭatvāt   
itiparibhāṣāvṛttau dhānyapādaḥ samāptaḥ   
svārthikāḥ prakṛtito liṅgavacanānyativarttante'pi   
tena kuṭira ityatra liṅgātikramaḥ 
apkalpamityatra ca liṅgavacanayorubhayorapi 
pacatorūpa pacantirūpamityatra vacanātikramaḥ 
apiśabdānnāpyativarttante 
kutsitośvo'śvaka iti 
jñāpaka cātra ṇacaḥ striyāmañ ityatra striyāmiti vacanam 
liṅgānatikrame hi striyamiti na karttavyam 
karmavyatihāre ṇac striyām iti ṇacaḥ striyāmeva vidhānāt striyāmañapi siddha iti 
etasyā udāharaṇāntaram 
dvipadikā dviśatiketi pustvanapusakatvayoratikramaḥ 
atra hi dvaudvau pādau dadāti dvedve śate dadātīti pādaśatasya sakhyādervīpsāyā vun lopaśca iti vunpratyayo'ntyākāralopaśca 
atra codayanti 
nanu kimarthamanena vunvidhīyate kanneva vidhīyatām 
tenāpi hi dviśatiketi siddhyati 
eva ca sthūlādibhyaḥ prakāre kan iti kangrahaṇa karttavya na bhavati 
etadeva hyanuvarttiṣyate 
ucyate 
yadi kan vidhīyetāntyalope kṛte dviśatiketi na syāt 
tathā kani bhasajñābhāvāddvipadiketi bhasajñānibandhanaḥ pādaḥ pat iti padbhāvo na syāt 
athāstu padbhāvastathāpi dvipadiketi na syāt 
padbhāvasya halantatvād dvipatketi syāt 
eva ca yattatra rakṣitenoktam 
kanvidhāne'pi siddhyati dviśatiketi sthūlādibhyaḥ prakāre kan ityekatkarttavya na bhavati 
dvipadiketi tu bhasajñānimittapadādeśābhāvād rūpa ca na siddhyatīti tadayuktam
kanpratyaye'ntyalope ca kṛte dviśatiketyetadapi na siddhyati 
tatkathamucyate kanvidhāne'pi siddhyati dviśatiketi 
atha lopagrahaṇamapi na karttavya tarhi bhasajñānimittapadādeśābhāvād rūpa ca na siddhyatīti yadukta tadasaṅgata syāt 
tathāhi yathā bhasajñā nāsti tathā dakārāntaḥ pācchabdo'pi nāsti katha vā tadrūpañca na siddhyatītyucyate 
yāvatā'ntyalope kṛte padādeśe cābhyupagate satyantyo yo'kārastasyettve sati dvipadiketi siddhyatyeva 
ki cottaraphakkikāyā lopagrahaṇa pratyākhyātavyameva 
adhunā tatpratyākhyānamayuktam 
ucyate 
rūpa ca na siddhyatīti yadukta tadubhayatra veditavyam 
tato'yamarthaḥ 
dviśatiketi na siddhyati dvipadiketi ca na siddhyati 
anye tvāhuriha duravagamau maitreyābhiprāyaḥ 
na kevalamihaivāpi tvanyatrāpi 
tathāhi vibhaktipāde adhunā ityatra sūtre rakṣitenoktam 
yadyayamadhunā pratyayaḥ syāttadā pūrvasūtra evādhunā pratyaya vidadhyāt 
nādbhāvanipātanārthamida vaktavyam 
idama iś itīśādeśe kṛte yasyeti lope satyadhunetyasya siddhatvāt 
tasmādasāvanipātanārtha yatpṛthagyoga karoti tato'numīyate nāyamadhunāpratyayaḥ
tarhi dhunaiva 
sve ca viśeṣo vṛttikṛto'bhipretaḥ 
bhāṣye punaradhunāpratyaya evāya yasmādādisūtre kathitaḥ strī adhuneti pratyudāharaṇena
tathā tu yogavibhāgo'narthakaḥ asminkāle vastunīti vivakṣāyāmikoci iti nummābhūditi   
śatapādaḥ samāptaḥ   
iti pañcamo'dhyāyaḥ   
saprasāraṇa saprasāraṇāśraya ca kārya balīyo bhavati   
tena juhāvayiṣatītyatra hvaḥ saprasāranam iti śācchāsāhvāvyā iti yuka badhitvā saprasāranam 
juhūṣatītyatrābhyastasya iti dvirvacanātprāk saprasāraṇam
juhuvaturitya trākāralopa bādhitvā saparmāranapūrvarūpatve eva bhavataḥ 
tenāci śnudhātu ityādinovaṅ sidhyati 
anyathā''to lopa iṭi ca ityākāralope sati tasyāsiddhavadatrābhāt ityasiddhatvāduvaṅna syāt 
katha tarhi brahmaśabda upapade jināterddhātorāto'nupasarge ka iti ke kṛte brahmajya iti syāt 
yāvata'trāpi juhuvaturjuhavurityuvaṅādeśavadiyaṅā bhavitavyam 
na cātrairanekāco'sayogapūrvasya iti yaṇādeśo vācyaḥ 
aṅgasyakāctvāt 
tathā ca brahmajiya ityaniṣṭa rūpa syāt 
ucyate 
sarvatra saprasāraṇibhyo ḍo vaktavya iti ḍapratyayena bhavitavyamiti 
yathāhvaḥ prahva ityatroktam 
atha vā kva cideṣā na sarvatreti 
ata eva sahivahorodavarnasya ityatra nyāsakṛtoktam 
kva cideṣā na sarvatreti 
tena brahmajyaḥ āhvaḥ prahva iti kapratyaye saprasāraṇapūrvarūpa bādhitvā ikāralopastasyāsiddhatvādiyaṅuvaṅau na bhavataḥ 
tathā ceko yaṇaci iti kṛte siddha brahmajya ityādi 
jñāpaka cāsyā bhāṣye liṭyabhyāsasyobhayeṣām ityatrobhayeṣā vacanamuktam 
 taddhi vavraścetyādau halādiḥ śeṣaḥ bādhitvā saprasāraṇa yathā syādityevamartha kṛta tena kāryāntara bādhitvā saprasāraṇasya pravarttanādasyā  
astitva gamayati  
punaścāsyā bhāṣye pratyākhyānamuktam 
juhuvaturityādau pūrvavipratiṣedhena saprasāraṇasya saprasāraṇāśrayasya ca siddhiḥ 
 ki tu vyākhyānāt paribhāṣāśrayaṇameva laghviti nyāsakāreṇa punariya sahivahorodavarṇasya ityatrāvarṇagrahaṇena jñāpitā tasyaitat prayojanamūḍha  
ūḍhavānityatra saprasāraṇe pūrvarūpatve cokārasyautva mābhūditi  
etaccāprayojanam 
 dhatvaḍhatvaḍhalopesu saprasāraṇapūrvarūpatvābhyā paratvādakārasyautve kṛte saprasāraṇapūrvarūpatva ca kariṣyāma iti na ki cidaniṣṭamāpadyate 
tadevamavarṇagrahaṇamasyā jñāpakamiti 
atha juhūṣatītyatrādeśapratyayayoḥ iti katha mūrddhanyaḥ 
yāvatā sthānedvirvacanapakṣe hūso dvirvacane kṛte juhūsādeśasya śabdāntaratvāt prakṛtipratyayavibhāgo nāsti 
na ca mūrddhanyasyaiva dvirvacanam 
pūrvatrāsiddham ityasiddhatvāt 
pūrvatrāsiddhīyamadvirvacana iti tu prāyikam 
ubhau sābhyāsasya iti vacanāt 
ucyate 
tattvādhyavasāyena kāryakāraṇāt pratyayāśraya ṣatva bhavati 
tathaikāc sūtre rakṣitaḥ 
 tatrāya sādhāraṇaśca parihāraḥ sicprabhṛtīnā ṣopadeśasya sāmarthyāt stautiṇyoreva iti stautigrahaṇāt sico yaṅi iti pratiṣedhāccaiva jñāpyate  
śrutyabhedāttattvādhyavasāyena sthāne dvirvacane'pi kāryāṇi kriyante  
anyathā kaḥ prasaṅgaḥ ṣatvasya syāditi 
atrocyate 
nanu katha sico yaṅi ityasya jñāpakatvamuktam 
yāvatopasargāt sunīti ityādinā ṣatve prāpte tanniṣedhārtha tat syāt 
paritosicyata iti 
etacca sico yaṅi ityatra vṛttāvuktam 
 upasargāt sunoti iti yā prāptiḥ sā padādilakṣanameva ṣatvapratiṣedhamanantaratvād bādhate na sico yaṅi iti tasmādaya pratiṣedhaḥ sarvatreti 
ucyate 
sātpadādyoḥ iti pratiṣedhe prāpta upasargādi sūtreṇa ṣatva vidhīyate 
sātpadādyoḥ ityanena cādeśapratyayayoḥ ityasyaiva pratiṣedhaḥ 
ādeśapratyayayoḥ ityanena ca ṣatvasyāprāptiḥ 
sakārasyānādeśatvāt 
naitat 
sthite tathāvidho'syārthaḥ 
idānī punaraprāptamevopasargādi sūtreṇa ṣatva vidhāsyate 
atastatpratiṣedhārthameva sico yaṅi iti syāt 
na ca vācya sātpadādyoḥ ityādeśapratyayayoḥ ityasyāpavādaḥ 
tatsāhacaryātsico yaṅi ityapyādeśalakṣaṇaṣatvāpavādaḥ 
yata ubhayasambhave sāhacaryamucyate 
aya cādeśalakṣanaṣatvāpavādo na sambhavatītyanupapanna sāhacaryam 
ucyate 
 sthānedvirvacanapakṣe parisesicyata ityatrāpi yakāravataḥ sicyabhāgasya dvirvacane sesicyādeśasya sijvyapadeśābhāvātkathamupasargādi sūtreṇa  
sijdvārikā mūrddhanyasya prāptiryanniṣedhārtha sicoyaṅi iti syāt  
atha vā yadyatra sico'yaṅi iti kriyatām 
 aya cārthaḥ yaṅpratyaya varjayitvopasargāt sicaḥ ṣatvamiti tataḥ parisesicyata iti siddhe yatsico yaṅi iti kṛta tadādeśapratyayayoḥ ityasyāpi  
pratiṣedhārthamiti  
etasminpāde omāṅośca ityatra raksite pūrvapakṣo bahulapāde purastādapavādaparibhāṣāyāmuktaḥ   
ubhayata āśraye nāntādivat   
 ekaḥ pūrvaparayoḥ ityataḥ pūrvagrahaṇānuvṛtyā'ntādivacca ityanenaikādeśaḥ pūrvasya kārya pratyantavat parasya kārya pratyādivatkriyate tatra  
yathā śakyeta vidhiḥ karttumiti pūrvasyāntavattvenāmū ityatrādaso'serdādu do ma iti bhavati tathā parasyādivattvenāgnī vṛkṣāvityatra pragṛhyatve  
bhavataḥ  
yatra tvekādeśa ubhayamāśrayati pūrva para ca tatrobhayata āśraye nāntavattva nāpyādivattvamiti vākyārthaḥ 
tena vṛkṣamityatraikādeśasya pūrvagrahaṇenāgrahaṇānnaṅgasyākārāntatva paragaraṇenāgrahaṇānmakārasya na suptvamiti dīrghatvābhāvaḥ 
tathā prohyata ityatropasargāḍvrasva ūhateḥh iti na bhavati 
atreda na vaktavyam 
ekādeśasya pūrvagrahaṇena grahaṇe kṛte ekadeśavikṛtadvāreṇa makāramātrasya suptvamāśritya dīrghatvena bhavitavyamiti 
yadyatraikadeśaparibhāṣā syādubhayatāśrayaparibhāṣā nirviṣayā syāt 
iya ca paribhāṣāntādivacca ityatra bhāṣyakāreṇa paṭhitā 
tatrokto laukiko nyāyaḥ 
yathobhayostulyabalayorekaḥ preṣyo bhavati avirodhārthī ubhayorapi kāryena pravarttata iti   
varṇāśraye vidhau nāntādivattvam   
tena khaṭvābhirmālābhirityatra pūrva pratyantavattvābhāvādato bhisa es ityaisna bhavati 
taparakaraṇa tu somapābhirityatra kritārtham 
tathā hvayaterjuhāvetyatra saprasāraṇapūrvarūpasyānādivattvādāta au ṇala iti na bhavati 
tathā asyai aśvaḥ asyā aśva iti āṭaśca iti na vṛddhiḥ 
iya ca paribhāṣāntādivacca ityatra bhāṣye paṭhitā 
jñāpaka cāsyāḥ ṣatvatukorasiddha iti tugvidhāṣasiddhavacana kaiyaṭenoktam 
tathāhi 
yadyeṣā na syāttadādhītyetyatra savarṇadīrghasya paragrahaṇena grahaṇe kṛte hrasvāśrayastuk siddhastukyasiddhavacanamanarthaka syāt 
 nanvasyā satyā kṣīrapeṇetyatra pūrva pratyanantavattvenaikājuttarapadeṇa iti ṇatva na prāpnotyekājāśrayeṇa varṇāśrayatvāttatra pratiṣedha  
eva yuktaḥ  
śriyāmityatra para pratyādivattvābhāvādiyaṅna syāt 
yāveva pūrvaparau varṇāvāśrityaikādeśaḥ pravarttate tadvarṇāśraye'ntādivadbhāvo neṣyate 
atideśasya tatraiva vyāpārāttatraiva pratiṣedho yuktaḥ 
iha tvekādeśa eva kṛte yo varṇa ekājuttara ākāraśca tadāśrayau ṇatveyaṅvidhī na tau nivartyete 
tathā cāhuḥ 
ihādyantaśabdayoravayavavacanatvāttadavayavakaraṇe'syātideśasya vyāpāro na tu tatkaraṇa iti 
tadeva khaṭvābhirityādau pūrva pratyantavattve'pi tadekadeśatā labhyate na tu tadrūpateti tatkuta aisprasaṅga iti 
etadeva nyāsakṛtoktamatādrūpyo'yamatideśa iti   
ekācpādaḥ samāptaḥ   
kṛdgrahaṇe gatikārakapūrvasyāpi grahaṇam   
iya ca pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣāyā apavādaḥ 
yatra sajñayā svarūpeṇa vā kṛto grahana bhavati 
tatra gatikārakapūrvamapi gṛhyate na tu yataḥ pratyayastadādyeva 
tadyathā kṣepa iti ktāntena samāsaḥ sagatinā sakārakeṇa ca bhavati 
udakeviśīrṇamavataptekulasthitamiti 
aṇinuṇa itīnuṇantātsagateraṇ bhavati 
sārāviṇa iti 
jñāpaka cāsyā gatiranantara ityanantaragrahaṇam 
tena ktānta uttarapade pūrvasyānantarasya gatisvaro vidhīyate 
udbhatamavadhūtamiti na hi vyavahitasyābhyuddhūtamiti 
 tatra yadīya paribhāṣā na bhavet tadā pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣyaivoddhūtaśabde saghāte saktānte prāptireva nāstīti kimetannivṛttyarthenānantaragrahaṇena  
tatkṛta jñāpayatyastīya paribhāṣeti  
liṅgamātrañcedam 
kātyāyanabhāṣyakārābhyupagamādeva siddheyam 
anyathā kārakapūrvagrahaṇasya grahaṇe ki jñāpaka syāt 
 anayā paribhāṣayā kṛttaddhitasamāsāśca ityatrāpi kṛdgrahaṇe gatikārakapūrvasyāpi grahaṇa prāpnoti tatra yat samādhāna ca tadgatikārakopapadānā  
kṛdbhiḥ samāsavacanamityasyā paribhāṣāyāmuktam  
lakṣyavaśādiya na pravarttata ityapīti 
tena prajñāsukaraḥ kaṭa ityatra khityanavyayasya iti hrasvo'rurdviṣadajantasya iti ca mumna bhavati kūlamudraja itivat   
samāsānto vidhiranityaḥ   
tena bhuvāraṇyāśasādhṛtadhanuṣayāhūya tṛṇavaḍhityatra dhanuṣaśca ityanaṅna bhavati 
tathā bahvāmpi taḍāgānītyatra ṛkpūrabdhūḥ ityakāro na bhavati 
jñāpaka cāsyāḥ sphigapūtavīṇāñjodhvakukṣisīranāmanāma ca ityatrādhvagrahaṇam 
taddhyapācca ityato'pādityanuvṛttāvapāduttarasyādhvano'ntodāttatva yathā syāditi kriyate 
yadi ca nityaḥ samāsāntaḥ syāttadopasargādadhvana iti samāsānte'ci kṛte cittvādevāntodāttatva siddhamiti tatrādhvagrahaṇa na kuryāt 
kṛta cāto jñāpayatyastīya paribhāṣeti 
tathā bhāṣye dvitribhyā pāddanmūrddhasu bahuvrīhau ityatra sūtre'kritasamāsāntasya mūrddhaśabdasyopādāna liṅgam 
 nitye hi samāsānte yathā pāditi daditi ca pādasya lopo'hastyādibhya iti vayasi dantasya datṛ iti kṛtasamāsantau nirddiṣṭau tathā mūrddhaśabdo'pi  
dvitribhyā ṣa mūrddhna iti kṛtasamāsānto nirddiṣṭaḥ syāt  
tataśca mūrddheṣviti nirddeśaḥ syāttasmāttathā cākṛtasamāsāntanirddeśaḥ samāsāntavidheranityatva jñāpayati 
tena dvimūrddhā trimūrddhetyatrāpyudāttatva bhavati 
yataśca jñāpiteya paribhāṣā bhāṣye 
tato yaduktam 
yasmātpratyayavidhi sūtre bhāgavṛttikṛtā samāsānto vidhiranitya iti naiṣā paribhāṣā bhāṣye jñāpakābhāvāditi tadayuktam 
nanu lāghavārtha samāsāntanirdeśo na kṛto'nyathā mūrddheṣviti gaurava syāt 
yadyeva mūrddhapāddatsviti kuryāt 
eva ca samāsāntakramo na laṅghito bhavatīti jñāpitam   
bahuvrīhipādaḥ samāptaḥ   
sannipātalakṣaṇo vidhiranimitta tadvighātasya   
ānantaryalakṣaṇo vidhistadvighātasya nimittanna bhavati 
yasyānantaryeṇa yo vihitastadānantaryamasau na viruṇaddhītyarthaḥ 
tadyathā grāmaṇi brāhmaṇakulamityatra hrasvatve kṛte tugna bhavati 
naitatprayojanam 
asiddha bahiraṅgamantaraṅga ityanenaiva siddhatvāt 
vṛttau paddhatāvityatra tarhyacca gheḥ ityadādeśe kṛte ṭab mābhūditi prayojanam 
etadapi na adādeśasya taparatvāt 
tasyaitatprayojana vāmanenokta ṭāb mābhūditi 
ida tarhi prayojanam 
śatāni sahasrāṇīti vibhaktisanipātena numi kṛte tasya vibhaktiluka pratyanimittatvāt ṣṇāntā ṣaṭ iti ṣaṭsajñā na bhavati 
yadi syātṣaḍbhyo luk iti luksyāt 
tathā kumbhakārebhya ityatraitve kṛte kṛnmejanta iti na bhavati 
iya ca paribhāṣā kṛnmejanta ityatra bhāṣyakāreṇa paṭhitā 
jñāpakamasyā na tisṛcatasṛ iti dīrghapratiṣedhavacanam 
 taddhi satyāmasyā vibhaktinimittayostricaturoḥ striyā tisṛcatasṛ iti ṛkārāntaorvyavadhānakāriṇa ṅīpa pratyanimittatvāddīrghaprāptau pratiṣedhavacanamupapadyate 
anyathā tu ṅīpā vyavahitatvānnāmi dīrghatvāprāpteḥ pratiṣedhavacanamanarthaka syāt 
ṅīpaśca dīrghādīrghābhyāmaviśeṣāt 
anityā ceya kaṣṭāya kramaṇa iti nirddeśe'kārāntanimitte ṅerya iti ye kṛte yādau supi ca iti dīrghakaraṇādāhuḥ tena 
dākṣirityatra yasya iti lopaḥ siddhyati 
tathā yā sā ityatra ṭāppratyayaḥ 
nanu katha kaṣṭāya iti jñāpaka yāvatā'to dīrgho yañīti yakāreṇa pratyāhārasāmarthyāt 
kaṣṭāya ityatra supi ca ipi dīrghatva siddhyati 
ucyate 
 pvādīnā hrasva ityatrāgaṇāntāḥ pvādaya iti darśane jānātītyatra jñājanorjā iti jādeśe kṛte hrasvatva prāpnoti tanmābhūdityevamartha dīrghāntādeśavidhānamuktam 
anyathā yadi jānātītyatrapvādīnā hrasva iti hrasvatvena bhavitavyam 
tadā hrasvameva kriyāt jñājanorja iti 
nanu jayata ityatra dīrghaśrutyartha dīrghāntajādeśavidhāna syāt 
naitat 
jabhāve'pi kṛte'to dīrgho yañi iti dīrghatvamiti na śakyate vaktum 
yadi punarāgaṇāntāḥ pvādayo na bhavantīti darśanam 
tadā jānātītyatra pvādīnām iti nāsti 
aṅgavṛttaparibhāṣayā vā hrasvābhāvo'bhidhīyate kṛte vā hrasvatve tu punarato dīrgho yaṅi iti dīrghatvam 
tadā yakāreṇa pratyāhāragrahaṇasāmarthyād dīrghatva śakyata eva vaktumiti nānityatve jñāpakam 
anityatve tvetadeva jñāpakam 
nalopaḥ supsvarasajñātugvidhiṣu kṛti iti tuggrahaṇam 
yadīya nityā syāt tadā vṛtrahabhyāmityatrānayaiva tag na bhaviṣyatīti tuggrahanamanarthakam   
aninasmangrahaṇānyarthavatā cānarthakena ca tadantavidhi prayojayanti   
tenāllopo'na iti yathā sārthakasya bhavati rājño rājñeti 
tathā nirarthakasya dadhno dadhneti 
tathenhanpūṣāryamṇā śau iti 
yathā bahudaṇḍīni brāhmaṇakulānītyatra bhavati 
tathā bahuvāgmīnītyatrāpi syāt 
tathā'tvasantasya cādhātoḥ iti 
yathā supayā iti 
tathā nirgatastato nistatā ityatrāpi bhavati 
mana iti ṅīppratiṣedho yathā sudāmetyatra bhavati tathā suprathimetyatrāpi 
ida ca kātyāyanavacana paribhāṣārūpeṇa paṭhyate 
arthavatparibhāṣāyāścānityatvamasyā mūlam 
taccānityatvamaptrādi sūtre tṛntṛcorbhedenopādānādāhuḥ 
tṛntṛcorbhedenopādānamarvaṇastrasāvanaña ityarvādeśatṛśabdaparihārārtham 
yadi tvarthavarparibhāṣā nityā syāttardārthavatparibhāṣayaivārvādeśasya tṛśabdasya nirāse siddhe tṛntṛcormedenopādānamanarthakam 
kṛta ca tadanityatve jñāpakam 
nanu kimartharvādeśatṛśabdagrahaṇanirāsārtha tṛntṛcorbhedonopādānam 
yāvatāstu tasyāpi grahaṇam 
na caivamarvantāvarvanta ityatra dīrghatva syāt 
yato nityatvānnumi kṛte upadhāyā vihitatvāddīrthatva na bhaviṣyati 
ucyate 
vā ṣapūrvasya nigama ityataḥ pūrvagrahaṇānuvṛtternumaḥ prāg dīrghatvameva bhaviṣyatīti manyate 
etaccāvaśya vaktavyam 
anyathā bahvāmpi taḍāgānītyatrāpi numi kṛte dīrghatva na syāt 
anyastvāha tṛntṛcorbhedenopādāna sāmānye'pi nirddeśe kvacidviśeṣo gṛhyata iti jñāpanārtham 
tena na kopadhāyā ityatra sāmānyoktāvapi taddhitavusambadhyeva kakāro ghyate na kakāramātram 
tena kopadhapratiṣedhe taddhitavugrahaṇa karttavyamityetadvaktavya na bhavati 
etanmate paribhāṣāyā anityatve āniloṭ ityatra loḍgrahaṇa jñāpakam 
tathāhi pravayāni māsānītyatrānarthakalvādeva ṇatvābhāvaḥ siddha iti   
vārṇādāṅgambalīyaḥ   
varṇakāryādaṅgakārya balīyastvād bhavati 
tena bhavatītyatra yaṇādeśa bādhitvā guṇa eva bhavati 
paribhāṣā ceya saśeṣā samānāśraya iti
tena vyāśraye na pravarttate
tena siverauṇādike na pratyaye syona ityatra siuna iti sthite'ntaraṅgatvāllaghūpadhaguṇa bādhitvā yaṇeva bhavati 
atra cārthe cchoḥ śūḍanunāsike ca ityatra satukkasya chakārasyopādāna liṅgam 
 yadi vyāśraye'pi pravarttate tadā chakāranimitta varṇatuka bādhitvā viśna ityādāvanunāsikanimitta āṅgaśchakārasya śakāraḥ syāttatra kṛte  
nimittābhāvānnāsti tugiti ki satukkachakāropādāneneti  
na cāsiddhaparibhāṣayā tugāśaṅganīyaḥ 
tukaḥ pūrvameva bādhitatvāt 
nyāsakāreṇa tu sārvadhātukamapit ityatra vyāśraye'pīyamuktā
yadāha cyavante plavante ityatra vārṇādāṅga balīya ityekādeśāt prāgguṇa iti 
 tatrāsyāḥ kva cidvyāśraye'pi pravṛttirityatrārthe yajayācayatavicchapraccharakṣo naṅ ityatra naṅo ṅitkaraṇa guṇapratiṣedhārtha kriyamāṇa  
jñāpakam  
anyathā hi vicchestuki sati guṇaprasaṅga eva nāstīti naṅo ṅitkaraṇamanarthakasyāt 
jñāpitā ceya paribhāṣā'bhyāsasyāvarṇa ityatrāsavarṇagrahaṇena
taddhyevamartha kriyate
īṣaturīṣurūṣaturūṣurityatra savarṇe'cīyaṅuvaṅau mābhūtāmiti 
yadi ca vārṇādāṅgasya balīyastva na syāt 
tadā'ntaraṅgatvātkṛte savarṇadīrghatve iyaṅuvaṅoḥ prāptireva nāstīti kimasavarṇeneti tatkṛta jñāpayatyastīya paribhāṣeti 
atrocyate 
yadi savarṇe'cīyaṅuvaṅau na bhavatastadeyeṣovoṣetyatrāpīyaṅuvaṅau na prāpnutaḥ
yato'trāpyacaḥ parasminpūrvavidhau iti sthānivadbhāvādiyaṅuvaṅośca karttavyayoḥ savarṇasya parasyāco vidyamānatvamiti 
eva ca vidherabhāvādasavarṇagrahaṇamanarthakameva 
ucyate 
nātra sthānivadbhāvo'styādiṣṭādacaḥ pūrvatvādabhyāsasya 
tathāhi 
paratvādguṇe kṛte dvirvacane'ci iti sthānivadbhāvād dvirvacanam 
dvirvacane kṛte sthānivadbhāvavidhau dvirvacana evetyavadhāraṇādguṇaḥ pūrvarūpeṇā'vatiṣṭhate 
na punardvirvacanāduttarakāla punaḥ kriyate 
tenācaḥ parasmin itīyaṅuvaṅoḥ karttavyayoḥ sthānivadbhāvo na bhavati 
yadi hi syāttadārtterevābhyāsāsyeyaṅādeśo vidheya ityartterabhyāsastyetyeva brūyāt 
idamevāsavarṇagrahaṇa yohyanādiṣṭādacaḥ pūrvastasya vidhi prati sthānivadityasyāḥ paribhāṣāyā mūlam   
yo hyanādiṣṭādacaḥ purvastasya vidhi prati sthānivat   
yo hyacaḥ parasmin iti sthānivadbhāvaḥ so'nādiṣṭādacaḥ pūrvasya kārye bhavati 
tena paṭayatītyatra ṭāśabdākārādanādiṣṭādacaḥ pūrvo yaḥ paśabdākārastasyā'ta upadhāyā iti vṛddhi prati lopaḥ sthānivadbhavati 
ādiṣṭādacaḥ pūrvasya kārye tu na sthānivattva yathā vaiyākaraṇaḥ sauvaśva iti 
tenaico'yavāyāva iti na bhavati 
atra hyacaḥ pūrvayorecoḥ sambhavo nāsti yakāravakārābhyā pūrvayoraicorvidhānāt 
nyāsakṛtā tvatrāsiddha bahiraṅgamantaraṅga ityanena samāhitam 
tanmatenācīkaradītyudāhāryam 
ādiṣṭādacaḥ pūrvasya kva cit sthānivattvamupeyivānitīḍarthanipātanātpratīyate 
yadi hyādiṣṭādacaḥ pūrvasya kārye sthānivattva na syāttarhīḍarthanipātana vṛttikṛtoktamayukta syāt 
 tathāhīṇ dvirvacane kṛte dīrgha iṇaḥ kiti iti dīrghatve kṛte tataḥ savarṇadīrghatvenaikāctvādeva vasvekājādghamām itīḍāgamaḥ siddhaḥ syādupeyivānityatra 
na ca vācya dīrgha īṇaḥ kiti iti dīrghavidhānasāmarthyātsavarṇadīrghatvena na bhavitavyam 
īyaturīyurityatra yaṇādeśe caritārthatvāt 
na ca sthānivadbhāvāddīrghatvaprāptiḥ 
ādiṣṭādacaḥ purvatvād dvirvacanasya 
yata evādiṣṭādacaḥ pūrvasya kva citkārye sthānivattva pravarttate'ta eva savarṇavidhi prati na sthānivaditi pratiṣedha upapadyate 
śiṇḍhi piṇḍhīti 
 tathā yadvakṣyatyupadhāyā ca ityatra dīrghavidhau riryatū riryurityatra sthānivattvapravṛttyā yaṇādeśa kṛtvā dvirvacane kṛte'caḥ parasmin  
iti sthānivadbhāvānna dīrgha iti tadupapadyate  
aya cārthoaḥ parasminpūrvavidhāvityasyārthaḥ paribhāṣārūpeṇa paṭhyate 
tatrājapekṣamādeśāpekṣa nimittāpekṣa vā pūrvatvamāśrīyata ityuktam 
tatra yadā'japekṣa pūrvatva tadā'yamarthaḥ 
ajādeśaḥ paranimittakaḥ pūrvasya vidhau sthānivat kutaḥ pūrvasya vidhau sthānivattvamacaḥ 
tadevamajaprekṣapūrvatvamasyā mūlam 
jñāpaka cāhuḥ 
abhyāsasyāvarṇa ityatrāsavarṇagrahaṇam 
atsmṛdṛtvaraprathamradastṝspaśām iti vacana vā 
tena hi sanvadbhāvabādhanārthamad vidhīyate 
yadi cādiṣṭādapyacaḥ pūrvatra kārye sthānivattva syāttadā'ttvamapi naiva kuryāt   
prakṛtigrahaṇe yaṅlugantasyāpi grahaṇam   
tena vido laṭo vā iti ṇalādyādeśavikalpo yaṅlugantasyāpi bhavati
