nyāyasiddhatvamasyā niṣṭhā śīṅādi sūtre nyāsakṛtā darśitam 
tathāhi 
sthānedvirvacanapakṣe sthānivadbhāvātprakṛtivyapadeśaḥ 
dviḥ prayoge ca sa eva dvirāvarttyata iti yukta prakṛtigrahaṇe yaṅlugantasyāpi grahaṇamiti 
jñāpakamapyāhuḥ 
ūdupadhāyā goha ityatropadhāgrahaṇam 
ūdorgoha iti lāghavārtha vaktavye yadupadhāgrahaṇa karoti tadyaṅluki jogṛhatītyatra yo'bhāsasyaukārastasya mābhūdityevamartha kriyate 
etacca tadā syāt 
yadi prakṛtigrahaṇe yaṅlugantasyāpi grahaṇa bhavatīti 
nanu cottarārthamupadhāgrahaṇa gamahanajanakhanaghasām iti 
anyathā'lontyasya lopaḥ syāt 
ucyate 
jñāpakavādino mate tatrāta iti nīstha prtipādayitavyaḥ 
śtipā nirddeśe caiṣā nopatiṣṭhate 
tathā ca smṛtiḥ 
śtipā śapā'nubandhena nirddiṣṭa yadgaṇena ca 
yaccaikājgrahaṇa tatra pañcaitāni na yaṅluki śtipā nirddeśa indhibhavatibhyā ca iti 
śapā bharajñapisanām ityatra bhara iti 
anubandhena śīṅo ruṭ iti 
gaṇena vatatitanotyādīnām iti 
ekājgrahaṇena ekāca upadeśe'nudāttāt iti 
śryukaḥ kiti itīṭpratiṣedhaḥ 
atra śloke ki ciditi śeṣaḥ 
yatrakājgrahaṇena dhāturviśeṣyate tatparigrahaṇārtham 
yatra tu dhātvavayavasya nirddeśo yathaikāco dve prathamasya ityatraikājgrahaṇa yaṅluṅnivṛttyartha na bhavati 
tena yaṅluki dvirvacanena bobhavatīti siddhyatīti yathākathañcidāhuḥ 
nanu bhavatītyatrākartṛvācini sārvadhātuke śtipi katha śabutpadyate 
ucyate 
śtipaḥ śittvādakartṛvācinyapi śap 
naitat 
śittvasyādeca upadeśe'śiti ityāttvapratiṣedhe caritārthatvāt 
roditirityatra rudādibhyaḥ sārvadhātuka itīḍarthatvācca 
kiñcāsati śittva ārddhadhātukatvāt śtipīṭ syāt 
atha titutratatha iti pratiṣedhādiḍabhāvaḥ 
evamapyārddhadhātukatvāsmeraniṭi iti ṇerlopaḥ syādeva 
eva tarhi indhibhavatibhyā ca iti nirdeśādeva śap 
katha tarhīkśtipau dhātunirddeśe vaktavyāviti vyācakṣāṇena nyāsakṛtokta śitkaraṇasāmarthyācchabiti 
ucyate 
śitaḥ karaṇa yasyeti bahuvrīhiṇā śitkaraṇaśabdena bhavatinirddeśa evocyate 
tadayamarthaḥ 
bhavatīti nirddeśakaraṇasāmarthyācchabiti 
anyastvāha 
śtipi dvau śakārāvanubandhau laśakvataddhite ityatropadeśānadhikārāditsañjñā 
etaccānunyāsakṛnmatamekayoganirddiṣṭaparibhāṣāyāmuktam 
tadeva dvitīyaśitkaraṇasāmarthyācchap   
asiddha bahiraṅgamantaraṅge   
antaranṅge kārye karttavye bahiraṅgamasiddha bhavati 
tena pacāvedamityādau bahiraṅgasyādguṇasyāsiddhatvādeta aina bhavati 
grāmaṇi brāhmaṇakulamityatra hrasvasya piti kṛti iti na tuk 
nārkuṭo nārpatyamityatra kharavasānayoḥ iti na bhavati 
rājanyatretyatra sayogāntalopo na bhavati 
jñāpaka cātra vāha ūṭh ityūṭho vidhānam 
tatra hyucyate 
prakṛta samprasāraṇameva vakārasya vidhīyatā tataḥ pūrvarūpatvam 
tato ṇvipratyayasya pratyayalakṣaṇenokārasyaukāro guṇastato vṛddhirecīti vṛddhyā siddha praṣṭhauheti 
anakārānte copapade chandasi vaherṇvirnna dṛśyate 
tatkimūṭho vidhānena tat kṛta jñāpayatyastīya paribhāṣeti 
 bahiraṅga samprasāraṇa bhasañjñānimittapratyaye vidhānāttatrāntaraṅge'bhyantaraṅge pratyayāśraye guṇe karttavye bahiraṅgasya samprasāraṇasyāsiddhatvādukāro  
nāstīti katha guṇaḥ syāditi  
anityā ceya paribhāṣā 
taccānityatva nalopaḥ supsvara iti tugvidhau nalopasyāsiddhatvena jñāpitam 
tathāhi 
yadīya nityā syāt 
tadā'nayaiva vṛtrahabhyāmityatrāntaraṅge tuki karttavye bahiraṅgasya nalopasyāsiddhatva siddhamevetyanityatve jñāpakam 
nanu siddhe punaryadasiddhavacana tanniyamārtha syāt 
kṛtpratyayalakṣaṇe tukyevāsiddha na chalakṣaṇa iti 
tena vṛtrahacchatramityatra tuki karttavye'siddha bahiraṅgamantaraṅga iti na pravarttate 
na ca vidhiniyamasambhave vidhireva jyāyānityasti
niyamajñāpakayorarthadvayāpekṣitvena tulyatvāt 
ucyate 
vṛtrahacchatramityatra nalopo na bahiraṅgo'pi tu tugeva tuko dvipadāśrayatvāt 
vṛtrahabhyāmityatra tu vibhaktimāśritya nalopa iti tatra tasya bahiraṅgatvam 
anityatve cāmū ityatraikādeśasya bahiraṅgasyāntaraṅge utve matve ca karttavye'siddhatvanna bhavati 
tathā papuṣaḥ paśyetyatra samprasāraṇasyāsiddhatvādvalakṣaṇo vasvekājādbhasām itīṇ na bhavati 
atra cāsyāḥ pravarttanābhāva upāyāntaramakṛtavyūhā ityatroktam   
nājānantarye bahiṣṭvapraklṛtptiḥ   
pūrvāpavādo'ya yogaḥ 
acorānantarye bahiraṅgaparibhāṣā nāsti 
tena bahava ityādāveco'yavāyāva iti bhavati 
tathā'kṣadyūrityatreko yaṇaci iti 
yūno maghona ityatrākaḥ savarṇādguṇau 
yadyeva pacāvedamityatrāpyeta aiprāpnoti 
atrāpyacorānantarye bahiraṅgasyādguṇasya pravṛttatvād siddha bahiraṅgamantaraṅga ityasyāḥ pratiṣedho yuktaḥ 
naitat 
acorānantarye sati yatrobhayamantaraṅga bahiraṅgañca tatreya pratiṣidhyate yathā bahavo'kṣadyūriti 
tathāhyatra bahiraṅge pravṛtte vidyamāna eva guṇa ūṭhi vāntaraṅgāvayaṇādeśau karttavyatayā vidyete 
pacāvedamityatra bahiraṅga ekādeśe kṛte'corānantarya nivṛttamityacorānantarye dvaya na vidyate 
tatkathamasyāḥ pratiṣedhaḥ 
yadyevamadhītya pretyetyatrāpyekādeśe kṛte'corānantarye dvayannāsti katha tadā ṣatvatukorasiddha ityasya jñāpakatopapattiḥ 
tathāhyatra pūrva dhāturupasargeṇa yujyata ityatra darśane dīrghāduttarakālamantaraṅge tuki karttavye'corānantaryannasti 
eva tarhi pūrva dhātuḥ sādhanena yujyata ityasmin darśane'dhītya pretyetyatra nājānantarya ityucyate 
etaddarśane hyekādeśāt prāg lyapi kṛte'corānantarye'ntaraṅga bahiraṅga ca iya vidyata eva 
na cāsmin darśane'ntaraṅgatvāttuki kṛte ṣatvatukorasiddha ityasyānarthakyam 
yathāntaraṅgatva tukastathā nityatva dīrghasya
tadetayornnityāntaraṅgayoḥ paratvāddīrghatva syāt 
atha vā pūrva dhāturupasargeṇa yujyate ityatrāpyakṛtavyūhā iti pravibhajyānvākhyāne'corānantaryamasti 
ki ca ṣatvatukīrasiddha ityatra dhātostannimittasyaiva ityatra nyāsakṛtā vyākhyātam 
sahitādhikārīye kārye karttavye'siddha bahiraṅgamantaraṅga iti nājānantarya ityanayā bādhyate 
eta ai itīda prakaraṇāntaravihita kāryamiti kutastatra karttavye pratiṣedhe ucyate 
etadeva cchvoḥ śūḍanunāsike ca ityatra maitreyeṇoktam 
acorānantarye yattad dvaya prāpnotyantaraṅga bahiraṅga ca tatreya pratiṣidhyate
iha tu kṛta eva bahiraṅge'corānantarye ca nivṛtte'ntaraṅga prāpnotīti kutastasyāḥ pratiṣedha ityādinā granthena 
asyāyamarthaḥ 
astītyadhyāhāryam 
tadayamarthaḥ 
 acorānantarye yatra dvayamasti bahiraṅga pravṛttamantaraṅga prāpnotyantaraṅga pravṛtta bahiraṅga vā tatra bahiraṅgaparibhāṣā pratiṣidhyata  
iti  
jñāpaka cātra ṣatvatukorasiddha iti tukyekādeśasyāsiddhavacanam 
 yadyacorānantarye'pi bahiraṅgasyāsiddhatva syāttadādhītyetyādāvantaraṅge tuki karttavye padadvayāśritasya savarṇadīrghasyāsiddha bahiraṅgamantaraṅga  
ityata evāsiddhatvādasiddhavacanamanarthaka syāt 
anayā cāntaraṅgaparibhāṣā na bādhyata ityantaraṅgaparibhāṣāmuktam   
sajñāpūrvako vidhiranityaḥ   
tena dhāma svāyambhuva yayurityatraurguṇa ityasyābhāvāduvaṅ siddhyati 
tathā jyogiṣamityatrāṇyādivṛddhirna bhavati 
pañcabāṇaḥ kṣiṇotītyatra na guṇaḥ 
udaśvitvānityatra śvayateḥ kvipi na samprasāraṇam 
jñāpaka cātra oroditi karttavye orguṇa iti guṇagrahaṇam
tathoto vṛddhirluki hali ityatra auditi karttavye vṛddhigrahaṇam 
tena stuyādityatra vṛddhirna bhavati 
 eva ca kṅiti ca ityatrācinavamasunavamitisiddhyartha vṛttau yadukta yāsuṭo ṅidvacana jñāpaka lakārāśraya ṅittvamādeśānā na bhavatīti  
tadupapadyate  
anyathā yāsuṭo ṅidvacana stuyādityatrāniglakṣaṇavṛddhipratiṣedhārtha syāttatkuto jñāpakam 
nanu tathāpyasya jñāpakatvamayukta vinuyurityādau jusi ca iti pratiṣedhārthatvāt 
etaccāyuktam 
yataḥ satyapi ṅittve bhavitavyamevātra jusi ca iti guṇena
kṅidviṣaya eva tasyārambhāt  na 
yena nāprāptinyāyena sārvadhātukamapit ityanena yan ṅittva tadevānena bādhyate 
na yāsuḍāśritamapi 
ucyate 
yadyetāvatprayojana syāt 
skasyāci ityato'cītyanuvarttyājādau jusi guṇo vidheya iti 
yāsuṭo ṅittva jñāpakameva 
apiḥ padārthasambhāvanā ityatra stuyādityatra ṅicca pinna bhavatīti vacanādrakṣitena vṛddhyabho vyākhyātaḥ 
stuyādityakṛtsārvadhātukayoḥ iti na dīrghaḥ 
sārvadhātukayakāratvāt 
nanu cācinavamityādisiddhyartha jñāpakamabhidhīyate 
yāvatā picca ṅinna bhavatyanena ṅittvābhāvādguṇaḥ siddha eva 
ucyate 
bhāṣyamatamida na sūtrakṛtaḥ 
ata eva serhyapicca ityatra nyāsa uktam 
serhiṅiditi kriyamāṇe sthānivadbhāvena pittva syāditi 
anyathā tatrāpi ṅicca pinna bhavatīti kaḥ prasaṅgaḥ pittvasya syāditi 
nanu yadi sūtrakārasyānapekṣitamida ṅicca pinna bhavatīti tathā brūtādbhavānityatra pittvasya sthānivadbhāvād bruva īṭ itīṭ syāt 
ucyate 
satyapi sambhave bādhana bhavatīti tātaṅo ṅittvena tipaḥ pittva bādhanīyam 
eva bhindyādityatrāpi tipaḥ pittvena liṅo ṅittvasya bādhitatvāt   
sanniyogaśiṣṭānāmanyatarāpāye ubyorapyapāyaḥ   
tadyathā 
 dhīvarītyādau ṅīpsanniyogaśiṣṭo vano ra ca iti rephādeśaḥ pañcadhīvetyādau pañcabhirddhīvarībhiḥ krītetyārhīyasya ṭhako'dhyarddhadvigorlugasajñāyām  
iti luki kṛte luktaddhitaluki iti ṅīpo nivṛttau rephasyāpi nivṛttiḥ  
ayāḥ paribhāṣāyāśchedādibhyo nityam ityatra bhāṣyakāreṇa nyāyasiddhatvamuktam 
taduktam 
laukika evāya nyāyaḥ sanniyogaśiṣṭānāmanyatarāpāye ubhayorapyapāyaḥ 
tadyathā devadattayajñadattābhyāmida karttavyamityukte devadattāpāye yajñadatto'pi na karotīti 
jñāpakamapyasyā bhāṣyakāreṇabilvakādibhyaśchasya luk ityatra vyākhyātam 
tatra hyukta vilvakādibhya iti kukā nirddeśaḥ
 kuk cā'ya naḍādīnā kukca iti chapratyayasaniyuktastaśca bilvādibhyaḥ paraścha eva sambhavatīti bilvakādibhyo lugityucyamāne bhasañjñānimittapratyaye  
chasyaiva lugbhaviṣyati ki chagrahaṇena tatkṛta chasyaiva kevalasya lugyathā syāt  
anyathā sanniyogaparibhāṣayā kuko'pi nivṛttiḥ syādityevarmartham 
eva cāsyāḥ paribhāṣāyā astitve jñāpakam 
atrocyate 
nanu yadi bilvakādibhyo lugityucyate sāmānyena pratyayamātrasya luksyāt 
tathā ca bilvakādityatra supo'pi luk syāt 
ucyate 
halastaddhitasya ityasmāttaddhitagrahaṇānuvṛtterna bhaviṣyati 
nanvevamapi bilvakasyāvayavo vikāro vā bailvaka ityatra kopadhācca ityasyāṇo luk prāpnoti 
eva tarhyāpatyasya ca taddhite'nāti ityatastaddhita ityanuvṛttestaddhitasya bhasajñasya taddhite parato luk 
evamapi bilvake bhavī bailvako vailvakasyeda bailvakīyamityatra prāpnoti 
naitat 
bilvakādibhyo yo vihitastasmin lugucyate 
na cātra bilvakāccho vihito'pi tu bailvakāditi 
anityā ceyam 
taccānityatva bhyasyāḍhe taddhita ityaḍha iti puvadbhāvapratiṣedhena jñāpitam 
tatra hyaḍha iti kimityutkvā śyaineyo rauhiṇeya iti prtyudāhṛtam 
yadi ceya nityā syāt 
tadā yasyeti ca iti lope kṛte sanniyogaparibhāṣayā nakārasyā'pi nivṛttiḥ syāt 
tataśca puvadbhāve'viśeṣādaḍha iti pratiṣedho'narthakaḥ syāt 
nanu kathamanarthako yāvatā lope satyacaḥ parasmin iti sthānivadbhāvena pratyayalakṣaṇenāsiddha paribhāṣayā vā ṅīsanniyogo vidyata eva 
eva ca sati sanniyogaparibhāṣāyā anupasthānānnakārādeśo na nivarttate 
ucyate 
sthānivadbhāvādinā kārya kriyate 
na tu luptavarṇasannidhāna na caiva sanniyogaparibhāṣāyā anupasthānam 
apāyamātre tatpravarttanāt 
jñāpakamapyasyāstādṛśameva 
anyathā chasya lukyapi kṛte kuko nivṛttirna prāpnoti pratyayalakṣaṇādinā tasya vidyamānatvāt   
tācchīlike ṇe'pyaṇkṛta kārya bhavati   
aṇā kṛta kāryamaṇkṛtam 
taṇapratyaye'pi bhavati tena cūrā śīlamasyā iti chatrāditvāṇapratyayāntādapi ṅībhavati 
caurī tāpasī 
tācchīlike iti kim 
śīlikāmibhikṣyācaribhyo ṇo vaktavyaḥ 
māsaśīlā māsabhikṣā 
prajñāśraddhārcāvṛttibhyo'ṇaḥ prājñā brāhmaṇīti 
atrāṇkṛta ṅīb na bhavati 
kārmastāchīlya ityatra jñāpiteyam 
tatra karmaśabdāttacchīlamityanuvarttamāne chatrāditvāṇapratyaye kārma iti nipātyate 
atrocyate 
tastaddhita iti ṭilopena kārma iti siddhe ṭilopārtha nipātanamayuktam 
na cānniti prakṛtibhāvo'sti
aṇi tasya vidhānāt 
eva tarhyetaj jñāpayatyastīya paribhāṣeti 
atrocyate 
yadi tācchīlike'pyaṇkṛta kārya bhavatīti kimartha tarhi tācchīlike'ṣvaṇpratyaya eva na vidhīyate 
eva ca jñāpaka karttavya na bhavati 
ucyate 
vaicitryārtha na kṛtam   
dhātoḥ kāryamucyamāna tatpratyaya eva bhavati   
dhātoryatkāryamucyate taddhātupratyaya eva bhavati 
tena sṛjidṛśorjhalyamakiti ityam rajjusṛgbhyāmityatra kvibantānā satyapi dhātutve supi prātipadikapratyaye na bhavati 
tathā'ci vibhāṣā iti girau gira ityatra na bhavati 
tathodakamagbhyā prāṇanagbhyāmityatra masjinaśorjhali iti num 
yadyeva yathā prāṇanagbhyāmityatra na num 
tathā naśervā iti naśadhātvāśrita kutvamapi pakṣe na syāt 
ucyate 
padasya kutvavidhānānna dhātupratyayāśrita kutva numāgamastu dhātupratyayāśrita eva 
imāmeva paribhāṣāmavalambyopayaṭkāmyatītyatra kāmyacaḥ kakārasyānitsajñā 
śriyau śriyo bhruvau bhruva ityādau prātipadikapratyayepīyaṅuvaṅau bhavataḥ 
oḥ supi iti varṣābhvaśca iti sūtrārambhāt 
parivyavebhyaḥ kriyaḥ bhuvaḥ prabhava iti nirddeśācca 
vārttikakārāstvanyādṛśī paribhāṣā paṭhanti 
dhātoḥ svarūpagrahaṇe tatpratyaya eva kāryavijñānamiti 
atra hi pāṭhe dṛgbhyā dṛgbhirityatrānudāttasya cardupadhasyānyatarasyām ityatrāsvarūpadhātugrahaṇāt supyapyamāgamaḥ syāt

tathāhi yadyeṣā na syāt tadā hanasto'ciṇaloḥ iti ṣyañi tatva siddhamiti nipātanamanarthaka syāt

nipātanamida kutvābhāvārtha syāt

na kvādeḥ iti yogavibhāgena kutva bhaviṣyati

abādhakānyapi nipātanāni bhavanti   
tena purāṇaprokteṣu iti nipātanasya nityamabādhakatvāt sāyaciraprāhṇepragevyayebhyaṣṭyuṭyulau tuṭ ca iti ṭyuṭyulau tuḍāgamo'pibhavati

jñāpaka cātra trayāṇāmiti siddhaye trestraya iti sūtram 
yadi hi bādhakānyeva nipātanāni syustadā nijāntrayāṇām iti siddha syāt 
yadā tvabādhakānyapi nipātanāni bhavanti tadā trīṇāmiti prayoganivṛttyartha trestraya iti sūtramarthavadbhavati 
anye tvāhuḥ 
neya paribhāṣā nāpi bhāṣyakāravacanam 
bādhakānyeva nipātanānīti sarvādīni ityādisūtre vyākhyātam 
ata eva tatraiva sūtre bhāgavṛttiḥ purātanamunermunitāmiti 
purātanīrnnadīriti ca pramādapāṭhāvetau gatānugatikatayā kavayaḥ prayuñjate na teṣā lakṣaṇa cakṣuriti   
aṅgādhikāre tasya taduttarapadasya ca   
tenāsthidadhītyādiā priyāsthnā priyadadhnetya trāpyanaṅ bhavati grahaṇavatā prātipadikenetyasyāyamapavādaḥ 
jñāpaka cātra yujerasamāsa ityatrāsamāsagrahaṇam 
 taddhyaśvayugityatra nummābhūdityevamartha kriyate yadi cāṅgādhikāre taduttarapadasyāpi kārya na bhavati tadā yujernnumyaśvayuji kaḥ prasaṅgo  
yanniṣedhārthamasamāsagrahaṇa syāditi    
pratyeka vākyaparisamāptiḥ   
iha śāstre pratyeka vākyāni parisamāpyante 
yathā vṛddhisajñā pratyekamādaicām 
guṇasajñā cādeṅām 
laukika evāya nyāya ubhe abhyastam ityatra bhāṣyakāreṇa vyākhyātaḥ 
taduktam 
devadattayajñadattaviṣṇumitrā bhojyantāmityukte na punarucyate pratyekamiti
atha ca pratyeka bhojyanta iti 
atra śabdaśaktireva pramāṇam 
jñāpakamapyatra ṇaluttama ityatrottamagrahaṇa ṇalo viśeṣaṇam 
yadi hi pratyeka vākyasambandho na syāttadottamagrahaṇamiḍvasmasā trikeṇa sambaddhamiti ṇalaḥ kevalasya viśeṣaṇa na syāt   
kva cit samudāye vākyaparisamāptiḥ   
yathā halo'nantarāḥ sayoga iti sayogasajñāvidhānam 
etadartha sayoga iti mahatī sajñā kṛteti nyāsakṛtoktam 
laukika evāya nyāyo vṛddhirādaijityatra bhāṣye darśitaḥ 
gargāḥ śata daṇḍyantāmiti samudāyenārthino rājānohiraṇyena bhavantīti 
na cātra pratyeka daṇḍayanti 
atrāpi śabdaśaktireva pramāṇam 
ke cidatra yuktimāhuḥ 
śatamatra pradhāna karma gargāstu guṇakarma tadaṅgatvāt 
guṇabhede ca pradhānabhedo na yuktaḥ 
jñāpakamapyāhuḥ 
prathayoḥ pūrvasavarṇa ityatra prathamādvitīyayorvvacanaṣaṭkayoḥ prayukta prathamayoriti padam 
prathamāśabdo hi yadi supā trikasya svaujasiti samudāyasya sañjñā syāt 
sāmīpyāccāmauṭśasiti trikeṣu prayujyate tadā prathamayoriti nirddeśaḥ sādhīyān bhavati 
 yadi tu pratyeka prathamāśabdaḥ syāttadā sorekavacanasya prathamāśabdena grahaṇa syāt sāmīpyāccāma iti lāghavārtha svamorityeva kuryāt 
tasmātprathamayoḥ iti nirddeśena samudāyena vākye parisamāpti bodhayati 
yatheṣṭa ca pakṣayorāśrayaṇam 
ke cittu yathā vākyaparisamāptirityāhuḥ 
yathā gargaiḥ saha na bhoktavyamiti pratyeka na bhujyate samuditaiśceti 
 tena svādividhivākyasya bahuṣu bahuvacanam ityādinā karmaṇi dvitīyā ityādinā ca śāstreṇaikavākyatāpattau tatra tatrābhidhīyamānāvupayujyate  
iti    
abhedakā iha śāstre guṇāḥ   
tena vṛddhirādaic ityudāttasvaritānāmādaicā vṛddhisañjñāsiddhiḥ 
loke guṇānā bhedakatvamabhedakatva ca 
yathaikamudakamida śītamidamuṣṇamiti guṇabhedādbhidyate 
 abhedakatva ca yathā devadatto gauro lohitaḥ kṛṣṇo vā vṛddho veti svāmabhikhyā na jahāti eva ca śāstra ubhayagrahaṇe prāpte niyamo'yam  
aya cārthaścaturanaḍuhorāmudātta ityudāttagrahaṇena jñāpitaḥ 
tathā'sthidadhi ityatrodātta ityanena
luṅlaṅ ityatrodāttagrahaṇena ca 
yadi bhedakāḥ syurguṇāstadodāttaguṇayukta evākāra uccārayitavya ityudāttagrahaṇamanarthaka syāt 
ato jñāpakam   
iti yuvapādaḥ   
aupadeśikaprāyogikayoraupadeśikasyaiva grahaṇam   
upadeśe bhava aupadeśikaḥ prayoge bhavaḥ prāyogikaḥ adhyātmāditvāṭṭhañ 
tayormadhye aupadeśikasyaiva grahaṇam 
tadyathā taraptamapaugha iti pratyayasyaiva tarapo ghasañjñā 
brāhmaṇitareti 
na tu taratareppratyaye kṛte yaḥ prayogastasya nadītara iti 
yadi tu syād gharūpa iti hrasvaḥ syāt 
jñāpaka cātra śvīdito niṣṭhāyām iti śvigrahaṇam 
 yadi prāyogikasyāpi grahaṇamabhaviṣyat tadā samprasāraṇe kṛte śūnaḥ śūnavānityatrogantatvādeva śyukaḥ kiti itīṭpratiṣedhaḥ siddha iti śvigrahaṇa  
na kuryāt  
etaccāyuktam 
ekāca upadeśe ityata upadeśagrahaṇānuvṛtteḥ śyukaḥ kiti ityanenopadeśa ugantātpratiṣedhaḥ 
śūna ityatra tu nopadeśa ugantatvamapi tu prayoge 
tathā ca śvīdito niṣṭhāyām ityatra rakṣitaḥ 
upadeśagrahaṇānuvṛtteḥ śyukaḥ kiti iti pratiṣedho na prāpnotīti śvigrahaṇamiti 
ucyate 
jñāpakavādino'yamabhiprāyaḥ śyukaḥ kiti ityatropadeśādhikāro na svīkriyate 
an caiva tīrṇamityādāviṭpratiṣedhābhāvaḥ prāpnoti 
śvīdito niṣṭhāyām ityatra śvigrahaṇenaupadeśikogantādiṭpratiṣedhāt 
nanu śvigrahaṇamiṭpratiṣedhārthamayuktam 
uḍḍīna ityetadudo dittvādeveḍāgamābhāvasya siddhatvāt 
ki ca paribhāṣāyāḥ prayojana nāsti 
taraptamapau ityatra tamapā sāhacaryāllakṣaṇaparibhāṣayā ca pratyayasyaiva tarapo grahaṇāt 
tathopadeśāvasthāyā pakārasyetsañjñālope kṛte guṇaparavelāyā pakārābhāvāttarapsamudāyo nāstīti katha nadītara ityatra ghasañjñāśañkā 
ki ca yadīya paribhāṣā'sti tadā 
kimupadeśe'janunāsika ityādāvupadeśagrahaṇena 
ucyate 
ādyastāvanna bhavati prapañcārthatvāt 
dvitīyo'pi na 
upāyasyānupāyatopālambho na rūpāya gauravamiti vacanāt 
tṛtīyo'pi na 
sarvatraivetsajñāyā lope kṛte bhūtapūrvagatyā pakāramāśritya sajñāvidhānāt 
caturtho'pi na 
paribhāsāśrayāpekṣayā prakriyālāghavārthatvāt   
sarvavidhibhya iḍvidhirbalavān   
tena śvayitvetyatra samprasāraṇāt pūrvamiḍāgama eva bhavati 
tathā na tkvā seṭ ityakittvātsamprasāraṇābhāvaḥ 
jñāpaka cātra sani grahaguhośca ityatroko'nukarṣaṇārtha cakārakaraṇam 
anyathā rurūṣatīttyatreko jhal iti sanaḥ kittve śyukaḥ kiti ityeveṭpratiṣedhaḥ siddha iti kimuko'nukarṣaṇārthena cakāreṇa
paśyati tvācāryo'nyatreḍvidhirbalavāniti prathamatastasminkṛte jhalāditvābhāvātkittva nāstītyuko'nukarṣaṇa karoti   
lugvikaraṇālugvikaraṇayoralugvikaraṇasyaiva grahaṇam   
tena gopoṣṭak ityalumvikaraṇasyaiva pibatergrahaṇam 
na tu lugvikaraṇasya pāteḥ 
satsūddhiṣādi sūtre vidagrahaṇa eṣā na pravarttate 
yujavida ityakārāntasyopādānādgaṇe ye'kārāntā vidadhātavo vida jñāne vida vicāraṇe vida sattāyāmiti te sarve gṛhyante 
tasyāścāstitve svaratisūtisūyati ityatra sūtimūyatyorvikaraṇanirddeśo jñāpakaḥ 
tatra hyaktam 
sūṅiti sāmānyanirddeśo'tu tata evādādikadaivādikayorgrahaṇa bhaviṣyati 
na sū preraṇe ityasya 
tatki vikaraṇanirddeśena
eva tarhi jñāpayatyastīya paribhāṣā sūṅgrahaṇe lumvikaraṇaparibhāṣayā daivādikasyaiva grahaṇa syāt nādādikasya
vikaraṇenobhayornnirddeśaḥ kriyamāṇo'syā jñāpako bhavati 
nanu ca sūtiriti śtipā nirddeśaḥ kva cit śtipi pitkārya na bhavatīti jñāpanārthaḥ 
tena śtipo'pittvān ṅittvena sūti ityatra kṅiti ca iti guṇapratiṣedhaḥ sidhyati 
tathā manyakarmaṇyanādare vibhāṣā ityatra manutergrahaṇa mābhūdityatra manuteriti gaṇābhāvena sidhyati 
ucyate 
sūtisūyatīti vikaraṇanirddeśaḥ pittvābhāva bodhayanneva paribhāṣāstitva jñāpayati
 anyathā yadi vikaraṇanirddeśasya pittvābhāvajñāpanameva kevala prayojana syāttadā sūtīti nirddeśa kṛtvā sūṅgrahaṇameva kṛta syāt svaratisūtisūṅdhūṅūdito  
veti  
atrāpi sūtisūṅorupādāna pittvābhāvajñāpanārtha bhaviṣyati 
atra tu lugvikaraṇālumviraṇayorlumvikaraṇasyaiva grahaṇamiti viparīto'rtho na jñāpyate 
na hyaniṣṭārthā śāstre prakḷptiryujyata itivacanāt 
vettervibhāṣā ityatra vetteriti śtipā nirddeśācca 
tasya hyetatprayojanam 
lumvikaraṇaparibhāṣayā raudhādikasya vida vicāraṇe ityasya grahaṇa mābhūditi 
 yadi ca lumvikaraṇālumvikaraṇayorlumvikaraṇasyaiva grahaṇamiti syāttadā vida ityapi kṛte vida jñāna ityasyaiva grahaṇa bhaviṣyati ki śtipā  
nirddeśena  
na ca yaṅlugnivṛttyarthamiti vācyam 
śīṅo ruṭ ityatra śīṅo'yaṅluggrahaṇena sāhacaryācca yaṅluggrahaṇābhāvasiddheḥ   
vartsyatpravṛttyeha kāryāṇi kriyante   
bhaviṣyantī pravṛttimāśritya kāryāṇi kriyanta ityarthaḥ 
yathā śadeḥ śita ityanena bhāvinā śittvena śīyata ityatrātmanepadam 
tathā ninyaturninyurityatra bhaviṣyadanekāctvena dvirvacanāt prāgevairanekāco'sayogapūrvasya iti yaṇādeśaḥ anyatheyaṅ syāt 
jñāpaka cātra vasvekājādghasām ityekājgrahaṇam
taddhi liṭi dvirvacanasyāvaśyakatvānna kaścidekājastīti bhaviṣyadabhyāsalopapravṛtteruttarakāla bhāvī ya ekāctadartha kṛtam 
tadarthatā ca tadā syādyadi vartsyatpravṛttyeha kāryāṇi syuḥ 
nanu dvirvacanātprāgyo dhāturekāc tadarthamekājgrahaṇa syāt 
tatkathamuktārthasya jñāpakam 
ucyate 
dvirvacanātprāk sarve dhātava ekāca evetyekājgrahaṇamanarthaka syāt 
naitat 
svādau cirijirī paṭhyete pratyayāntāśca ye'nekāco dhātavastannivṛttyarthatvāt 
asadetat 
kāsyanekāca iti vaktavyamityanekājbhyo nityamāmvidhānāt 
jāgarttevyāvṛttyartha tarhi syāt 
jāgarttertdyuṣavidajāgṛtyo'nyatarasyām iti vikalpenāmvidhānāt 
ucyate 
yadyetadarthamekājgrahaṇa syāttadaikājgrahaṇamapanīya na jāgurityeva brūyāt 
aya cārthaḥ
jāgarttervasoriṇna bhavati 
natūrṇotirapi vyāvṛtyo'sti 
naitat 
vācya urṇorṇuvadbhāva iti ṇuvadbhāvātideśenorṇoterekāckāryeṇa bhāvyameveti jñāpakameva 
dvirvacane kṛte yadaikāctva bhavati tadaiva tadarthatvāt 
yukta caitat 
anyathā ghasigrahaṇamanarthaka syāt 
ghasibhasorhali ca iti lopātprāk paratvādekāca ityanenaivātreḍāgamena bhavitavyam 
tatra hi kṛte gamahanajanakhanaghasām ityupadhālopasya dvirvacane'ci iti sthānivadbhāvātsiddhañjakṣivāniti 
ucyate 
jñāpakavādino'yamabhiprāyaḥ 
ekājgrahaṇāttāvatkṛtadvirvacanānāmiṭā bhavitavyam 
sa ceṭ dvirvacanātprāg yadi kriyate tadā paratvanyāyo na laṅghito bhavati 
tathā ca vasvekājāt iti sūtre rakṣitaḥ
dvirvacanotpatteḥ prāgeva paratvādiḍāgama iti 
ghasigrahaṇa tu pratyākhyāyata eveti 
atha vā'na upadhālopino'nyatarasyām iti bhaviṣyadupadhālopino ṅībvīdhāna jñāpakam 
anyathā sati ṅīpyupadhālopaḥ satyupadhālope ca ṅībityasaṅgatiḥ syāt 
atha vartsyatpravṛcyeti katham 
yāvatā sayoge guru iti gurusajñābādhanālladhūpadhaguṇo na prāpnoti 
ucyate 
vihitaviśeṣaṇasvīkāre laghūpadhādvihita yatsārvadhātukamārddhadhātuka vā tasmin guṇa ityadoṣaḥ 
na caiva kuṇḍitetyatra guṇaprasaṅgaḥ 
dhātugrahaṇena dhātūpadeśa eva numpravṛtteḥ 
vihitaviśeṣaṇena tarhi ruṇaddhityatrāpi guṇaḥ syāt 
eva tarhi nābhyastasyāci piti sārvadhātuka ityatrājgrahaṇātsayoge guṇo bhaviṣyati 
anyathā hi nenektītyatra guṇabhāvārthamacītyarthaka syāt 
naivam 
anenegityatra guṇapratiṣedhābhāvārthatvādajgrahaṇasya 
eva tarhi prakṛtipratyayayorhalorāntarye gurusajñā na bhavati 
trasigṛdhidhṛṣikṣipeḥ knuḥ iti knoḥ kitkaraṇāt 
halantācca iti laghūpadhaguṇapratiṣedhārthāt kittvācca 
taduktam 
knusanoryatkṛta kittva jñāpaka syāllaghorguṇa iti 
yadyeva dṛḍhaḥ sthūlabalayoḥ ityatra tarhi nyāse yadukta tadasagatam 
tatra hyuktam 
kimartha hakāralopo nipātyate 
yāvatā ho ḍhaḥ iti ḍhatve kṛte ḍho ḍhe lopa ityeva siddha dṛḍha iti 
satya siddhyati 
draḍhīyānityatra tu rephādeśo na siddhyati 
ra ṛto halāderlaghoḥ iti karttavye ḍhalopasyāsiddhatvād gurusajñayā laghusajñābādhanāt 
ucyate 
eva manyate guṇa eva karttavye gurusajñā na pravarttate 
ato raphādeśe karttavye syādeva gurusajñā 
tathā ca kḷptaśikha ityatra guroranṛto'nantyasyāpyekaikasya prācām iti gurutvāt pluto bhavatyeva 
etaccāyuktam 
ato halāderlaghīḥ ityatra pratyudāhṛtamiṭītyevāpākṣīditi 
tasya dvyaṅgavaikalyāt 
tathāhi 
yathā sijiḍādirnna bhavati tathā laghurakāro'pi
sayogagurutvena laghutvasya bādhanāt 
tarhyevammanyate draḍhīyānityatra jñāpakasiddha na sarvatreti laghusajñayā na bhavitavyam 
tathā kḷptaśikha ityatrāpi gurusajñaiva bhavati 
 atha vā yatra pratyaye prakṛtihalā sayogastasminneva pratyaye yadi laghusajñākāryaprāptistadaiva knusanoḥ kittvāj jñāpakād gurusajñā na  
bhavati jñāpakasya tulyatvāt  
tathāhi bhettetyādau tṛci guṇaprāptiḥ 
apākṣīdityatrāpi sici vṛddhiprāptiḥ parasmaipadagrahaṇa tu sico viśeṣaṇam 
draḍhayati draḍīyānityatra tu ṇāvīyasuni ca rephādeśo na tu kte 
kḷptaśikha ityatrāpi na ktāśrayaḥ pluto'pi tu prakṛtipratyayasayogāśrayaḥ
ato'tra gurusajñaiveti 
anyastvāha 
knoḥ kittvādgurutvena laghutva na bādhyate 
api tūbhayasajñāsamāveśaḥ kriyate 
tena bhettetyādau satyapi gurutve laghvāśrayo bhavatyeva guṇaḥ kḷptaśikha ityatrāpi gurusajñāśrayaḥ plutaḥ 
apākṣīdityatrāpi laghvāśrayā vṛddhiḥ syāt 
 ra ṛto halāderlaghoḥ ityanena tu kumbhīdhānyanyāyena laghusajñakasyaiva ṛkārasya rephādeśa ityāśaṅkānirāsārtha hakāralopanipātana nyāsakṛtoktam 
aya bhāvaḥ 
anyathā ḍhalopasyāsiddhatvādgurusajñako'yamṛkāro na ta laghusajñaka eveti rephādeśo na syāt   
antaraṅgānapi vidhīn bahiraṅgo lug bādhate   
antaraṅgānapi numādīn bādhitvā bahiraṅgo lugeva pravarttate 
tena gomān priyo'sya gomatpriyaḥ 
gomānivācarati gomatyate ityatra supo luki kṛte sarvanāmasthānābhāvānnumna pravarttate 
pratyayalakṣaṇa na nāsti 
na lumatāṅgasya iti niṣedhāt 
iya paribhāṣā pratyayottarapadayośca ityatra bhāṣya kāreṇa jñāpitā 
tatra hyuktam 
 tavāya tvadīyo mamāya madīya ityādau chapratyaye tava putrastvatputrī mama putrī matputra ityādau cottarapade vibhaktyāśrayatvāttvamāvekavacana  
ityanenaiva tvamau bhaviṣyataḥ  
samāsottarakālabhāvī lug bahiraṅgaḥ sa paścād bhaviṣyati 
na ca nimittāpāyaparibhāṣayā tvamāvapi nivartteta 
yato bahiraṅgasya luko'siddhatvādvidyata eva nimitta
siddhau pūrveṇa tvamāviti ki pratyayottarapadayośca ityanena tadetkṛta jñāpayati 
astīya paribhāseti 
tena tvamau bādhitvā vibhaktiluki kṛte vibhaktyābhāvātpūrveṇa tvamau na prāpnuta iti vacanamarthavadbhavati 
 nanu tvattaro mattara iti tarapi tvamau yathā syātāmiti pratyayagrahaṇa syāt prātipadikamātrādeva tarabādayaḥ svārthikā vidhīyante na tu subantāt  
samarthādhikāranivṛtteḥ  
tathā ca samarthānā prathamāddhā ityatra vyākhyāta svārthikapratyayāvadhiścāyamadhikāra iti 
uttarapadagrahaṇamapi karttavyam 
tava putrastvatputrastubhya hita tvaddhitamityatra tavamamau ṅasi tubhyamahyau ṅayi iti bādhitvā tvamau yathā syātām 
 anyathā yathā tava tubhyamityatra tavabubhyau bhavatastathātrāpi syātām pratyayottarapadayośca iti sūtre tu kṛte tayorapavādau tvamāveva kriyete  
iti katha jñāpakam  
ucyate 
ādyastāvadadoṣaḥ 
yataḥ svārthikā api nivṛtte'pi samarthādhikāre'ntaraṅgatvāt supi kṛte suvantādeva bhavantīti vyavasthitam 
tathā ca kutsita ityatra sūtre bhāṣyam 
 svārthamabhidhāya śabdo nirapekṣo dravyamāha tatsamaveta samavetasya ca liṅga sakhyā vibhaktiścābhidhāya tataḥ priyakutsanādiṣu varttate'sau  
vibhaktyanta iti  
tasmātsubantasyaiva priyakutsanādayo'rthā viśeṣamiti subantādeva tarabādaya iti yuktamukta pratyayagrahaṇa jñāpakamiti 
 ye tu manyante tarabādiprakṛtestarabādividhau ṅyāpprātipadikasyaiva svabhāvataḥ puruṣādyathāvṛttitvamityanavakāśatvāt supa bādhitvā prātipadikādeva  
tarabādibhirbhavitavyamiti tamate naiva tarabādividhau ṅyāpprātipadikādityanuvarttate iti vṛttāvuktam  
tathā svādiṣvasarvanāmasthāna ityatra rājataro rājatama ityudāhṛtam 
tanmate pratyayagrahaṇa na jñāpakamityāhuḥ 
uttarapadagrahaṇameva jñāpakam 
dvitīyo'pyadoṣaḥ 
 tathāhi yadi tavatubhyādeśa bādhitvā pratyayottarapadayoścetyanena bhavitavya tadotsargasamānatvādapavādānām maparyantasyaiva tau bhaviṣyato  
na sarvasyeti ki maparyantasyetyanukarṣaṇārthena cakāreṇeti  
tavatubhyādeśabādhanayā bhavitavyam 
tadā cakāreṇa maparyantasyetyanukarṣaṇa yatkṛta tadanarthaka syāt 
tasyaitatprayojana sarvādeśārthatve tu sarvādeśaḥ syāt

yathā brāhmaṇebhyo dadhi dīyatā takra kauṇḍinyāyeti

tanna

jñāpaka cātra pravāhaṇasya ḍhe ityanena pravāhaṇasyāpatya prāvāhaṇeya iti śubhrāditvāḍ ḍhaki uttarapadavṛddhividhānam

 yadyeva katha tatra tarhi nyāsakṛtā vyākhyāta jāteśca iti puvadbhāvapratiṣedhe siddhe vṛddhinimittasya iti puvadbhāvapratiṣedhārtha pravāhaṇasya

jñāpaka cātra na yāsayoḥ itīttvapratiṣedhārtha vacanam

tyadādyatve kṛte garbhavaṭṭāpo'bhāvāt yakā saketi na syāt 
eva ca pratyayasthāt itīttvaprāpterabhāvānna yāsayoḥ ityanarthaka syāt

śrīpuruṣottamadevena tu vyākhyātam 
jñāpaka ca na yāsayorittvapratiṣedhavacanam

tatki pratiṣedheneti   
vidhau paribhāṣopatiṣṭhate nānuvāde

pradhānāpradhānanyāyalabdho'yamarthaḥ 
jñāpaka cātrodīcāmātaḥ

avyāpikā ceya sakhyāvyayādeḥ ityatrādigrahaṇāt 
anyathā sakhyāvyayābhyāmityevocyeta 
aya cārthaḥ

pañcaghaṭoghnīti

ucyate 
pratyāsattyodhaḥśabda eva sakhyāvyayayorviśeṣyo na bahuvrīhiḥ
tathāhi sakhyāvyayābhyāmityatrodhaśśabda eva pratyāsanno netaraḥ 
nanvevamapi tripade bahuvrīhau na prāpnoti tadartha yatna āstheyaḥ   
prakṛtigrahaṇe ṇyadhikasyāpi grahaṇa bhavati   
tena heracaṅi iti hinoterṇyantādapi sani kṛte 
jighāyiṣatīti kutva bhavati 
 abhiṣāvayati pariṣāvayatītyatra tu sunotimeva prati kriyāyogo na tu sāvayati pratītyupasargātsunoti iti ṣatvamiti vṛttavukta na tvanayā paribhāṣayeti 
jñāpaka cātra heracaṅi iti pratiṣedhaḥ 
yadi prakṛtigrahaṇe ṇyadhikasya grahaṇa na syāt 
tadā kevalasya hinoteraṅgasyābhysanimittapratyaye kutvamucyamāna kaḥ prasaṅgo ṇyadhike syāt 
yadarthamacaṅīti pratiṣedhaḥ kriyata iti 
avyāpikā ceyam 
na bhādi sūtre ṇyantānā bhādīnāmupasakhyānamiti vacanāt 
tenārha ityatra ṇyantasyārhatergrahaṇa na bhavatīti rakṣitenoktam   
aṅgavṛtte punaraṅgavṛttāvavidhirnniṣṭhitasya   
aṅgakāryasya vṛttiḥ pravṛttiraṅgavṛttistato hetornniṣṭhitasya prayogārhasyāṅgasya punaraṅgakāryapravṛttāvavidhiravidhāna bhavati

tena pibatītyatra pibādeśe kṛte laghūpadhaguṇo na bhavat

tathāhi pūrvatroktam

pūrvatrāsiddhīye na sthānivat   
tena papaktiryā yaṣṭirityatra pūrvatrāsiddhādhikārīye kutve ṣatve ca karttavye'to lopasyāsthānivattvājjhalādau kutva ṣatva ca siddhyati

naitat 
ato lopa ityakāralope kṛte yaṅo'ci ca iti yakāramātrameva lupyate 
kuta etat 
na padāntādi sūtre yāyāvara ityatra sthānivadbhāvapratiṣedhārthādvaregrahaṇāt 
samudāyalope hi sthānivattvaprāptyabhāvādvare sthānivattvapratiṣedho'narthaḥ syāt 
yadyeva na dhātulopa ārddhadhātuka ityanarthakam 
yaṅo'kārasya sthānivattvena loluvaḥ popuva ityādeḥ siddhatvāt 
eva tarhi na dhātulopa sūtrasāmarthyādaci pratyaye lopaḥ samudāyasyaiva kriyata iti jñāpyate 
anyatra tu pratyeka tena sanīsrasa ityādi siddhyat 
tathā sanīsrasako danīdhvasaka iti 
yadyeva niṣṭhā śīṅ ityatra yannyāsakṛtīkta śīṅo ṅitkaraṇasya prayojana yaṅluki kittvapratiṣedho mā bhūccheśyitaḥ śeśyitavāniti 
tadasagatam 
niṣṭhāyāḥ satyapyakittve yaṅo'kārasya sthānivattvena guṇāprasaṅgāt 
eva tarhyārddhadhātuka ityasya viṣayasaptamītvamāśritya tatra vyākhyātam 
yadi cāci lopaḥ samastasyaivānyatra tu niyamo nāṣtīti vākyārthaḥ 
tena pratyeka samudāyasyāpi lopaḥ 
ato yadā samudāyalopastadhā śeśyita ityatrākittvapratiṣedhārtha ṅitkaraṇamiti nyāsakārasyābhiprāyaḥ 
iya ca paribhāṣā nāglopiśāsvṛditām ityatra bhāṣye jñāpitā 
 tatra hyuktamacakathadityādāvajādeśasya sthānivattvādeva ṇau hrasvo na bhaviṣyati kimaglopinā neti pratiṣedhena tata ukta yatra sthānivadbhāvo  
nāsti tadarthamatyararājaditi na hyatra ṭilopo'jādeśaḥ ki tarhi halacorādeśa iti tataḥ punarukta na tarhyaglopinā neti pratiṣedho'tra prāptoti  
na hyatrāgeva lupyate ki tarhyanyo'pi atha yo'trāglupyate tadāśrayo niṣedhaḥ eva tarhi yo'j lupyate tadāśrayaḥ sthānivadbhāvo'pi bhaviṣyatītyutkvopasahṛtam 
 eva tarhi yadaglopinā neti pratiṣedha śāsti tato jñāpayatyācārya iti ārabhyottaratra sthānivadbhāvo na bhavatīti tena pūrvatrāsiddhīye na  
sthānivaditi vaktavyanna bhavatīti

sthavīyāniti

na padāntādi sūtre dvirvacanagrahaṇāt

paragrahaṇa yuktam

satyam 
yatra parāśrito vidhiryathā vṛkṣādityatra supaḥ paragrahaṇāt suptvātpadatva kuṭādītyatra na paragrahaṇāśrita jaśtvam 
na hi jaśtvamākāramapekṣate

yadyapi jaśtvamākāramapekṣate 
ucyate 
yadyapi jaśtvasyākāro nimitta na bhavati tathāpi paragrahaṇe sati kuḍiti ṭakārānta pada bhavatīti jaśtvasya paragrahaṇameva nimittam 
nanu satyapi paragrahaṇe jaśtvannāsti ṭakārasyāpadāntatvāt 
akārānta hi pada tataḥ subvidhiḥ 
ucyate 
paragrahaṇe kṛte ekadeśavikāradvāreṇa ṭakārānta padam 
naitat 
antādivattva ekadeśavikārābhāvāt
anyathā hi vṛkṣamityatrāpyekādeśasya pūrvagrahaṇemakārasyakadeśavikāradvāreṇa suptve supi ca iti dīrghaḥ syādeva 
eva cobhayata āśraye nāntādivaditi vyartha syāt 
ucyate 
yatra vidhirubhayamāśrayati ekamantādivattvenāparamekadeśavikāradvāreṇa tatraikadeśavikārasvīkāro yathā vṛkṣamiti

nanu tathāpyatra padāntavidhau jaśtve karttavye padāntavidhi prati na sthānivaditisthānivattvapratiṣedhājjaśtvena bhavitavyameva

sati sthānivattvaniṣedhe padāntatva sati ca padāntatve sthānivattvaniṣedha itītaretarāśrayatvam 
evamapi jhalā jaśo'nta iti jaśtvamastyeva na cāsti sthānivattva jaśtvavidhi prati na sthānivaditi tanniṣedhāt

etacca ṭhājādāvṛddhva dvitīyādaca ityatra ṣāḍikaprastāve rakṣitenoktam   
upajātanimitto'pyutsarga upajaniṣyamāṇanimittenāpavādena bādhyate 
parihṛtyāpavādaviṣayamutsargo'bhiniviśate   
tena dadhatītyatropajātanimitto'pyantaraṅo jho'nta ityantādeśa upajaniṣyamāṇanimittenādabhyastāt ityadādeśena bādhyate 
jñāpaka cātra śīṅaḥ sārvadhātuke guṇa ityatraikāre vidhātavye guṇagrahaṇam 
tasyaitatprayojana guṇaśrutyekaparibhāṣopasthānādika eva sthāne guṇo yathā syāditi 
 anyathā śete ityatra ṅakārasyetsajñā bādhitvaikāraḥ syāt tatra yadyantaraṅgastadā guṇagrahaṇamanarthaka ṅakāre lupte'nyathaivekārasyaikārādeśaprasaṅgāt 
ata eva śīṅaḥ sārvadhātuke guṇa ityapanīya sārvadhātukamapidaśīṅa iti na kṛtam 
na caivamadhiśayyete ityatra ṅittvapratiṣedhādāto ṅita itīyādeśo na syāditi vācyam 
yato'śīṅa iti pañcamīnirddeśācchīṅga uttarasya pratiṣedhena bhavitavyam 
na cāśīṅga iti paryudāsācca sādṛśyenājantatvāccāco ṅittvena bhavitavyam 
paryudāsasyāgrahaṇāt 
atha vā na śīṅa iti pṛthageva kriyāmiti 
tasmātparibhāṣādvayasya jñāpakamiti 
upajātanimitto'pyutsarga upajaniṣyamāṇanimittenāpavādena bādhyata ityatrārthe ṛcchatṝtāmityatra ṛkārapraśleṣo rakṣitena jñāpaka uktaḥ 
yadyeṣā na syāt ṛ atusiti sthite iko re yaṇādeśe kṛte sthānivadbhāvād dvirvacane kṛte'ta ādeḥ iti dīghatvena siddhamāraturāruriti 
asyā tu satyā yaṇādeśo nāsti 
dvirvacane kṛte upajaniṣyamāṇanimittena sarvaṇadīrghatvena bādhitatvāt 
savarṇadīrghatve ca kṛte prakṛtigrahaṇena grahaṇādraturiti syāt 
abhyāsagrahaṇapakṣe rephalopo āto lopa iṭi ca ityākāralope cāturiti syāt 
ṛgatāvityasya tu grahaṇe guṇenāraturāruriti siddhyati 
etacca vārṇādāṅga balīya ityasyāvyāśrayatvapakṣāśrayaṇāducyate 
yadi tu vyāśraye vārṇādāṅga balīya iti syāt tadā savarṇadīrghatvambādhitvoradattvādika syāt 
ata evośca ityatra rakṣitenoktam 
atha vā ṛgrahaṇa tatra pratyākhyāta yata iti   
ṇau kṛta sthānivat   
ṇau parato yad vṛddhyādika kṛta tad dvirvacane karttavye sthānivatsyāt 
tena śuśāvayiṣati juhāvayiṣatītyatrābhyāsasyovarṇāntatva siddha bhavati 
aśūśavadityatra tu vakārasya saprasāraṇa ṇau kṛtamapi dvirvacane na sthānivadbhavati 
ajādeśasyaiva ṇau kṛtasya dvirvacane sthānivadityubhyupagamāt 
etacca dvirvacane'ci ityatra bhāṣya uktam 
jñāpaka cātra oḥ puyaṇjyapara ityatrābhyāsaviśeṣaṇamoriti padam 
tena hi pavarge yaṇi jakāre cā'cpare'bhyāsasyetva vidhīyate bibhāvayiṣatītyādiṣu
yadi ca ṇau kṛta vṛddhyāvādeśādikārya sthānivanna syātkathamabhyāsasyokāretva vidhīyate

etattu na samyak 
stautiṇyoreva ṣaṇyabhyāsāt ityatra siṣedhayiṣatītyudāharaṇa ekārapare'nayā sthānivattva kṛtvā dvirvacanasya pratipāditatvāt 
 tathaujaḍhadityatrānayā sthānivattvena dvirvacanamuktamayukta syāt tathā lopaḥ pivaterīccābhyāsasya ityatrāpīpyadityatra ṇau kṛta sthānivadbhavatīti  
vṛttikṛdvacana vyāhata syāt  
tasmātsāmānyena paribhāṣā 
jñāpakasiddha na sarvatretyacikīrttadityatra vyavasthā 
avaśya caitat 
anyathā'dhijigāpayiṣatītyatra kā gatiḥ 
anyastvāha 
aṅgaikadeśājādeśo ṇau kṛta sthānivaditi 
tenādhijigāpayiṣatītyatra sthānivattva na 
tacca ṇau ca saścaṅoḥ ityatra rakṣitena vyākhyātam 
evamapyacikorttadityatra doṣa eva   
abhyāsavikāreṣvapavādā notsargānvidhīnvbādhante   
abhyāsakikāreṣvapavādatvāntaraṅgatvaparatvādibhirbādhakā bādhyān vidhīnna bādhante 
tena mīmāsata ityatra mānvadhādinā dīrgheṇa sanyataḥ itīttva na bādhyate 
tathā'cikṣaṇadityatra sāvakāśa sanyata itīttvamacīkaradityādau dīgho laghoḥ ityanena na bādhyate 
jñāpaka cātra dīrgho'kita ityatrākiṅgrahaṇam 
taddhi grayamyata ityādau dīrgho mā bhūdityevamartha kriyate 
 yadi cābhyāsavikāreṣvapi bādhyabādhakabhāvaḥ syāttadā nugāgame kṛte'najantatvādeva dīrgho na bhaviṣyati kimakidgrahaṇena tat kṛtamuktārthasya  
jñāpakamiti    
iti paribhāṣāvṛttau ṇaupādaḥ   
iti saptamo'dhyāhaḥ   
pūrvatrāsiddhīyamadvirvacane   
dvirvacane karttavye pūrvatrāsiddham iti na pravarttate 
tena drogdhādogdhā droḍhādroḍhetyatra druherjhali ghatvaḍhatvayoḥ kṛtayoḥ sarvasya dve iti dvirvacana bhavati 
anyathā pūrvatrāsiddham ityasiddhatvād droh tetyasya dvirvacana syāt 
tato vā druhamuheti ghatvavikalpaḥ 
tatraitanna labhyate yadā prakṛterghatva tadā dviruktasyāpīti 
tataśca ḍhatvamapi kadā citsyāt 
eva ca drogdhādroḍhetyaniṣṭa syāt 
nanvasiddhapāda paṭhitvā sarvasya dvepādaḥ paṭhyatā tato'siddhatva na bhaviṣyati 
naitat 
eva hi paṭhatipaṭhatitarāmityatra prakarṣapratyayātparatvena dvirvacana na syāt 
pūvatrāsiddhīye nāsti paratvamabhāvāduttarasyetivacanādgrāmastvekṣata ityatra ca tvāmau dvitīyāyā ityasyāsiddhatvāḍhādguṇo na syāt 
jñāpaka cātra sarvasya dve ityatra sarvasyeti vacanam 
taddhi matvarthīyākārapratyayāntam 
tenāyamarthaḥ 
sarvakāryayuktasya dvirvacana sarvakārya kṛtvā dvirvacana bhavatītyarthaḥ 
eva ca tadupapadyate yadyasiddhatvanna bhavatīti jñāpakam 
nanu sarvasyeti vacana sarvasya dvirvacanārtham 
anyathā parervarjana iti dvirvacanamantyasya syāt 
etaccāyuktam 
dve vidhīyeye tayoścānekāltvātsarvādeśaḥ siddha eva 
satyam 
halenteṣu paryādiṣvikārasyālontyasya syāt 
nanu dvāvikārau syātām 
tataścānekāltvādyukta sarvādeśatvam 
na ca dvāvikārau kṛtaikādeśāvādeśatva pratipadyete ityekāltvādādeśo'ntyasya syāt 
na hyapravṛttayostayorekādeśaśāstrapravṛttirasti pravṛttikāle cānekakāltvātsarvādeśatvamiti nāstyantyasya vidhiḥ 
syādetat 
 aco'rddhamātre tarhi prāpnutaḥ pariśabdasyārddhamātre dve vidhīyamāne'lgrahaṇena cārddhamātrāyā agrahaṇādanekāltvābhe'sati sarvasyeti vacane'ntyasya  
prāpnuta iti  
etaccātīvāsamyak 
aśliṣṭasyārddhamātrādvayasyoccāraṇāyogyatvādaśakya ādeśaḥ karttum 
anyastvāha 
sarvasya dve ityatra sūtre kātyāyanavākyamida paribhāṣārūpeṇa paṭhyate 
pūrvatrāsiddhīyamadvirvacana iti 
anityā ceyam 
ubhau sābhyāsasya iti vacanāt 
tena praṇināyeti siddhyati   
iti paribhāṣāvṛttau sarvasya dvepādaḥ   
anityamāgamaśāsanam   
tena śāka pacānasyetyāne mugna bhavati 
sāgara tarttumicchatītyatreḍ na bhavati 
jñāpaka cātrāni loṭ ityatrānītyāgamasahitasya nergrahaṇa nitye hyāgamaśāsana āṭa upādānamakṛtvā niloṭ ityeva kuryāt 
tathā yuvoranākau ityatra nyāse ghorlopo leṭi vā iti vāgrahaṇena jñāpitā 
ke cittu stoḥ ścunā ścuḥ ityakṛtanumāgamanirddeśa jñāpakamāhuḥ 
nanvāgamaśāsanamiti katham 
yāvatā'mi pūrva ityekādeśasya paragrahaṇena grahaṇādantarvarttinī vibhaktimāśritya padatvānnalopena bhavitavyam 
ucyate 
acaḥ parasmin iti sthānivattvānna bhaviṣyati 
na cātra padāntavidhi prati na sthānivadityasti
itaretarāśrayatvāt 
sati sthānivattvapratiṣedhe padāntatva sati ca padāntatve sthānivattvapratiṣedha iti 
nanvevamapi pūrvatrāsiddhīye na sthānivaditi sthānivattva na prāpnoti 
ucyate 
uttarapadatve cāpadādividhāvityuttarasya padatve karttavye pratyayalakṣaṇapratiṣedhācchāsanasya padatva nāstīti kuto nalopaḥ 
 yadeva ṣātpadāntāt ityatra vṛttau yadvākhyāta pade'ntaḥ padānta iti saptamīsamāso'ya teneha na bhavati susarpiṣkeṇa suyajuṣkeṇeti tadasaṅgatam 
tathāhi 
yathā susarpiṣkeṇetyatra kapratyaye'pade parataḥ ṣakārāntantathaivāpadāntatva ṣantasya 
ucyate 
padādividhiśabdena sātpadādyoḥ ityārabhya ye vidyayaste gṛhyante 
tenāpadādividhāvitivacanāduttarasya padatva bhavatyeva 
atra cārthe ṣātpadāntādityatra padāntagrahaṇa jñāpakam 
tathā ca padavyavāye'pi ityatra maitreyaḥ 
atra ca jñāpakam 
ṣātpadāntādityatra pade'ntaḥ padānta ityevamarthasya padāntagrahaṇasyopādānam 
na hi tadanyathā sambhavatīti 
atrocyate 
nanu yadyevamartha padāntagrahaṇa tadā tadakṛtvā ṣātsupītyeva kriyatām 
ṣātpada iti vā 
aya cārthaḥ subante parato yaḥ ṣakāraḥ pade parata iti etadevamuktārthasya jñāpaka bhaviṣyati 
ki caivavidhajñāpane na prayojanam 
ṣātpadāntāditi karttavye pratyayalakṣaṇa bhavatītyevāstu 
ucyate 
yattāvadukta 
supīti kriyatā pada iti vā 
tanna 
yadi tannirvahati 
tadā ki padāntagrahaṇasyoktārthajñāpakā vyāhanyate 
dvitīyamapi na 
 yata evavidhajñāpane druṇaso vārddhrīṇas ityādāvuttarasya naḥśabdasya padāntatvātpūrvapadātsajñāyāmaga iti ṇatva bhavati carmanāsike ṇatvābhāvaḥ 
anyathā mātṛbhogīṇavaccarmanāsika ityatrāpi ṇatva syāt 
tathā māṣakumbhavāpeneti samāsa uttarasya kumbhaśabdasya padatva bhavati 
tena māṣakumbhavāpenetyatra padavyavāye ṇatvapratiṣedhaḥ siddhyati 
anyathā pratyayalaksaṇābhāvānnimittanimittinoḥ padavyavāyo na syāt 
nanvatrāpi padavyāye'pi itisāmarthyātpratyayalakṣaṇena padatva bhaviṣyati 
ucyate 
yadi sāmarthyādvyavasthā tadoktamprakāre niṣphalo vyāroṣaḥ 
nanu yadi sātpadādyoḥ ityārabhya kārye'padādividhāvitivacanāduttarasya padatva bhavati 
tarhi bhāvakarmaṇoḥ ityādau padāntasya iti karttavye ṇatvapratiṣedhe padatva prāpnoti tataśca padāntasya iti ṇatvapratiṣedhena bhavitavyam
ucyate 
bhāvakarmaṇoḥ iti nirddeśādadoṣaḥ 
nanu ca yadyuttarapadatve cāpadādividhāvityasti 
katha tarhi vimaladyu dinamiti 
yāvatā'trāpyuttarapadatve cāpadādividhāvitivacanāddivaśabdasya padatva nāsti 
ucyate 
tatraiṅaḥ padāntādati ityato'ntagrahaṇamanuvarttate 
tena tadantavidhinā divaśabdāntapadasyottvamiti siddha vimaladyu dinamiti 
kevale tu dyubhyāmityādau vyapadeśivadbhāvāduttvam 
na cāsti vyapadeśivadbhāvo'prādipadikeneti 
dyuprāgapāgudakpratīco yat ityatra nirddeśāt   
nimittāpāye naimittakasyāpyapāyaḥ   
nimittena nirmita naimittikam 
vuñchaṇādau kumudāditvāṭṭhak 
kāraṇāpāye tatkāryamapyapaiti 
tena snātītyatra mūrddhanyābhāve ṇatvamapaiti 
paṭubhārya ityatra ṅībnivṛttau yaṇādeśo nivarttate 
jñāpaka cāsyā udaḥ sthāstambhoḥ pūrvasya ityādau ṣakāranivṛttau ṭhasya thakāroccāraṇam 
laukikaścaiṣa savyabhicāro nyāyaḥ 
loke hi japākusumasannidhau sphaṭike rāgastanivṛttau nivarttate
takṣākābhāve ca prāsādo'styeva 
tenāsyāpatyamiti prakṛterapāye pratyayo na nivarttate 
tathā abhūnnipa ityādau padasaskāre bhūtasāmānye luṅanadyatanāvagamavelāyā na nivarttate 
 etasmin pāde upasargādasamāse'pi ṇopadeśasya ityatra sthāne dvirvacanapakṣe'pi śrutyabhedāttattvādhyavasāyena kāryāṇi pravattanta iti sopadeśānā  
sicprabhṛtīnā pāṭhena sico yaṅi itipratiṣedhārthenetyādiphakkikāyā dūṣaṇa samādhana caikācpāde saprasāraṇabhāṣāyāmuktam    
iti paribhāṣāvṛttau rephapādaḥ   
ityaṣṭamo'dhyāyaḥ
